taddhaitad eva jagdhaṃ yad āśaṃsamānam ārtvijyaṃ kārayata uta vā me dadyād uta vā mā vṛṇīteti taddha tat parāṅ eva yathā jagdhaṃ na haiva tad yajamānam bhunakti | [AB, 3, 46 2]
atha haitad eva gīrṇaṃ yad bibhyad ārtvijyaṃ kārayata uta vā mā na bādhetota vā me na yajñaveśasaṃ kuryād iti taddha tat parāṅ eva yathā gīrṇaṃ na haiva tad yajamānam bhunakti | [AB, 3, 46 3]
atha haitad eva vāntaṃ yad abhiśasyamānam ārtvijyaṃ kārayate yathā ha vā idaṃ vāntān manuṣyā bībhatsanta evam tasmād devās taddha tat parāṅ eva yathā vāntaṃ na haiva tad yajamānam bhunakti | [AB, 3, 46 4]
sa eteṣāṃ trayāṇām āśām neyāt | [AB, 3, 46 5]
taṃ yady eteṣāṃ trayāṇām ekaṃ cid akāmam abhyābhavet tasyāsti vāmadevyasya stotre prāyaścittiḥ | [AB, 3, 46 6]
idaṃ vā idaṃ vāmadevyaṃ yajamānaloko 'mṛtalokaḥ svargo lokaḥ | [AB, 3, 46 7]
tat tribhir akṣarair nyūnaṃ tasya stotra upasṛpya tredhātmānaṃ vigṛhṇīyāt pu ru ṣa iti | [AB, 3, 46 8]
sa eteṣu lokeṣv ātmānaṃ dadhāty asmin yajamānaloke 'sminn amṛtaloke 'smin svarge loke sa sarvāṃ duriṣṭim atyeti | [AB, 3, 46 9]
api yadi samṛddhā iva ṛtvijaḥ syur iti ha smāhātha haitaj japed eveti | [AB, 3, 46 10]
{AB, 3, 47}
chandāṃsi vai devebhyo havyam ūḍhvā śrāntāni jaghanārdhe yajñasya tiṣṭhanti yathāśvo vāśvataro vohivāṃs tiṣṭhed evaṃ tebhya etam maitrāvaruṇam paśupuroﾱāśam anu devikāhavīṃṣi nirvapet | [AB, 3, 47 1]
dhātre puroﾱāśaṃ dvādaśakapālaṃ yo dhātā sa vaṣaṭkāraḥ | [AB, 3, 47 2]
anumatyai caruṃ yānumatiḥ sā gāyatrī | [AB, 3, 47 3]
rākāyai caruṃ yā rākā sā triṣṭup | [AB, 3, 47 4]
sinīvālyai caruṃ yā sinīvālī sā jagatī kuhvai caruṃ yā kuhūḥ sānuṣṭup | [AB, 3, 47 5]
etāni vāva sarvāṇi chandāṃsi gāyatraṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatam ānuṣṭubham anv anyāny etāni hi yajñe pratamām iva kriyante | [AB, 3, 47 6]
etair ha vā asya chandobhir yajataḥ sarvaiś chandobhir iṣṭam bhavāti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 3, 47 7]
tad vai yad idam āhuḥ sudhāyāṃ ha vai vājī suhito dadhātīti chandāṃsi vai tat sudhāyāṃ ha vā enaṃ chandāṃsi dadhati | [AB, 3, 47 8]
ananudhyāyinaṃ lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 3, 47 9]
taddhaika āhur dhātāram eva sarvāsām purastāt purastād ājyena pariyajet tad āsu sarvāsu mithunaṃ dadhātīti | [AB, 3, 47 10]
tad u vā āhur jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyate yatra samānībhyām ṛgbhyāṃ samāne 'han yajatīti | [AB, 3, 47 11]
yadi ha vā api bahvya iva jāyāḥ patir vāva tāsām mithunaṃ tad yad āsāṃ dhātāram purastād yajati tad āsu sarvāsu mithunaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 3, 47 12]
iti nu devikānām | [AB, 3, 47 13]
{AB, 3, 48}
atha devīnām | [AB, 3, 48 1]
sūryāya puroﾱāśam ekakapālaṃ yaḥ sūryaḥ sa dhātā sa u eva vaṣaṭkāraḥ | [AB, 3, 48 2]
dive caruṃ yā dyauḥ sānumatiḥ so eva gāyatry uṣase caruṃ yoṣāḥ sā rākā so eva triṣṭub gave caruṃ yā gauḥ sā sinīvālī so eva jagatī pṛthivyai caruṃ yā pṛthivī sā kuhūḥ so evānuṣṭup | [AB, 3, 48 3]
etāni vāva sarvāṇi chandāṃsi gāyatraṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ jāgatam ānuṣṭubham anv anyāny etāni hi yajñe pratamām iva kriyanta etair ha vā asya chandobhir yajataḥ sarvaiś chandobhir iṣṭam bhavati ya evaṃ veda tad vai yad idam āhuḥ sudhāyāṃ ha vai vājī suhito dadhātīti chandāṃsi vai tat sudhāyāṃ ha vā enaṃ chandāṃsi dadhaty ananudhyāyinaṃ lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ veda taddhaika āhuḥ sūryam eva sarvāsām purastāt purastād ājyena pariyajet tad āsu sarvāsu mithunaṃ dadhātīti tad u vā āhur jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyate yatra samānībhyām ṛgbhyāṃ samāne 'han yajatīti yadi ha vā api bahvya iva jāyāḥ patir vāva tāsām mithunaṃ tad yad āsāṃ sūryam purastād yajati tad āsu sarvāsu mithunaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 3, 48 4]
tā yā imās tā amūr yā amūs tā imā anyatarābhir vāva taṃ kāmam āpnoti ya etāsūbhayīṣu | [AB, 3, 48 5]
tā ubhayīr gataśriyaḥ prajātikāmasya saṃnirvapet | [AB, 3, 48 6]
na tv eṣiṣyamāṇasya | [AB, 3, 48 7]
yad enā eṣiṣyamāṇasya saṃnirvaped īśvaro hāsya vitte devā arantor yad vā ayam ātmane 'lam amaṃsteti | [AB, 3, 48 8]
tā ha śucivṛkṣo gaupalāyano vṛddhadyumnasyābhipratāriṇasyobhayīr yajñe saṃniruvāpa tasya ha rathagṛtsaṃ gāhamānaṃ dṛṣṭvovācettham aham asya rājanyasya devikāś ca devīś cobhayīr yajñe samamādayaṃ yad asyetthaṃ rathagṛtso gāhata iti catuḥṣaṣṭiḥ kavacinaḥ śaśvaddhāsya te putranaptāra āsuḥ | [AB, 3, 48 9]
{AB, 3, 49}
agniṣṭomaṃ vai devā aśrayantokthāny asurās te samāvadvīryā evāsan na vyāvartanta tān bharadvāja ṛṣīṇām apaśyad ime vā asurā uktheṣu śritās tān eṣāṃ na kaścana paśyatīti so 'gnim udahvayat | [AB, 3, 49 1]
ehy ū ṣu bravāṇi te 'gna itthetarā gira iti | [AB, 3, 49 2]
asuryā ha vā itarā giraḥ | [AB, 3, 49 3]
so 'gnir upottiṣṭhann abravīt kiṃ svid eva mahyaṃ kṛśo dīrghaḥ palito vakṣyatīti | [AB, 3, 49 4]
bharadvājo ha vai kṛśo dīrghaḥ palita āsa | [AB, 3, 49 5]
so 'bravīd ime vā asurā uktheṣu śritās tān vo na kaścana paśyatīti | [AB, 3, 49 6]
tān agnir aśvo bhūtvābhyatyadravad yad agnir aśvo bhūtvābhyatyadravat tat sākamaśvaṃ sāmābhavat tat sākamaśvasya sākamaśvatvam | [AB, 3, 49 7]
tad āhuḥ sākamaśvenokthāni praṇayed apraṇītāni vāva tāny ukthāni yāny anyatra sākamaśvād iti | [AB, 3, 49 8]
pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena praṇayed ity āhuḥ pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena vai devā asurān ukthebhyaḥ prāṇudanta | [AB, 3, 49 9]
tat prāhaiva pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena nayet pra sākamaśvena | [AB, 3, 49 10]
{AB, 3, 50}
te vā asurā maitrāvaruṇasyoktham aśrayanta so 'bravīd indraḥ kaś cāhaṃ cemān ito 'surān notsyāvahā ity ahaṃ cety abravīd varuṇas tasmād aindrāvaruṇam maitrāvaruṇas tṛtīyasavane śaṃsatīndraś ca hi tān varuṇaś ca tato 'nudetām | [AB, 3, 50 1]
te vai tato 'pahatā asurā brāhmaṇācchaṃsina uktham aśrayanta so 'bravīd indraḥ kaścāhaṃ cemān ito 'surān notsyāvahā ity ahaṃ cety abravīd bṛhaspatis tasmād aindrābārhaspatyam brāhmaṇācchaṃsī tṛtīyasavane śaṃsatīndraś ca hi tān bṛhaspatiś ca tato'nudetām | [AB, 3, 50 2]
te vai tato 'pahatā asurā achāvākasyoktham aśrayanta so 'bravīd indraḥ kaś cāhaṃ cemān ito 'surān notsyāvahā ity ahaṃ cety abravīd viṣṇus tasmād aindrāvaiṣṇavam achāvākas tṛtīyasavane śaṃsatīndraś ca hi tān viṣṇuś ca tato 'nudetām | [AB, 3, 50 3]
dvandvam indreṇa devatāḥ śasyante dvandvaṃ vai mithunaṃ tasmād dvandvān mithunam prajāyate prajātyai | [AB, 3, 50 4]
prajāyate prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 3, 50 5]
atha haite potrīyāś ca neṣṭrīyāś ca catvāra ṛtuyājāḥ ṣaﾱ ṛcaḥ sā virāḍ daśinī tad virāji yajñaṃ daśinyām pratiṣṭhāpayanti pratiṣṭhāpayanti | [AB, 3, 50 6]
{AB, 4, 1}
devā vai prathamenāhnendrāya vajraṃ samabharaṃs taṃ dvitīyenāhnāsiñcaṃs taṃ tṛtīyenāhnā prāyacchaṃs taṃ caturthe 'han prāharat tasmāccaturthe 'han ṣoﾱaśinaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 1 1]
vajro vā eṣa yat ṣoﾱaśī tad yac caturthe 'han ṣoﾱaśinaṃ śaṃsati vajram eva tat praharati dviṣate bhrātṛvyāya vadhaṃ yo 'sya stṛtyas tasmai startavai | [AB, 4, 1 2]
vajro vai ṣoﾱaśī paśava ukthāni tam parastād ukthānām paryasya śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 1 3]
taṃ yat parastād ukthānām paryasya śaṃsati vajreṇaiva tat ṣoﾱaśinā paśūn parigacchati tasmāt paśavo vajreṇaiva ṣoﾱaśinā parigatā manuṣyān abhy upāvartante tasmād aśvo vā puruṣo vā gaur vā hastī vā parigata eva svayam ātmaneta eva vācābhiṣiddha upāvartate vajram eva ṣoﾱaśinam paśyan vajreṇaiva ṣoﾱaśinā parigato vāgghi vajro vāk ṣoﾱaśī | [AB, 4, 1 4]
tad āhuḥ kiṃ ṣoﾱaśinaḥ ṣoﾱaśitvam iti ṣoﾱaśaḥ stotrāṇāṃ ṣoﾱaśaḥ śastrāṇāṃ ṣoﾱaśabhir akṣarair ādatte ṣoﾱaśibhiḥ praṇauti ṣoﾱaśapadāṃ nividaṃ dadhāti tat ṣoﾱaśinaḥ ṣoﾱaśitvam | [AB, 4, 1 5]
dve vā akṣare atiricyete ṣoﾱaśino 'nuṣṭubham abhisaṃpannasya vāco vāva tau stanau satyānṛte vāva te | [AB, 4, 1 6]
avaty enaṃ satyaṃ nainam anṛtaṃ hinasti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 1 7]
{AB, 4, 2}
gaurivītaṃ ṣoﾱaśi sāma kurvīta tejaskāmo brahmavarcasakāmas tejo vai brahmavarcasaṃ gaurivītaṃ tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān gaurivītaṃ ṣoﾱaśi sāma kurute | [AB, 4, 2 1]
nānadaṃ ṣoﾱaśi sāma kartavyam ity āhur indro vai vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat tam asmai prāharat tam abhyahanat so 'bhihato vyanadad yad vyanadat tan nānadaṃ sāmābhavat tan nānadasya nānadatvam abhrātṛvyaṃ vā etad bhrātṛvyahā sāma yan nānadam | [AB, 4, 2 2]
abhrātṛvyo bhrātṛvyahā bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān nānadaṃ ṣoﾱaśi sāma kurute | [AB, 4, 2 3]
tad yadi nānadaṃ kuryur avihṛtaḥ ṣoﾱaśī śaṃstavyo 'vihṛtāsu hi tāsu stuvate yadi gaurivītaṃ vihṛtaḥ ṣoﾱaśī śaṃstavyo vihṛtāsu hi tāsu stuvate | [AB, 4, 2 4]
{AB, 4, 3}
athātaś chandāṃsy eva vyatiṣajaty ā tvā vahantu haraya upo ṣu śṛṇuhī gira iti gāyatrīś ca paṅktīś ca vyatiṣajati gāyatro vai puruṣaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ puruṣam eva tat paśubhir vyatiṣajati paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati yad u gāyatrī ca paṅktiś ca te dve anuṣṭubhau teno vāco rūpād anuṣṭubho rūpād vajrarūpān naiti | [AB, 4, 3 1]
yadindra pṛtanājye 'yaṃ te astu haryata ity uṣṇihaś ca bṛhatīś ca vyatiṣajaty auṣṇiho vai puruṣo bārhatāḥ paśavaḥ puruṣam eva tat paśubhir vyatiṣajati paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati yad uṣṇik ca bṛhatī ca te dve anuṣṭubhau teno vāco rūpād anuṣṭubho rūpād vajrarūpān naiti | [AB, 4, 3 2]
ā dhūrṣu asmai brahman vīra brahmakṛtiṃ juṣāṇa iti dvipadāṃ ca triṣṭubhaṃ ca vyatiṣajati dvipād vai puruṣo vīryaṃ triṣṭup puruṣam eva tad vīryeṇa vyatiṣajati vīrye pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmāt puruṣo vīrye pratiṣṭhitaḥ sarveṣām paśūnāṃ vīryavattamo yad u dvipadā ca viṃśatyakṣarā triṣṭup ca te dve anuṣṭubhau teno vāco rūpād anuṣṭubho rūpād vajrarūpānnaiti | [AB, 4, 3 3]
eṣa brahmā pra te mahe vidathe śaṃsiṣaṃ harī iti dvipadāś ca jagatīś ca vyatiṣajati dvipād vai puruṣo jāgatāḥ paśavaḥ puruṣam eva tat paśubhir vyatiṣajati paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmāt puruṣaḥ paśuṣu pratiṣṭhito 'tti cainān adhi ca tiṣṭhati vaśe cāsya yad u dvipadā ca ṣoﾱaśākṣarā jagatī ca te dve anuṣṭubhau teno vāco rūpād anuṣṭubho rūpād vajrarūpān naiti | [AB, 4, 3 4]
trikadrukeṣu mahiṣo yavāśiram pro ṣv asmai puroratham ity aticchandasaḥ śaṃsati chandasāṃ vai yo raso 'tyakṣarat so 'ticchandasam abhy atyakṣarat tad aticchandaso 'ticchandastvaṃ sarvebhyo vā eṣa chandobhyaḥ saṃnirmito yat ṣoﾱaśī tad yad aticchandasaḥ śaṃsati sarvebhya evainaṃ tac chandobhyaḥ saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 3 5]
sarvebhyaś chandobhyaḥ saṃnirmitena ṣoﾱaśinā rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 3 6]
{AB, 4, 4}
mahānāmnīnām upasargān upasṛjati | [AB, 4, 4 1]
ayaṃ vai lokaḥ prathamā mahānāmny antarikṣaloko dvitīyāsau lokas tṛtīyā sarvebhyo vā eṣa lokebhyaḥ saṃnirmito yatṣoﾱaśī tad yan mahānāmnīnām upasargān upasṛjati sarvebhya evainaṃ tal lokebhyaḥ saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 4 2]
sarvebhyo lokebhyaḥ saṃnirmitena ṣoﾱaśinā rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 4 3]
pra pra vas triṣṭubham iṣam arcata prārcata yo vyatīṁr aphāṇayad iti prajñātā anuṣṭubhaḥ śaṃsati tad yatheha ceha cāpathena caritvā panthānam paryaveyāt tādṛk tad yat prajñātā anuṣṭubhaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 4 4]
sa yo vyāpto gataśrīr iva manyetāvihṛtaṃ ṣoﾱaśinaṃ śaṃsayen nec chandasāṃ kṛcchrād avapadyā ity atha yaḥ pāpmānam apajighāṃsuḥ syād vihṛtaṃ ṣoﾱaśinaṃ śaṃsayed vyatiṣakta iva vai puruṣaḥ pāpmanā vyatiṣaktam evāsmai tat pāpmānaṃ śamalaṃ hanti | [AB, 4, 4 5]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 4 6]
ud yad bradhnasya viṣṭapam ity uttamayā paridadhāti svargo vai loko bradhnasya viṣṭapam svargam eva tal lokaṃ yajamānaṃ gamayati | [AB, 4, 4 7]
apāḥ pūrveṣāṃ harivaḥ sutānām iti yajati | [AB, 4, 4 8]
sarvebhyo vā eṣa savanebhyaḥ saṃnirmito yat ṣoﾱaśī tad yad apāḥ pūrveṣāṃ harivaḥ sutānām iti yajati pītavad vai prātaḥsavanam prātaḥsavanād evainaṃ tat saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 4 9]
atho idaṃ savanaṃ kevalaṃ ta iti mādhyaṃdinaṃ vai savanaṃ kevalam mādhyaṃdinād evainaṃ tat savanāt saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 4 10]
mamaddhi somam madhumantam indreti madvad vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ tṛtīyasavanād evainaṃ tat saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 4 11]
satrā vṛṣañ jaṭhara ā vṛṣasveti vṛṣaṇvad vai ṣoﾱaśino rūpaṃ sarvebhyo vā eṣa savanebhyaḥ saṃnirmito yat ṣoﾱaśī tad yad apāḥ pūrveṣāṃ harivaḥ sutānām iti yajati sarvebhya evainaṃ tat savanebhyaḥ saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 4 12]
sarvebhyaḥ savanebhyaḥ saṃnirmitena ṣoﾱaśinā rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 4 13]
mahānāmnīnām pañcākṣarān upasargān upasṛjaty ekādaśākṣareṣu pādeṣu sarvebhyo vā eṣa chandobhyaḥ saṃnirmito yat ṣoﾱaśī tad yan mahānāmnīnām pañcākṣarān upasargān upasṛjaty ekādaśākṣareṣu pādeṣu sarvebhya evainaṃ tac chandobhyaḥ saṃnirmimīte | [AB, 4, 4 14]
sarvebhyaś chandobhyaḥ saṃnirmitena ṣoﾱaśinā rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 4 15]
{AB, 4, 5}
ahar vai devā aśrayanta rātrīm asurās te samāvadvīryā evāsan na vyāvartanta so 'bravīd indraḥ kaś cāhaṃ cemān ito 'surān rātrīm anv aveṣyāva iti sa deveṣu na pratyavindad abibhayū rātres tamaso mṛtyos tasmāddhāpy etarhi naktaṃ yāvanmātram ivaivāpakramya bibheti tama iva hi rātrir mṛtyur iva | [AB, 4, 5 1]
taṃ vai chandāṃsy evānvavāyaṃs taṃ yacchandāṃsy evānvavāyaṃstasmād indraścaiva chandāṃsi ca rātrīṃ vahanti na nivicchasyate na puroruṅ na dhāyyā nānyā devatendraśca hyevachandāṃsi ca rātrīṃ vahanti | [AB, 4, 5 2]
tān vai paryāyair eva paryāyam anudanta yat paryāyaiḥ paryāyam anudanta tat paryāyāṇām paryāyatvam | [AB, 4, 5 3]
tān vai prathamenaiva paryāyeṇa pūrvarātrād anudanta madhyamena madhyarātrād uttamenāpararātrāt | [AB, 4, 5 4]
api śarvaryā anusmasīty abruvann apiśarvarāṇi khalu vā etāni chandāṃsīti ha smāhaitāni hīndraṃ rātres tamaso mṛtyor bibhyatam atyapārayaṃs tad apiśarvarāṇām apiśarvaratvam | [AB, 4, 5 5]
{AB, 4, 6}
pāntam ā vo andhasa ity andhasvatyānuṣṭubhā rātrīm pratipadyate | [AB, 4, 6 1]
ānuṣṭubhī vai rātrir etad rātrirūpam | [AB, 4, 6 2]
andhasvatyaḥ pītavatyo madvatyas triṣṭubho yājyā bhavanty abhirūpā yad yajñe 'bhirūpaṃ tat samṛddham | [AB, 4, 6 3]
prathamena paryāyeṇa stuvate prathamāny eva padāni punar ādadate yad evaiṣām aśvā gāva āsaṃs tad evaiṣāṃ tenādadate | [AB, 4, 6 4]
madhyamena paryāyeṇa stuvate madhyamāny eva padāni punar ādadate yad evaiṣām manorathā āsaṃs tad evaiṣāṃ tenādadate | [AB, 4, 6 5]
uttamena paryāyeṇa stuvata uttamāny eva padāni punar ādadate yad evaiṣāṃ vāso hiraṇyam maṇir adhyātmam āsīt tad evaiṣāṃ tenādadate | [AB, 4, 6 6]
ā dviṣato vasu datte nir enam ebhyaḥ sarvebhyo lokebhyo nudate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 6 7]
pavamānavad ahar ity āhur na rātriḥ pavamānavatī katham ubhe pavamānavatī bhavataḥ kena te samāvadbhājau bhavata iti | [AB, 4, 6 8]
yad evendrāya madvane sutam idaṃ vaso sutam andha idaṃ hy anv ojasā sutam iti stuvanti ca śaṃsanti ca tena rātriḥ pavamānavatī tenobhe pavamānavatī bhavatas tena te samāvadbhājau bhavataḥ | [AB, 4, 6 9]
pañcadaśastotram ahar ity āhur na rātriḥ pañcadaśastotrā katham ubhe pañcadaśastotre bhavataḥ kena te samāvadbhājau bhavata iti | [AB, 4, 6 10]
dvādaśa stotrāṇy apiśarvarāṇi tisṛbhir devatābhiḥ saṃdhinā rāthaṃtareṇa stuvate tena rātriḥ pañcadaśastotrā tenobhe pañcadaśastotre bhavatas tena te samāvadbhājau bhavataḥ | [AB, 4, 6 11]
parimitaṃ stuvanty aparimitam anuśaṃsati parimitaṃ vai bhūtam aparimitam bhavyam aparimitasyāvaruddhyā iti | [AB, 4, 6 12]
atiśaṃsati stotram ati vai prajātmānam ati paśavas tad yat stotram atiśaṃsati yad evāsyāty ātmānaṃ tad evāsyaitenāvarunddhe 'varunddhe | [AB, 4, 6 13]
{AB, 4, 7}
prajāpatir vai somāya rājñe duhitaram prāyacchat sūryāṃ sāvitrīṃ tasyai sarve devā varā āgacchaṃs tasyā etat sahasraṃ vahatum anvākarod yad etad āśvinam ity ācakṣate 'nāśvinaṃ haiva tad yad arvāksahasraṃ tasmāt tat sahasraṃ vaiva śaṃsed bhūyo vā | [AB, 4, 7 1]
prāśya ghṛtaṃ śaṃsed yathā ha vā idam ano vā ratho vākto vartata evaṃ haivākto vartate | [AB, 4, 7 2]
śakunir ivotpatiṣyann āhvayīta | [AB, 4, 7 3]
tasmin devā na samajānata mamedam astu mamedam astv iti te saṃjānānā abruvann ājim asyāyāmahai sa yo na ujjeṣyati tasyedam bhaviṣyatīti te 'gner evādhi gṛhapater ādityaṃ kāṣṭhām akurvata tasmād āgneyī pratipad bhavaty āśvinasyāgnir hotā gṛhapatiḥ sa rājeti | [AB, 4, 7 4]
taddhaika āhur agnim manye pitaram agnim āpim ity etayā pratipadyeta | [AB, 4, 7 5]
divi śukraṃ yajataṃ sūryasyeti prathamayaiva ṛcā kāṣṭhām āpnotīti | [AB, 4, 7 6]
tattan nādṛtyaṃ ya enaṃ tatra brūyād agnim agnim iti vai pratyapādy agnim āpatsyatīti śaśvat tathā syāt | [AB, 4, 7 7]
tasmād agnir hotā gṛhapatiḥ sa rājety etayaiva pratipadyeta gṛhapativatī prajātimatī śāntā sarvāyuḥ sarvāyutvāya | [AB, 4, 7 8]
sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 7 9]
{AB, 4, 8}
tāsāṃ vai devatānām ājiṃ dhāvantīnām abhisṛṣṭānām agnir mukham prathamaḥ pratyapadyata tam aśvināv anvāgacchatāṃ tam abrūtām apodihy āvāṃ vā idaṃ jeṣyāva iti sa tathety abravīt tasya vai mamehāpyastv iti tatheti tasmā apy atrākurutāṃ tasmād āgneyam āśvine śasyate | [AB, 4, 8 1]
tā uṣasam anvāgacchatāṃ tām abrūtām apodihy āvāṃ vā idaṃ jeṣyāva iti sā tathety abravīt tasyai vai mamehāpyastv iti tatheti tasyā apy atrākurutāṃ tasmād uṣasyam āśvine śasyate | [AB, 4, 8 2]
tāv indram anvāgacchatāṃ tam abrūtām āvāṃ vā idam maghavañ jeṣyāva iti na ha taṃ dadhṛṣatur apodihīti vaktuṃ sa tathety abravīt tasya vai mamehāpyastv iti tatheti tasmā apy atrākurutāṃ tasmād aindram āśvine śasyate | [AB, 4, 8 3]
tad aśvinā udajayatām aśvināv āśnuvātāṃ yad aśvinā udajayatām aśvināv āśnuvātāṃ tasmād etad āśvinam ity ācakṣate | [AB, 4, 8 4]
aśnute yad yat kāmayate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 8 5]
tad āhur yacchasyata āgneyaṃ śasyata uṣasyam śasyata aindram atha kasmād etad āśvinam ity ācakṣata ity aśvinau hi tad udajayatām aśvināv āśnuvātāṃ yad aśvinā udajayatām aśvināv āśnuvātāṃ tasmād etad āśvinam ity ācakṣate | [AB, 4, 8 6]
aśnute yad yat kāmayate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 8 7]
{AB, 4, 9}
aśvatarīrathenāgnir ājim adhāvat tāsām prājamāno yonim akūﾱayat tasmāt tā na vijāyante | [AB, 4, 9 1]
gobhir aruṇair uṣā ājim adhāvat tasmād uṣasy āgatāyām aruṇam ivaiva prabhāty uṣaso rūpam | [AB, 4, 9 2]
aśvarathenendra ājim adhāvat tasmāt sa uccairghoṣa upabdimān kṣatrasya rūpam aindro hi sa | [AB, 4, 9 3]
gardabharathenāśvinā udajayatām aśvināv āśnuvātāṃ yad aśvinā udajayatām aśvināv āśnuvātāṃ tasmāt sa sṛtajavo dugdhadohaḥ sarveṣām etarhi vāhanānām anāśiṣṭho retasas tv asya vīryaṃ nāharatāṃ tasmāt sa dviretā vājī | [AB, 4, 9 4]
tad āhuḥ sapta sauryāṇi chandāṃsi śaṃsed yathaivāgneyaṃ yathoṣasyaṃ yathāśvinaṃ sapta vai devalokāḥ sarveṣu devalokeṣu rādhnotīti | [AB, 4, 9 5]
tattan nādṛtyaṃ trīṇy eva śaṃset trayo vā ime trivṛto lokā eṣām eva lokānām abhijityai | [AB, 4, 9 6]
tad āhur ud u tyaṃ jātavedasam iti sauryāṇi pratipadyeteti | [AB, 4, 9 7]
tat tan nādṛtyaṃ yathaiva gatvā kāṣṭhām aparādhnuyāt tādṛk tat | [AB, 4, 9 8]
sūryo no divas pātv ity etenaiva pratipadyeta yathaiva gatvā kāṣṭhām abhipadyeta tādṛk tat | [AB, 4, 9 9]
ud u tyaṃ jātavedasam iti dvitīyaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 9 10]
citraṃ devānām ud agād anīkam iti traiṣṭubham asau vāva citraṃ devānām udeti tasmād etacchaṃsati | [AB, 4, 9 11]
namo mitrasya varuṇasya cakṣasa iti jāgataṃ tadvāśīḥpadam āśiṣam evaitenāśāsta ātmane ca yajamānāya ca | [AB, 4, 9 12]
{AB, 4, 10}
tad āhuḥ sūryo nātiśasyo bṛhatī nātiśasyā yat sūryam atiśaṃsed brahmavarcasam atipadyeta yad bṛhatīm atiśaṃset prāṇān atipadyeteti | [AB, 4, 10 1]
indra kratuṃ na ā bharety aindram pragāthaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 2]
śikṣā ṇo asmin puruhūta yāmani jīvā jyotir aśīmahīti | [AB, 4, 10 3]
asau vāva jyotis tena sūryaṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 4]
yad u bārhataḥ pragāthas tena bṛhatīṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 5]
abhi tvā śūra nonuma iti rāthaṃtarīṃ yoniṃ śaṃsati rāthaṃtareṇa vai saṃdhināśvināya stuvate tad yad rāthaṃtarīṃ yoniṃ śaṃsati rathaṃtarasyaiva sayonitvāya | [AB, 4, 10 6]
īśānam asya jagataḥ svardṛśam ity asau vāva svardṛk tena sūryaṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 7]
yad u bārhataḥ pragāthas tena bṛhatīṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 8]
bahavaḥ sūracakṣasa iti maitrāvaruṇam pragāthaṃ śaṃsaty ahar vai mitro rātrir varuṇa ubhe vā eṣo 'horātre ārabhate yo 'tirātram upaiti tad yan maitrāvaruṇam pragāthaṃ śaṃsaty ahorātrayor evainaṃ tat pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 4, 10 9]
sūracakṣasa iti tena sūryaṃ nātiśaṃsati yad u bārhataḥ pragāthas tena bṛhatīṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 10]
mahī dyauḥ pṛthivī ca nas te hi dyāvāpṛthivī viśvaśambhuveti dyāvāpṛthivīye śaṃsati dyāvāpṛthivī vai pratiṣṭhe iyam eveha pratiṣṭhāsāv amutra tad yad dyāvāpṛthivīye śaṃsati pratiṣṭhayor evainaṃ tat pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 4, 10 11]
devo devī dharmaṇā sūryaḥ śucir iti tena sūryaṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 12]
yad u gāyatrī ca jagatī ca te dve bṛhatyau tena bṛhatīṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 13]
viśvasya devī mṛcayasya janmano na yā roṣāti na grabhad iti dvipadām śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 14]
citaidham uktham iti ha sma vā etad ācakṣate yad etad āśvinaṃ nirṛtir ha sma pāśiny upāste yadaiva hotā paridhāsyaty atha pāśān pratimokṣyāmīti tato vā etām bṛhaspatir dvipadām apaśyan na yā roṣāti na grabhad iti tayā nirṛtyāḥ pāśinyā adharācaḥ pāśān apāsyat tad yad etāṃ dvipadāṃ hotā śaṃsati nirṛtyā eva tat pāśinyā adharācaḥ pāśān apāsyati svasty eva hotonmucyate sarvāyuḥ sarvāyutvāya | [AB, 4, 10 15]
sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 10 16]
mṛcayasya janmana ity asau vāva marcayatīva tena sūryaṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 17]
yad u dvipadā puruṣachandasaṃ sā sarvāṇi chandāṃsy abhyāptā tena bṛhatīṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 10 18]
{AB, 4, 11}
brāhmaṇaspatyayā paridadhāti brahma vai bṛhaspatir brahmaṇy evainaṃ tad antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 4, 11 1]
evā pitre viśvadevāya vṛṣṇa ity etayā paridadhyāt prajākāmaḥ paśukāmaḥ | [AB, 4, 11 2]
bṛhaspate suprajā vīravanta iti prajayā vai suprajā vīravān | [AB, 4, 11 3]
vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām iti | [AB, 4, 11 4]
prajāvān paśumān rayimān vīravān bhavati yatraivaṃ vidvān etayā paridadhāti | [AB, 4, 11 5]
bṛhaspate ati yad aryo arhād ity etayā paridadhyāt tejaskāmo brahmavarcasakāmo 'tīva vānyān brahmavarcasam arhati | [AB, 4, 11 6]
dyumad iti dyumad iva vai brahmavarcasaṃ vibhātīti vīva vai brahmavarcasam bhāti | [AB, 4, 11 7]
yad dīdayac chavasa ṛtaprajāteti dīdāyeva vai brahmavarcasam | [AB, 4, 11 8]
tad asmāsu draviṇaṃ dhehi citram iti citram iva vai brahmavarcasam | [AB, 4, 11 9]
brahmavarcasī brahmayaśasī bhavati yatraivaṃ vidvān etayā paridadhāti | [AB, 4, 11 10]
tasmād evaṃ vidvān etayaiva paridadhyāt | [AB, 4, 11 11]
brāhmaṇaspatyā tena sūryaṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 11 12]
yad u triṣṭubhaṃ triḥ śaṃsati sā sarvāṇi chandāṃsy abhyāptā tena bṛhatīṃ nātiśaṃsati | [AB, 4, 11 13]
gāyatryā ca triṣṭubhā ca vaṣaṭkuryāt | [AB, 4, 11 14]
brahma vai gāyatrī vīryam triṣṭub brahmaṇaiva tad vīryaṃ saṃdadhāti | [AB, 4, 11 15]
brahmavarcasī brahmayaśasī vīryavān bhavati yatraivaṃ vidvān gāyatryā ca triṣṭubhā ca vaṣaṭkaroti | [AB, 4, 11 16]
aśvinā vāyunā yuvaṃ sudakṣobhā pibatam aśvineti | [AB, 4, 11 17]
gāyatryā ca virājā ca vaṣaṭkuryād brahma vai gāyatry annaṃ virāḍ brahmaṇaiva tad annādyaṃ saṃdadhāti | [AB, 4, 11 18]
brahmavarcasī brahmayaśasī bhavati brahmādyam annam atti yatraivaṃ vidvān gāyatryā ca virājā ca vaṣaṭkaroti | [AB, 4, 11 19]
tasmād evaṃ vidvān gāyatryā caiva virājā ca vaṣaṭkuryāt pra vām andhāṃsi madyāny asthur ubhā pibatam aśvinety etābhyām | [AB, 4, 11 20]
{AB, 4, 12}
caturviṃśam etad ahar upayanty ārambhaṇīyam | [AB, 4, 12 1]
etena vai saṃvatsaram ārabhanta etena stomāṃś ca chandāṃsi caitena sarvā devatā anārabdhaṃ vai tac chando 'nārabdhā sā devatā yad etasminn ahani nārabhante tad ārambhaṇīyasyārambhaṇīyatvam | [AB, 4, 12 2]
caturviṃśaḥ stomo bhavati tac caturviṃśasya caturviṃśatvam | [AB, 4, 12 3]
caturviṃśatir vā ardhamāsā ardhamāsaśa eva tat saṃvatsaram ārabhante | [AB, 4, 12 4]
ukthyo bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 4, 12 5]
tasya pañcadaśa stotrāṇi bhavanti pañcadaśa śastrāni sa māso māsaśa eva tat saṃvatsaram ārabhante | [AB, 4, 12 6]
tasya ṣaṣṭiś ca trīṇi ca śatāni stotriyās tāvanti saṃvatsarasyāhāny ahaśśa eva tat saṃvatsaram ārabhante | [AB, 4, 12 7]
agniṣṭoma etad ahaḥ syād ity āhur agniṣṭomo vai saṃvatsaro na vā etad anyo 'gniṣṭomād ahar dādhāra na vivyāceti | [AB, 4, 12 8]
sa yady agniṣṭomaḥ syād aṣṭācatvāriṃśās trayaḥ pavamānāḥ syuś caturviṃśānītarāṇi stotrāṇi tad u ṣaṣṭiś caiva trīṇi ca śatāni stotriyās tāvanti saṃvatsarasyāhāny ahaśśa eva tat saṃvatsaram ārabhante | [AB, 4, 12 9]
ukthya eva syāt paśusamṛddho yajñaḥ paśusamṛddhaṃ satraṃ sarvāṇi caturviṃśāni stotrāṇi pratyakṣāddhyetad ahaś caturviṃśaṃ tasmād ukthya eva syāt | [AB, 4, 12 10]
{AB, 4, 13}
bṛhadrathaṃtare sāmanī bhavata ete vai yajñasya nāvau sampāriṇyau yad bṛhadrathaṃtare tābhyām eva tat saṃvatsaraṃ taranti | [AB, 4, 13 1]
pādau vai bṛhadrathaṃtare śira etad ahaḥ pādābhyām eva tacchriyaṃ śiro 'bhyāyanti | [AB, 4, 13 2]
pakṣau vai bṛhadrathaṃtare śira etad ahaḥ pakṣābhyām eva tacchriyaṃ śiro 'bhyāyuvate | [AB, 4, 13 3]
te ubhe na samavasṛjye ya ubhe samavasṛjeyur yathaiva chinnā naur bandhanāt tīraṃ tīram ṛcchantī plavetaivam eva te satriṇas tīraṃ tīram ṛcchantaḥ plaveran ya ubhe samavasṛjeyuḥ | [AB, 4, 13 4]
tad yadi rathaṃtaram avasṛjeyur bṛhataivobhe anavasṛṣṭe atha yadi bṛhad avasṛjeyū rathaṃtareṇaivobhe anavasṛṣṭe | [AB, 4, 13 5]
yad vai rathaṃtaraṃ tad vairūpaṃ yad bṛhat tad vairājam yad rathaṃtaraṃ tacchākvaraṃ yad bṛhat tad raivatam evam ete ubhe anavasṛṣṭe bhavataḥ | [AB, 4, 13 6]
ye vā evaṃ vidvāṃsa etad ahar upayanty āptvā vai te 'haśśaḥ saṃvatsaram āptvārdhamāsaśa āptvā māsaśa āptvā stomāṃś ca chandāṃsi cāptvā sarvā devatās tapa eva tapyamānāḥ somapītham bhakṣayantaḥ saṃvatsaram abhiṣuṇvanta āsate | [AB, 4, 13 7]
ye vā ata ūrdhvaṃ saṃvatsaram upayanti guruṃ vai te bhāram abhinidadhate saṃ vai gurur bhāraḥ śṛṇāty atha ya enam parastāt karmabhir āptvāvastād upaiti sa vai svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute | [AB, 4, 13 8]
{AB, 4, 14}
yad vai caturviṃśaṃ tan mahāvratam bṛhaddivenātra hotā retaḥ siñcati tad ado mahāvratīyenāhnā prajanayati saṃvatsare saṃvatsare vai retaḥ siktaṃ jāyate tasmāt samānam bṛhaddivo niṣkevalyam bhavaty eṣa ha vā enam parastāt karmabhir āptvāvastād upaiti ya evaṃ vidvān etad ahar upaiti | [AB, 4, 14 1]
svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 14 2]
yo vai saṃvatsarasyāvāraṃ ca pāraṃ ca veda sa vai svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute 'tirātro vā asya prāyaṇīyo 'vāram udayanīyaḥ pāram | [AB, 4, 14 3]
svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 14 4]
yo vai saṃvatsarasyāvarodhanaṃ codrodhanaṃ ca veda sa vai svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute 'tirātro vā asya prāyaṇīyo 'varodhanam udayanīya udrodhanam | [AB, 4, 14 5]
svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 14 6]
yo vai saṃvatsarasya prāṇodānau veda sa vai svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute 'tirātro vā asya prāyaṇīyaḥ prāṇa udāna udayanīyaḥ | [AB, 4, 14 7]
svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 14 8]
{AB, 4, 15}
jyotir gaur āyur iti stomebhir yanty ayaṃ vai loko jyotir antarikṣaṃ gaur asau loka āyuḥ | [AB, 4, 15 1]
sa evaiṣa uttaras tryahaḥ | [AB, 4, 15 2]
jyotir gaur āyur iti trīṇy ahāni gaur āyur jyotir iti trīṇi | [AB, 4, 15 3]
ayaṃ vai loko jyotir asau loko jyotis te ete jyotiṣī ubhayataḥ saṃlokete | [AB, 4, 15 4]
tenaitenobhayatojyotiṣā ṣaﾱahena yanti tad yad etenobhayatojyotiṣā ṣaﾱahena yanty anayor eva tal lokayor ubhayataḥ pratitiṣṭhanto yanty asmiṃś ca loke 'muṣmiṃś cobhayoḥ | [AB, 4, 15 5]
pariyad vā etad devacakraṃ yad abhiplavaḥ ṣaﾱahas tasya yāv abhito 'gniṣṭomau tau pradhī ye catvāro madhya ukthyās tan nabhyam | [AB, 4, 15 6]
gacchati vai vartamānena yatra kāmayate tat svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 15 7]
yo vai tad veda yat prathamaḥ ṣaﾱahaḥ sa vai svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute yas tad veda yad dvitīyo yas tad veda yat tṛtīyo yas tad veda yac caturtho yas tad veda yat pañcamaḥ | [AB, 4, 15 8]
{AB, 4, 16}
prathamaṃ ṣaﾱaham upayanti ṣaﾱ ahāni bhavanti ṣaḍ vā ṛtava ṛtuśa eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanty ṛtuśaḥ saṃvatsare pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 4, 16 1]
dvitīyaṃ ṣaﾱaham upayanti dvādaśāhāni bhavanti dvādaśa vai māsā māsaśa eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanti māsaśaḥ saṃvatsare pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 4, 16 2]
tṛtīyaṃ ṣaﾱaham upayanty aṣṭādaśāhāni bhavanti tāni dvedhā navānyāni navānyāni nava vai prāṇā nava svargā lokāḥ prāṇāṃś caiva tat svargāṃś ca lokān āpnuvanti prāṇeṣu caiva tat svargeṣu ca lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 4, 16 3]
caturthaṃ ṣaﾱaham upayanti caturviṃśatir ahāni bhavanti caturviṃśatir vā ardhamāsā ardhamāsaśa eva tat saṃvatsaram āpnuvanty ardhamāsaśaḥ saṃvatsare pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 4, 16 4]
pañcamaṃ ṣaﾱaham upayanti triṃśad ahāni bhavanti triṃśadakṣarā vai virāḍ virāﾱ annādyaṃ virājam eva tan māsi māsy abhisaṃpādayanto yanti | [AB, 4, 16 5]
annādyakāmāḥ khalu vai satram āsata tad yad virājam māsi māsy abhisaṃpādayanto yanty annādyam eva tan māsi māsy avarundhānā yanty asmai ca lokāyāmuṣmai cobhābhyām | [AB, 4, 16 6]
{AB, 4, 17}
gavām ayanena yanti gāvo vā ādityā ādityānām eva tad ayanena yanti | [AB, 4, 17 1]
gāvo vai satram āsata śaphāñchṛṅgāṇi siṣāsantyas tāsāṃ daśame māsi śaphāḥ śṛṅgāṇy ajāyanta tā abruvan yasmai kāmāyādīkṣāmahy āpāma tam uttiṣṭhāmeti tā yā udatiṣṭhaṃs tā etāḥ śṛṅgiṇyaḥ | [AB, 4, 17 2]
atha yāḥ samāpayiṣyāmaḥ saṃvatsaram ity āsata tāsām aśraddhayā śṛṅgāṇi prāvartanta tā etās tūparā ūrjaṃ tv asunvaṃs tasmād u tāḥ sarvān ṛtūn prāptvottaram uttiṣṭhanty ūrjaṃ hy asunvan sarvasya vai gāvaḥ premāṇaṃ sarvasya cārutāṃ gatāḥ | [AB, 4, 17 3]
sarvasya premāṇaṃ sarvasya cārutāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 17 4]
ādityāś ca ha vā aṅgirasaś ca svarge loke 'spardhanta vayam pūrva eṣyāmo vayam iti te hādityāḥ pūrve svargaṃ lokaṃ jagmuḥ paścevāṅgirasaḥ ṣaṣṭyāṃ vā varṣeṣu | [AB, 4, 17 5]
yathā vā prāyaṇīyo 'tirātraś caturviṃśa ukthyaḥ sarve 'bhiplavāḥ ṣaﾱahā ākṣyanty anyāny ahāni tad ādityānām ayanam | [AB, 4, 17 6]
prāyaṇīyo 'tirātraś caturviṃśa ukthyaḥ sarve pṛṣṭhyāḥ ṣaﾱahā ākṣyanty anyāny ahāni tad aṅgirasām ayanam | [AB, 4, 17 7]
sā yathā srutir añjasāyany evam abhiplavaḥ ṣaﾱahaḥ svargasya lokasyātha yathā mahāpathaḥ paryāṇa evam pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaﾱahaḥ svargasya lokasya tad yad ubhābhyāṃ yanty ubhābhyāṃ vai yan na riṣyaty ubhayoḥ kāmayor upāptyai yaś cābhiplave ṣaﾱahe yaś ca pṛṣṭhye | [AB, 4, 17 8]
{AB, 4, 18}
ekaviṃśam etad ahar upayanti viṣuvantam madhye saṃvatsarasya | [AB, 4, 18 1]
etena vai devā ekaviṃśenādityaṃ svargāya lokāyodayacchan | [AB, 4, 18 2]
sa eṣa ita ekaviṃśaḥ | [AB, 4, 18 3]
tasya daśāvastād ahāni divākīrtyasya bhavanti daśa parastān madhya eṣa ekaviṃśa ubhayato virāji pratiṣṭhita ubhayato hi vā eṣa virāji pratiṣṭhitas tasmād eṣo 'ntaremāṃllokān yan na vyathate | [AB, 4, 18 4]
tasya vai devā ādityasya svargāl lokād avapātād abibhayus taṃ tribhiḥ svargair lokair avastāt pratyuttabhnuvan stomā vai trayaḥ svargā lokās tasya parāco 'tipātād abibhayus taṃ tribhiḥ svargair lokaiḥ parastāt pratyastabhnuvan stomā vai trayaḥ svargā lokās tat trayo 'vastāt saptadaśā bhavanti trayaḥ parastān madhya eṣa ekaviṃśa ubhayataḥ svarasāmabhir dhṛta ubhayato hi vā eṣa svarasāmabhir dhṛtas tasmād eṣo 'ntaremāṃllokān yan na vyathate | [AB, 4, 18 5]
tasya vai devā ādityasya svargāl lokād avapātād abibhayus tam paramaiḥ svargair lokair avastāt pratyuttabhnuvan stomā vai paramāḥ svargā lokās tasya parāco 'tipātād abibhayus tam paramaiḥ svargair lokaiḥ parastāt pratyastabhnuvan stomā vai paramāḥ svargā lokās tat trayo 'vastāt saptadaśā bhavanti trayaḥ parastāt te dvau dvau sampadya trayaś catustriṃśā bhavanti catustriṃśo vai stomānām uttamas teṣu vā eṣa etad adhyāhitas tapati teṣu hi vā eṣa etad adhyāhitas tapati | [AB, 4, 18 6]
sa vā eṣa uttaro 'smāt sarvasmād bhūtād bhaviṣyataḥ sarvam evedam atirocate yad idaṃ kiṃcottaro bhavati | [AB, 4, 18 7]
yasmād uttaro bubhūṣati tasmād uttaro bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 18 8]
{AB, 4, 19}
svarasāmna upayantīme vai lokāḥ svarasāmāna imān vai lokān svarasāmabhir aspṛṇvaṃs tat svarasāmnāṃ svarasāmatvaṃ tad yat svarasāmna upayanty eṣv evainaṃ tallokeṣv ābhajanti | [AB, 4, 19 1]
teṣāṃ vai devāḥ saptadaśānām pravlayād abibhayuḥ samā iva vai stomā avigūﾱhā iveme ha na pravliyerann iti tān sarvaiḥ stomair avastāt paryārṣan sarvaiḥ pṛṣṭhaiḥ parastāt tad yad abhijit sarvastomo 'vastād bhavati viśvajit sarvapṛṣṭhaḥ parastāt tat saptadaśān ubhayataḥ paryṛṣanti dhṛtyā apravlayāya | [AB, 4, 19 2]
tasya vai devā ādityasya svargāl lokād avapātād abibhayus tam pañcabhī raśmibhir udavayan raśmayo vai divākīrtyāni mahādivākīrtyaṃ pṛṣṭham bhavati vikarṇam brahmasāma bhāsam agniṣṭomasāmobhe bṛhadrathaṃtare pavamānayor bhavatas tad ādityam pañcabhī raśmibhir udvayanti dhṛtyā anavapātāya | [AB, 4, 19 3]
udita āditye prātaranuvākam anubrūyāt sarvaṃ hy evaitad ahar divākīrtyam bhavati | [AB, 4, 19 4]
sauryam paśum anyaṅgaśvetaṃ savanīyasyopālambhyam ālabheran sūryadevatyaṃ hy etad ahaḥ | [AB, 4, 19 5]
ekaviṃśatiṃ sāmidhenīr anubrūyāt pratyakṣāddhyetad ahar ekaviṃśam | [AB, 4, 19 6]
ekapañcāśataṃ dvipañcāśataṃ vā śastvā madhye nividaṃ dadhāti tāvatīr uttarāḥ śaṃsati śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ śatavīryaḥ śatendriya āyuṣy evainaṃ tad vīrya indriye dadhāti | [AB, 4, 19 7]
{AB, 4, 20}
dūrohaṇaṃ rohati svargo vai loko dūrohaṇam | [AB, 4, 20 1]
svargam eva tal lokaṃ rohati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 20 2]
yad eva dūrohaṇam asau vai dūroho yo 'sau tapati kaścid vā atra gacchati sa yad dūrohaṇaṃ rohaty etam eva tad rohati | [AB, 4, 20 3]
haṃsavatyā rohati | [AB, 4, 20 4]
haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity eṣa vai haṃsaḥ śuciṣat | [AB, 4, 20 5]
vasur antarikṣad ity eṣa vai vasur antarikṣasat | [AB, 4, 20 6]
hotā vediṣad ity eṣa vai hotā vediṣat | [AB, 4, 20 7]
atithir duroṇasad ity eṣa vā atithir duroṇasat | [AB, 4, 20 8]
nṛṣad ity eṣa vai nṛṣat | [AB, 4, 20 9]
varasad ity eṣa vai varasad varaṃ vā etat sadmanāṃ yasminn eṣa āsannas tapati | [AB, 4, 20 10]
ṛtasad ity eṣa vai satyasat | [AB, 4, 20 11]
vyomasad ity eṣa vai vyomasad vyoma vā etat sadmanāṃ yasminn eṣa āsannas tapati | [AB, 4, 20 12]
adbhyaḥ vai eṣā prātar udeti | [AB, 4, 20 637187_1]
apaḥ sāyam praviśati | [AB, 4, 20 637187_2]
gojā ity eṣa vai gojāḥ | [AB, 4, 20 14]
ṛtajā ity eṣa vai satyajāḥ | [AB, 4, 20 15]
adrijā ity eṣa vā adrijāḥ | [AB, 4, 20 16]
ṛtam ity eṣa vai satyam | [AB, 4, 20 17]
eṣa etāni sarvāṇy eṣā ha vā asya chandassu pratyakṣatamād iva rūpam | [AB, 4, 20 18]
tasmād yatra kva ca dūrohaṇaṃ roheddhaṃsavatyaiva rohet | [AB, 4, 20 19]
tārkṣye svargakāmasya rohet | [AB, 4, 20 20]
tārkṣyo ha vā etam pūrvo 'dhvānam aid yatrādo gāyatrī suparṇo bhūtvā somam āharat tad yathā kṣetrajñam adhvanaḥ puraetāraṃ kurvīta tādṛk tad yad eva tārkṣye 'yaṃ vai tārkṣyo yo 'yam pavata eṣa svargasya lokasyābhivoﾱhā | [AB, 4, 20 21]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam ity eṣa vai vājī devajūtaḥ | [AB, 4, 20 22]
sahāvānaṃ tarutāraṃ rathānām ity eṣa vai sahāvāṃs tarutaiṣa hīmāṃllokān sadyas tarati | [AB, 4, 20 23]
ariṣṭanemim pṛtanājam āśum ity eṣa vā ariṣṭanemiḥ pṛtanājid āśuḥ | [AB, 4, 20 24]
svastaya iti svastitām āśāste | [AB, 4, 20 25]
tārkṣyam ihā huvemeti hvayaty evainam etat | [AB, 4, 20 26]
indrasyeva rātim ājohuvānāḥ svastaya iti svastitām evāśāste | [AB, 4, 20 27]
nāvam ivā ruhemeti sam evainam etad adhirohati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai sampattyai saṃgatyai | [AB, 4, 20 28]
urvī na pṛthvī bahule gabhīre mā vām etau mā paretau riṣāmetīme evaitad anumantrayata ā ca parā ca meṣyan | [AB, 4, 20 29]
sadyaś cid yaḥ śavasā pañca kṛṣṭīḥ sūrya iva jyotiṣāpas tatāneti pratyakṣaṃ sūryam abhivadati | [AB, 4, 20 30]
sahasrasāḥ śatasā asya raṃhir na smā varante yuvatiṃ na śaryām ity āśiṣam evaitenāśāsta ātmane ca yajamānebhyaś ca | [AB, 4, 20 31]
{AB, 4, 21}
āhūya dūrohaṇaṃ rohati svargo vai loko dūrohaṇaṃ vāg āhāvo brahma vai vāk sa yad āhvayate tad brahmaṇāhāvena svargaṃ lokaṃ rohati | [AB, 4, 21 1]
sa pacchaḥ prathamaṃ rohatīmaṃ tal lokam āpnoty athārdharcaśo 'ntarikṣaṃ tad āpnoty atha tripadyāmuṃ tallokam āpnoty atha kevalyā tad etasmin pratitiṣṭhati ya eṣa tapati | [AB, 4, 21 2]
tripadyā pratyavarohati yathā śākhāṃ dhārayamāṇas tad amuṣmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhaty ardharcaśo 'ntarikṣe paccho 'smiṃlloka āptvaiva tat svargaṃ lokaṃ yajamānā asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhanti | [AB, 4, 21 3]
atha ya ekakāmāḥ syuḥ svargakāmāḥ parāñcam eva teṣāṃ rohet te jayeyur haiva svargaṃ lokam | [AB, 4, 21 4]
na tv evāsmiṃlloke jyog iva vaseyuḥ | [AB, 4, 21 5]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandāṃsi paśūnāṃ avaruddhyai | [AB, 4, 21 6]
{AB, 4, 22}
yathā vai puruṣa evaṃ viṣuvāṃs tasya yathā dakṣiṇo 'rdha evam pūrvo 'rdho viṣuvato yathottaro 'rdha evam uttaro 'rdho viṣuvatas tasmād uttara ity ācakṣate prabāhuk sataḥ śira eva viṣuvān bidalasaṃhita iva vai puruṣas taddhāpi syūmeva madhye śīrṣṇo vijñāyate | [AB, 4, 22 1]
tad āhur viṣuvaty evaitad ahaḥ śaṃsed viṣuvān vā etad ukthānām ukthaṃ viṣuvān viṣuvān iti ha viṣuvanto bhavanti śreṣṭhatām aśnuvata iti | [AB, 4, 22 2]
tat tan nādṛtyaṃ saṃvatsara eva śaṃsed reto vā etat saṃvatsaraṃ dadhato yanti | [AB, 4, 22 3]
yāni vai purā saṃvatsarād retāṃsi jāyante yāni pañcamāsyāni yāni ṣaṇmāsyāni srīvyanti vai tāni na vai tair bhuñjate | [AB, 4, 22 4]
atha yāny eva daśamāsyāni jāyante yāni sāṃvatsarikāṇi tair bhuñjate tasmāt saṃvatsara evaitad ahaḥ śaṃset | [AB, 4, 22 5]
saṃvatsaro hy etad ahar āpnoti saṃvatsaraṃ hy etad ahar āpnuvanty eṣa ha vai saṃvatsareṇa pāpmānam apahata eṣa viṣuvatāṅgebhyo haiva māsaiḥ pāpmānam apahate śīrṣṇo viṣuvatā | [AB, 4, 22 6]
apa saṃvatsareṇa pāpmānaṃ hate 'pa viṣuvatā ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 22 7]
vaiśvakarmaṇam ṛṣabhaṃ savanīyasyopālambhyam ālabheran dvirūpam ubhayata etam mahāvratīye 'hani | [AB, 4, 22 8]
indro vai vṛtraṃ hatvā viśvakarmābhavat prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā viśvakarmābhavat saṃvatsaro viśvakarmendram eva tadātmānam prajāpatiṃ saṃvatsaraṃ viśvakarmāṇam āpnuvantīndra eva tadātmani prajāpatau saṃvatsare viśvakarmaṇy antataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 22 9]
{AB, 4, 23}
prajāpatir akāmayata prajāyeya bhūyān syām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa tapas taptvemaṃ dvādaśāham apaśyad ātmana evāṅgeṣu ca prāṇeṣu ca tam ātmana evāṅgebhyaś ca prāṇebhyaś ca dvādaśadhā niramimīta tam āharat tenāyajata tato vai so 'bhavad ātmanā pra prajayā paśubhir ajāyata | [AB, 4, 23 1]
bhavaty ātmanā pra prajayā paśubhir jāyate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 23 2]
so 'kāmayata kathaṃ nu gāyatryā sarvato dvādaśāham paribhūya sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnuyām iti taṃ vai tejasaiva purastāt paryabhavac chandobhir madhyato 'kṣarair upariṣṭād gāyatryā sarvato dvādaśāham paribhūya sarvām ṛddhim ārdhnot | [AB, 4, 23 3]
sarvām ṛddhim ṛdhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 23 4]
yo vai gāyatrīṃ pakṣiṇīṃ cakṣuṣmatīṃ jyotiṣmatīm bhāsvatīṃ veda gāyatryā pakṣiṇyā cakṣuṣmatyā jyotiṣmatyā bhāsvatyā svargaṃ lokam ety eṣā vai gāyatrī pakṣiṇī cakṣuṣmatī jyotiṣmatī bhāsvatī yad dvādaśāhas tasya yāv abhito 'tirātrau tau pakṣau yāv antarāgniṣṭomau te cakṣuṣī ye 'ṣṭau madhya ukthyāḥ sa ātmā | [AB, 4, 23 5]
gāyatryā pakṣiṇyā cakṣuṣmatyā jyotiṣmatyā bhāsvatyā svargaṃ lokam eti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 23 6]
{AB, 4, 24}
trayaś ca vā ete tryahā ā daśamam ahar ā dvāv atirātrau yad dvādaśāhaḥ | [AB, 4, 24 1]
dvādaśāhāni dīkṣito bhavati yajñiya eva tair bhavati | [AB, 4, 24 2]
dvādaśa rātrīr upasada upaiti śarīram eva tābhir dhūnute | [AB, 4, 24 3]
dvādaśāham prasutaḥ | [AB, 4, 24 4]
bhūtvā śarīraṃ dhūtvā śuddhaḥ pūto devatā apyeti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 24 5]
ṣaṭtriṃśadaho vā eṣa yad dvādaśāhaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā vai bṛhatī bṛhatyā vā etad ayanaṃ yad dvādaśāho bṛhatyā vai devā imāṃllokān āśnuvata te vai daśabhir evākṣarair imaṃ lokam āśnuvata daśabhir antarikṣam daśabhir divaṃ caturbhiś catasro diśo dvābhyām evāsmiṃlloke pratyatiṣṭhan | [AB, 4, 24 6]
pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 24 7]
tad āhur yad anyāni chandāṃsi varṣīyāṃsi bhūyo 'kṣaratarāṇy atha kasmād etām bṛhatīty ācakṣata iti | [AB, 4, 24 8]
etayā hi devā imāṃllokān āśnuvata te vai daśabhir evākṣarair imaṃ lokam āśnuvata daśabhir antarikṣaṃ daśabhir divaṃ caturbhiś catasro diśo dvābhyām evāsmiṃlloke pratyatiṣṭhaṃs tasmād etām bṛhatīty ācakṣate | [AB, 4, 24 9]
aśnute yadyat kāmayate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 24 10]
{AB, 4, 25}
prajāpatiyajño vā eṣa yad dvādaśāhaḥ prajāpatir vā etenāgre 'yajata dvādaśāhena so 'bravīd ṛtūṃśca māsāṃśca yājayata mā dvādaśāheneti taṃ dīkṣayitvānapakramaṃ gamayitvābruvan dehi nu no 'tha tvā yājayiṣyāma iti tebhya iṣam ūrjam prāyacchat saiṣorg ṛtuṣu ca māseṣu ca nihitā dadataṃ vai te tam ayājayaṃs tasmād dadad yājyaḥ pratigṛhṇanto vai te tam ayājayaṃs tasmāt pratigṛhṇatā yājyam | [AB, 4, 25 1]
ubhaye rādhnuvanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃso yajante ca yājayanti ca | [AB, 4, 25 2]
te vā ima ṛtavaś ca māsāś ca gurava ivāmanyanta dvādaśāhe pratigṛhya te 'bruvan prajāpatiṃ yājaya no dvādaśāheneti sa tathety abravīt te vai dīkṣadhvam iti te pūrvapakṣāḥ pūrve 'dīkṣanta te pāpmānam apāhata tasmāt te diveva diveva hy apahatapāpmāno 'parapakṣā apare 'dīkṣanta te natarām pāpmānam apāhata tasmāt te tama iva tama iva hy anapahatapāpmānas tasmād evaṃ vidvān dīkṣamāṇeṣu pūrvaḥ pūrva eva didīkṣiṣeta | [AB, 4, 25 3]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 25 4]
sa vā ayam prajāpatiḥ saṃvatsara ṛtuṣu ca māseṣu ca pratyatiṣṭhat te vā ima ṛtavaś ca māsāś ca prajāpatāv eva saṃvatsare pratyatiṣṭhaṃs ta ete 'nyonyasmin pratiṣṭhitā evaṃ ha vāva sa ṛtviji pratitiṣṭhati yo dvādaśāhena yajate tasmād āhur na pāpaḥ puruṣo yājyo dvādaśāhena ned ayam mayi pratitiṣṭhād iti | [AB, 4, 25 5]
jyeṣṭhayajño vā eṣa yad dvādaśāhaḥ sa vai devānāṃ jyeṣṭho ya etenāgre 'yajata śreṣṭhayajño vā eṣa yad dvādaśāhaḥ sa vai devānāṃ śreṣṭho ya etenāgre 'yajata | [AB, 4, 25 6]
jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭho yajeta kalyāṇīha samā bhavati na pāpaḥ puruṣo yājyo dvādaśāhena ned ayam mayi pratitiṣṭhād iti | [AB, 4, 25 7]
indrāya vai devā jyaiṣṭhyāya śraiṣṭhyāya nātiṣṭhanta so 'bravīd bṛhaspatiṃ yājaya mā dvādaśāheneti tam ayājayat tato vai tasmai devā jyaiṣṭhyāya śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta | [AB, 4, 25 8]
tiṣṭhante 'smai svā jyaiṣṭhyāya śraiṣṭhyāya sam asmin svāḥ śreṣṭhatāyāṃ jānate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 25 9]
ūrdhvo vai prathamas tryahas tiryaṅ madhyamo 'rvāṅ uttamaḥ sa yad ūrdhvaḥ prathamas tryahas tasmād ayam agnir ūrdhva uddīpyata ūrdhvā hy etasya dig yat tiryaṅ madhyamas tasmād ayaṃ vāyus tiryaṅ pavate tiraścīr āpo vahanti tiraścī hy etasya dig yad arvāṅ uttamas tasmād asāv arvāṅ tapaty arvāṅ varṣaty arvāñci nakṣatrāṇy arvācī hy etasya dik samyañco vā ime lokāḥ samyañca ete tryahāḥ | [AB, 4, 25 10]
samyañco 'smā ime lokāḥ śriyai dīdyati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 25 11]
{AB, 4, 26}
dīkṣā vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat tāṃ vāsantikābhyām māsābhyām anvayuñjata tāṃ vāsantikābhyām māsābhyāṃ nodāpnuvaṃs tāṃ graiṣmābhyāṃ tāṃ vārṣikābhyāṃ tāṃ śāradābhyāṃ tāṃ haimantikābhyām māsābhyām anvayuñjata tāṃ haimantikābhyām māsābhyāṃ nodāpnuvaṃs tāṃ śaiśirābhyām māsābhyām anvayuñjata tāṃ śaiśirābhyām māsābhyām āpnuvan | [AB, 4, 26 1]
āpnoti yam īpsati nainaṃ dviṣann āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 26 2]
tasmād yaṃ sattriyā dīkṣopanamed etayor eva śaiśirayor māsayor āgatayor dīkṣeta sākṣād eva tad dīkṣāyām āgatāyām dīkṣate pratyakṣād dīkṣām parigṛhṇāti tasmād etayor eva śaiśirayor māsayor āgatayor ye caiva grāmyāḥ paśavo ye cāraṇyā aṇimānam eva tat paruṣimāṇaṃ niyanti dīkṣārūpam eva tad upaniplavante | [AB, 4, 26 3]
sa purastād dīkṣāyāḥ prājāpatyam paśum ālabhate | [AB, 4, 26 4]
tasya saptadaśa sāmidhenīr anubrūyāt saptadaśo vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai | [AB, 4, 26 5]
tasyāpriyo jāmadagnyo bhavanti | [AB, 4, 26 6]
tad āhur yad anyeṣu paśuṣu yathaṛṣy āpriyo bhavanty atha kasmād asmin sarveṣāṃ jāmadagnya eveti | [AB, 4, 26 7]
sarvarūpā vai jāmadagnyaḥ sarvasamṛddhāḥ sarvarūpa eṣa paśuḥ sarvasamṛddhas tad yajjāmadagnyo bhavanti sarvarūpatāyai sarvasamṛddhyai | [AB, 4, 26 8]
tasya vāyavyaḥ paśupuroﾱāśo bhavati | [AB, 4, 26 9]
tad āhur yad anyadevatya uta paśur bhavaty atha kasmād vāyavyaḥ paśupuroﾱāśaḥ kriyata iti | [AB, 4, 26 10]
prajāpatir vai yajño yajñasyāyātayāmatāyā iti brūyād yad u vāyavyas tena prajāpater naiti vāyur hy eva prajāpatiḥ | [AB, 4, 26 11]
tad uktam ṛṣiṇā pavamānaḥ prajāpatir iti | [AB, 4, 26 12]
satram u cet saṃnyupyāgnīn yajeran sarve dīkṣeran sarve sunuyur vasantam abhyudavasyaty ūrg vai vasanta iṣam eva tad ūrjam abhyudavasyati | [AB, 4, 26 13]
{AB, 4, 27}
chandāṃsi vā anyonyasyāyatanam abhyadhyāyan gāyatrī triṣṭubhaś ca jagatyai cāyatanam abhyadhyāyat triṣṭub gāyatryai ca jagatyai ca jagatī gāyatryai ca triṣṭubhaś ca tato vā etam prajāpatir vyūﾱhachandasaṃ dvādaśāham apaśyat tam āharat tenāyajata tena sa sarvān kāmāṃś chandāṃsy agamayat | [AB, 4, 27 1]
sarvān kāmān gacchati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 27 2]
chandāṃsi vyūhaty ayātayāmatāyai | [AB, 4, 27 3]
chandāṃsy eva vyūhati tad yathādo 'śvair vānaﾱudbhir vānyair anyair aśrāntatarair aśrāntatarair upavimokaṃ yānty evam evaitac chandobhir anyair anyair aśrāntatarair aśrāntatarair upavimokaṃ svargaṃ lokam yanti yacchandāṃsi vyūhati | [AB, 4, 27 4]
imau vai lokau sahāstāṃ tau vyaitāṃ nāvarṣan na samatapat te pañcajanā na samajānata tau devāḥ samanayaṃs tau saṃyantāv etaṃ devavivāhaṃ vyavahetāṃ rathaṃtareṇaiveyam amūṃ jinvati bṛhatāsāv imām | [AB, 4, 27 5]
naudhasenaiveyam amūṃ jinvati śyaitenāsāv imāṃ dhūmenaiveyam amūṃ jinvati vṛṣṭyāsāv imāṃ devayajanam eveyam amuṣyām adadhāt paśūn asāv asyām | [AB, 4, 27 6]
etad vā iyam amuṣyāṃ devayajanam adadhād yad etaccandramasi kṛṣṇam iva | [AB, 4, 27 7]
tasmād āpūryamāṇapakṣeṣu yajanta etad evopepsantaḥ | [AB, 4, 27 8]
ūṣān asāv asyāṃ taddhāpi turaḥ kāvaṣeya uvācoṣaḥ poṣo janamejayaketi tasmāddhāpyetarhi gavyam mīmāṃsamānāḥ pṛcchanti santi tatroṣāḥ iti ūṣo hi poṣo 'sau vai loka imaṃ lokam abhiparyāvartata | [AB, 4, 27 9]
tato vai dyāvāpṛthivī abhavatāṃ na dyāvāntarikṣān nāntarikṣād bhūmiḥ | [AB, 4, 27 10]
{AB, 4, 28}
bṛhac ca vā idam agre rathaṃtaraṃ cāstāṃ vāk ca vai tan manaś cāstāṃ vāg vai rathaṃtaram mano bṛhat tad bṛhat pūrvaṃ sasṛjānaṃ rathaṃtaram atyamanyata tad rathaṃtaraṃ garbham adhatta tad vairūpam asṛjata | [AB, 4, 28 1]
te dve bhūtvā rathaṃtaraṃ ca vairūpaṃ ca bṛhad atyamanyetāṃ tad bṛhad garbham adhatta tad vairājam asṛjata | [AB, 4, 28 2]
te dve bhūtvā bṛhac ca vairājaṃ ca rathaṃtaraṃ ca vairūpam cātyamanyetāṃ tad rathaṃtaraṃ garbham adhatta tacchākvaram asṛjata | [AB, 4, 28 3]
tāni trīṇi bhūtvā rathaṃtaraṃ ca vairūpam ca śākvaraṃ ca bṛhac ca vairājaṃ cātyamanyanta tad bṛhad garbham adhatta tad raivatam asṛjata | [AB, 4, 28 4]
tāni trīṇy anyāni trīṇy anyāni ṣaṭ pṛṣṭhāny āsan | [AB, 4, 28 5]
tāni ha tarhi trīṇi chandāṃsi ṣaḍ pṛṣṭhāni na udāpnuvan | [AB, 4, 28 637276_1]
sā gāyatrī garbham adhatta | [AB, 4, 28 637276_2]
sā anuṣṭubham asṛjata | [AB, 4, 28 637276_3]
tasyai janatāyai kalpate yatraivam etāṃ chandasāṃ ca pṛṣṭhānāṃ ca kﾱptiṃ vidvān dīkṣate dīkṣate | [AB, 4, 28 7]
{AB, 4, 29}
agnir vai devatā prathamam ahar vahati trivṛt stomo rathaṃtaraṃ sāma gāyatrī chandaḥ | [AB, 4, 29 1]
yathādevatam enena yathāstomaṃ yathāsāma yathāchandasaṃ rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 29 2]
yad vā eti ca preti ca tat prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ yad yuktavad yad rathavad yad āśumad yat pibavad yat prathame pade devatā nirucyate yad ayaṃ loko 'bhyudito yad rāthaṃtaraṃ yad gāyatraṃ yat kariṣyad etāni vai prathamasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 4, 29 3]
upaprayanto adhvaram iti prathamasyāhna ājyam bhavati | [AB, 4, 29 4]
preti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 5]
vāyav ā yāhi darśateti praugam eti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 6]
ā tvā rathaṃ yathotaya idaṃ vaso sutam andha iti marutvatīyasya pratipadanucarau rathavac ca pibavac ca prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 7]
indra nedīya ed ihītīndranihavaḥ pragāthaḥ prathame pade devatā nirucyate prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 8]
praitu brahmaṇaspatir iti brāhmaṇaspatyaḥ preti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 9]
agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apa iti dhāyyāḥ prathameṣu padeṣu devatā nirucyante prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 10]
pra vā indrāya bṛhata iti marutvatīyaḥ pragāthaḥ preti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 11]
ā yātv indro 'vasa upa na iti sūktam eti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 12]
abhi tvā śūra nonumo 'bhi tvā pūrvapītaya iti rathaṃtaram pṛṣṭham bhavati rāthaṃtare 'hani prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 13]
yad vāvāna purutamam purāṣāﾱ iti dhāyyā vṛtrahendro nāmāny aprā ity eti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 14]
pibā sutasya rasina iti sāmapragāthaḥ pibavān prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 29 15]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyam purastāt sūktasya śaṃsati svastyayanaṃ vai tārkṣyaḥ svastitāyai | [AB, 4, 29 16]
svastyayanam eva tat kurute svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 29 17]
{AB, 4, 30}
ā na indro dūrād ā na āsād iti sūktam eti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 1]
sampātau bhavato niṣkevalyamarutvatīyayor nividdhāne vāmadevo vā imāṃllokān apaśyat tān sampātaiḥ samapatad yat sampātaiḥ samapatat tat sampātānāṃ sampātatvaṃ tad yat sampātau prathame 'hani śaṃsati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai sampattyai saṃgatyai | [AB, 4, 30 2]
tat savitur vṛṇīmahe 'dyā no deva savitar iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau rāthaṃtare 'hani prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 3]
yuñjate mana uta yuñjate dhiya iti sāvitraṃ yuktavat prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 4]
pra dyāvā yajñaiḥ pṛthivī ṛtāvṛdheti dyāvāpṛthivīyam preti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 5]
iheha vo manasā bandhutā nara ity ārbhavaṃ yad vā eti ca preti ca tat prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ tad yat preti sarvam abhaviṣyat praiṣyann evāsmāllokād yajamānā iti tad yad iheha vo manasā bandhutā nara ity ārbhavam prathame 'hani śaṃsaty ayaṃ vai loka ihehāsminn evaināṃs tal loke ramayati | [AB, 4, 30 6]
devān huve bṛhacchravasaḥ svastaya iti vaiśvadevam prathame pade devatā nirucyante prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 7]
mahāntaṃ vā ete 'dhvānam eṣyanto bhavanti ye saṃvatsaraṃ vā dvādaśāhaṃ vāsate tad yad devān huve bṛhacchravasaḥ svastaya iti vaiśvadevam prathame 'hani śaṃsati svastitāyai | [AB, 4, 30 8]
svastyayanam eva tat kurute svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda yeṣāṃ caivaṃ vidvān etaddhotā devān huve bṛhacchravasaḥ svastaya iti vaiśvadevam prathame 'hani śaṃsati | [AB, 4, 30 9]
vaiśvānarāya pṛthupājase vipa ity āgnimārutasya pratipat prathame pade devatā nirucyate prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 10]
pratvakṣaso pratavaso virapśina iti mārutam preti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 11]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyām purastāt sūktasya śaṃsati svastyayanaṃ vai jātavedasyāḥ svastitāyai | [AB, 4, 30 12]
svastyayanam eva tat kurute svasti saṃvatsarasya pāram aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 30 13]
pra tavyasīṃ navyasīṃ dhītim agnaya iti jātavedasyam preti prathame 'hani prathamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 30 14]
samānam āgnimārutam bhavati yac cāgniṣṭome yad vai yajñe samānaṃ kriyate tat prajā anusamananti tasmāt samānam āgnimārutam bhavati | [AB, 4, 30 15]
{AB, 4, 31}
indro vai devatā dvitīyam ahar vahati pañcadaśaḥ stomo bṛhat sāma triṣṭup chandaḥ | [AB, 4, 31 1]
yathādevatam enena yathāstomaṃ yathāsāma yathāchandasaṃ rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 4, 31 2]
yad vai neti na preti yat sthitaṃ tad dvitīyasyāhno rūpaṃ yad ūrdhvavad yat prativad yad antarvad yad vṛṣaṇvad yad vṛdhanvad yan madhyame pade devatā nirucyate yad antarikṣam abhyuditaṃ yad bārhataṃ yat traiṣṭubhaṃ yat kurvad etāni vai dvitīyasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 4, 31 3]
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha iti dvitīyasyāhna ājyam bhavati kurvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 4]
vāyo ye te sahasriṇa iti praugaṃ sutaḥ soma ṛtāvṛdheti vṛdhanvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 5]
viśvānarasya vas patim indra it somapā eka iti marutvatīyasya pratipadanucarau vṛdhanvaccāntarvacca dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 6]
indra nedīya ed ihītyacyutaḥ pragātha ut tiṣṭha brahmaṇaspata iti brāhmaṇaspatya ūrdhvavān dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 7]
agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apa iti dhāyyā acyutā | [AB, 4, 31 8]
bṛhad indrāya gāyateti marutvatīyaḥ pragātho yena jyotir ajanayann ṛtāvṛdha iti vṛdhanvān dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 9]
indra somaṃ somapate pibemam iti sūktam sajoṣā rudrais tṛpad ā vṛṣasveti vṛṣaṇvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 10]
tvām iddhi havāmahe tvaṃ hy ehi cerava iti bṛhatpṛṣṭham bhavati bārhate 'hani dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 11]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 4, 31 12]
ubhayaṃ śṛṇavac ca na iti sāmapragātho yac cedam adya yad u ca hya āsīd iti bārhate 'hani dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 31 13]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 4, 31 14]
{AB, 4, 32}
yā ta ūtir avamā yā parameti sūktaṃ jahi vṛṣṇyāni kṛṇuhī parāca iti vṛṣaṇvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 1]
viśvo devasya netus tat savitur vareṇyam ā viśvadevaṃ satpatim iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau bārhate 'hani dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 2]
ud u ṣya devaḥ savitā hiraṇyayeti sāvitram ūrdhvavad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 3]
te hi dyāvāpṛthivī viśvaśambhuveti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ sujanmanī dhiṣaṇe antar īyata ity antarvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 4]
takṣan rathaṃ suvṛtaṃ vidmanāpasa ity ārbhavaṃ takṣan harī indravāhā vṛṣaṇvasū iti vṛṣaṇvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 5]
yajñasya vo rathyaṃ viśpatiṃ viśām iti vaiśvadevaṃ vṛṣā ketur yajato dyām aśāyateti vṛṣaṇvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 6]
tad u śāryātam aṅgiraso vai svargāya lokāya satram āsata te ha sma dvitīyaṃ dvitīyam evāhar āgatya muhyanti tān vā etac chāryāto mānavo dvitīye 'hani sūktam aśaṃsayat tato vai te pra yajñam ajānan pra svargaṃ lokaṃ tad yad etat sūktaṃ dvitīye 'hani śaṃsati yajñasya prajñātyai svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai | [AB, 4, 32 7]
pṛkṣasya vṛṣṇo aruṣasya nū saha ity āgnimārutasya pratipad vṛṣaṇvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 8]
vṛṣṇe śardhāya sumakhāya vedhasa iti mārutaṃ vṛṣaṇvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 9]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 4, 32 10]
yajñena vardhata jātavedasam iti jātavedasyaṃ vṛdhanvad dvitīye 'hani dvitīyasyāhno rūpam ahno rūpam | [AB, 4, 32 11]
{AB, 5, 1}
viśve vai devā devatās tṛtīyam ahar vahanti saptadaśaḥ stomo vairūpaṃ sāma jagatī chandaḥ | [AB, 5, 1 1]
yathādevatam enena yathāstomaṃ yathāsāma yathāchandasaṃ rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 1 2]
yad vai samānodarkaṃ tat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ yad aśvavad yad antavad yat punarāvṛttaṃ yat punarninṛttaṃ yad ratavad yat paryastavad yat trivad yad antarūpaṃ yad uttame pade devatā nirucyate yad asau loko 'bhyudito yad vairūpaṃ yaj jāgataṃ yat kṛtam etāni vai tṛtīyasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 1 3]
yukṣvā hi devahūtamāṁ aśvāṁ agne rathīr iveti tṛtīyasyāhna ājyam bhavati | [AB, 5, 1 4]
devā vai tṛtīyenāhnā svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tān asurā rakṣāṃsy anvavārayanta te virūpā bhavata virūpā bhavateti bhavanta āyaṃs te yad virūpā bhavata virūpā bhavateti bhavanta āyaṃs tad vairūpaṃ sāmābhavat tad vairūpasya vairūpatvam | [AB, 5, 1 5]
virūpaḥ pāpmanā bhūtvā pāpmānam apahate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 1 6]
tān ha smānv evāgacchanti sam eva sṛjyante tān aśvā bhūtvā padbhir apāghnata yad aśvā bhūtvā padbhir apāghnata tad aśvānām aśvatvam | [AB, 5, 1 7]
aśnute yad yat kāmayate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 1 8]
tasmād aśvaḥ paśūnāṃ javiṣṭhas tasmād aśvaḥ pratyaṅ padā hinasti | [AB, 5, 1 9]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 1 10]
tasmād etad aśvavad ājyam bhavati tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 11]
vāyav ā yāhi vītaye vāyo yāhi śivā diva indraś ca vāyav eṣāṃ sutānām ā mitre varuṇe vayam aśvināv eha gacchatam ā yāhy adribhiḥ sutaṃ sajūr viśvebhir devebhir uta naḥ priyā priyāsv ity auṣṇiham praugaṃ samānodarkaṃ tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 12]
taṃ tam id rādhase mahe traya indrasya somā iti marutvatīyasya pratipadanucarau ninṛttavat trivat tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 13]
indra nedīya ed ihīty acyutaḥ pragāthaḥ pra nūnam brahmaṇaspatir iti brāhmaṇaspatyo ninṛttavāṃs tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 14]
agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty āpa iti dhāyyā acyutāḥ | [AB, 5, 1 15]
nakiḥ sudāso ratham pary āsa na rīramad iti marutvatīyaḥ pragāthaḥ paryastavāṃs tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 16]
try aryamā manuṣo devatāteti sūktaṃ trivat tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 17]
yad dyāva indra te śataṃ yad indra yāvatas tvam iti vairūpam pṛṣṭham bhavati rāthaṃtare 'hani tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 18]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 5, 1 19]
abhi tvā śūra nonuma iti rathaṃtarasya yonim anu nivartayati rāthaṃtaraṃ hy etad ahar āyatanena | [AB, 5, 1 20]
indra tridhātu śaraṇam iti sāmapragāthas trivāṃs tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 1 21]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 1 22]
{AB, 5, 2}
yo jāta eva prathamo manasvān iti sūktaṃ samānodarkaṃ tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 1]
tad u sajanīyam etad vā indrasyendriyaṃ yat sajanīyam etasmin vai śasyamāna indram indriyam āviśati | [AB, 5, 2 2]
taddhāpyāhuś chandogās tṛtīye 'hani bahvṛcā indrasyendriyam śaṃsantīti | [AB, 5, 2 3]
tad u gārtsamadam etena vai gṛtsamada indrasya priyaṃ dhāmopāgacchat sa paramaṃ lokam ajayat | [AB, 5, 2 4]
upendrasya priyaṃ dhāma gacchati jayati paramaṃ lokaṃ ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 2 5]
tat savitur vṛṇīmahe 'dyā no deva savitar iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau rāthaṃtare 'hani tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 6]
tad devasya savitur vāryam mahad iti sāvitram | [AB, 5, 2 7]
anto vai mahad antas tṛtīyam ahas tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 8]
ghṛtena dyāvāpṛthivī abhīvṛte iti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ ghṛtaśriyā ghṛtapṛcā ghṛtāvṛdheti punarāvṛttam punarninṛttaṃ tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 9]
anaśvo jāto anabhīśur ukthya ity ārbhavam rathas tricakra iti trivat tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 10]
parāvato ye didhiṣanta āpyam iti vaiśvadevam anto vai parāvato 'ntas tṛtīyam ahas tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 11]
tad u gāyam etena vai gayaḥ plāto viśveṣāṃ devānām priyaṃ dhāmopāgacchat sa paramaṃ lokam ajayat | [AB, 5, 2 12]
upa viśveṣāṃ devānām priyaṃ dhāma gacchati jayati paramaṃ lokaṃ ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 2 13]
vaiśvānarāya dhiṣaṇām ṛtāvṛdha ity āgnimārutasya pratipad anto vai dhiṣaṇāntas tṛtīyam ahas tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 14]
dhārāvarā maruto dhṛṣṇvojasa iti mārutam bahvabhivyāhṛtyam anto vai bahv antas tṛtīyam ahas tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 2 15]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 2 16]
tvam agne prathamo aṅgirā ṛṣir iti jātavedasyam purastādudarkaṃ tṛtīye 'hani tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tvaṃ tvam ity uttaraṃ tryaham abhivadati saṃtatyai | [AB, 5, 2 17]
saṃtatais tryahair avyavacchinnair yanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃso yanti | [AB, 5, 2 18]
{AB, 5, 3}
āpyante vai stomā āpyante chandāṃsi tṛtīye 'hany etad eva tata ucchiṣyate vāg ity eva tad etad akṣaraṃ tryakṣaraṃ vāg ity ekam akṣaram akṣaram iti tryakṣaram | [AB, 5, 3 1]
sa evaiṣa uttaras tryaho vāg ekaṃ gaur ekaṃ dyaur ekam | [AB, 5, 3 2]
tato vai vāg eva caturtham ahar vahati | [AB, 5, 3 3]
tad yac caturtham ahar nyūṅkhayanty etad eva tad akṣaram abhyāyacchanty etad vardhayanty etat prabibhāvayiṣanti caturthasyāhna udyatyai | [AB, 5, 3 4]
annaṃ vai nyūṅkho yadelavā abhigeṣṇāś caranty athānnādyam prajāyate tad yaccaturtham ahar nyūṅkhayanty annam eva tat prajanayanty annādyasya prajātyai tasmāccaturtham ahar jātavad bhavati | [AB, 5, 3 5]
caturakṣareṇa nyūṅkhayed ity āhuś catuṣpādā vai paśavaḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 3 6]
tryakṣareṇa nyūṅkhayed ity āhus trayo vā ime trivṛto lokā eṣām eva lokānām abhijityai | [AB, 5, 3 7]
ekākṣareṇa nyūṅkhayed iti ha smāha lāṅgalāyano brahmā maudgalya ekākṣarā vai vāg eṣa vāva samprati nyūṅkhaṃ nyūṅkhayati ya ekākṣareṇa nyūṅkhayatīti | [AB, 5, 3 8]
dvyakṣareṇaiva nyūṅkhayet pratiṣṭhāyā eva dvipratiṣṭho vai puruṣaś catuṣpādāḥ paśavo yajamānam eva tad dvipratiṣṭhaṃ catuṣpātsu paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmād dvyakṣareṇaiva nyūṅkhayet | [AB, 5, 3 9]
mukhataḥ prātaranuvāke nyūṅkhayati mukhato vai prajā annam adanti mukhata eva tad annādyasya yajamānaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 3 10]
madhyata ājye nyūṅkhayati madhyato vai prajā annaṃ dhinoti madhyata eva tad annādyasya yajamānaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 3 11]
mukhato madhyaṃdine nyūṅkhayati mukhato vai prajā annam adanti mukhata eva tad annādyasya yajamānaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 3 12]
tad ubhayato nyūṅkham parigṛhṇāti savanābhyām annādyasya parigṛhītyai | [AB, 5, 3 13]
{AB, 5, 4}
vāg vai devatā caturtham ahar vahaty ekaviṃśaḥ stomo vairājaṃ sāmānuṣṭup chando yathādevatam enena yathāstomaṃ yathāsāma yathāchandasaṃ rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 4 1]
yad vā eti ca preti ca taccaturthasyāhno rūpaṃ yaddhyeva prathamam ahas tad etat punar yac caturthaṃ yad yuktavad yad rathavad yad āśumad yat pibavad yat prathame pade devatā nirucyate yad ayaṃ loko 'bhyudito yaj jātavad yaddhavavad yacchukravad yad vāco rūpaṃ yad vaimadaṃ yad viriphitaṃ yad vichandā yad ūnātiriktaṃ yad vairājaṃ yad ānuṣṭubhaṃ yat kariṣyad yat prathamasyāhno rūpam etāni vai caturthasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 4 2]
āgniṃ na svavṛktibhir iti caturthasyāhna ājyam bhavati vaimadaṃ viriphitaṃ viriphitasya ṛṣeś caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 3]
aṣṭarcam pāṅktam pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 4 4]
tā u daśa jagatyo jagatprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahas tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 5]
tā u pañcadaśānuṣṭubha ānuṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahas tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 6]
tā u viṃśatir gāyatryaḥ punaḥ prāyaṇīyaṃ hy etad ahas tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 7]
tad etad astutam aśastam ayātayāma sūktaṃ yajña eva sākṣāt tad yad etac caturthasyāhna ājyam bhavati yajñād eva tad yajñaṃ tanvate vācam eva tat punar upayanti saṃtatyai | [AB, 5, 4 8]
saṃtatais tryahair avyavacchinnair yanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃso yanti | [AB, 5, 4 9]
vāyo śukro ayāmi te vihi hotrā avītā vāyo śataṃ harīṇām indraś ca vāyav eṣāṃ somānām ā cikitāna sukratū ā no viśvābhir ūtibhis tyam u vo aprahaṇam apa tyaṃ vṛjinaṃ ripum ambitame nadītama ity ānuṣṭubham praugam eti ca preti ca śukravac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 10]
taṃ tvā yajñebhir īmaha iti marutvatīyasya pratipad īmaha ity abhyāyāmyam ivaitad ahas tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 11]
idaṃ vaso sutam andha indra nedīya ed ihi praitu brahmaṇaspatir agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apaḥ pra va indrāya bṛhata iti prathamenāhnā samāna ātānaś caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 12]
śrudhī havam indra mā riṣaṇya iti sūktaṃ havavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 13]
marutvān indra vṛṣabho raṇayeti sūktam ugraṃ sahodām iha taṃ huvemeti havavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 14]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 4 15]
imaṃ nu māyinaṃ huva iti paryāso havavāṃś caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 16]
tā u gāyatryo gāyatryo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti | [AB, 5, 4 17]
tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmād gāyatrīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 4 18]
pibā somam indra mandatu tvā śrudhī havaṃ vipipānasyādrer iti vairājam pṛṣṭham bhavati bārhate 'hani caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 19]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 5, 4 20]
tvām iddhi havāmaha iti bṛhato yonim anu nivartayati bārhataṃ hy etad ahar āyatanena | [AB, 5, 4 21]
tvam indra pratūrtiṣv iti sāmapragātho 'śastihā janiteti jātavāṃś caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 4 22]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 4 23]
{AB, 5, 5}
kuha śruta indraḥ kasminn adyeti sūktaṃ vaimadaṃ viriphitaṃ viriphitasya ṛṣeś caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 1]
yudhmasya te vṛṣabhasya svarāja iti sūktam ugraṃ gabhīraṃ januṣābhy ugram iti jātavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 2]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 5 3]
tyam u vaḥ satrāsāham iti paryāso viśvāsu gīrṣv āyatam ity abhyāyāmyam ivaitad ahas tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 4]
tā u gāyatryo gāyatryo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinam vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmād gāyatrīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 5 5]
viśvo devasya netus tat savitur vareṇyam ā viśvadevaṃ satpatim iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau bārhate 'hani caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 6]
ā devo yātu savitā suratna iti sāvitram eti caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 7]
pra dyāvā yajñaiḥ pṛthivī namobhir iti dyāvāpṛthivīyam preti caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 8]
pra ṛbhubhyo dūtam iva vācam iṣya ity ārbhavam preti ca vācam iṣya iti ca caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 9]
pra śukraitu devī manīṣeti vaiśvadevam preti ca śukravac ca caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 10]
tā u vichandasaḥ santi dvipadāḥ santi catuṣpadās tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 11]
vaiśvānarasya sumatau syāmety āgnimārutasya pratipad ito jāta iti jātavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 12]
ka īṃ vyaktā naraḥ sanīﾱā iti mārutaṃ nakir hy eṣāṃ janūṃṣi vedeti jātavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 13]
tā u vichandasaḥ santi dvipadāḥ santi catuṣpadās tena caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 14]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 5 15]
agniṃ naro dīdhitibhir araṇyor iti jātavedasyaṃ hastacyutī janayanteti jātavac caturthe 'hani caturthasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 16]
tā u vichandasaḥ santi virājaḥ santi triṣṭubhas tena caturthasyāhno rūpam ahno rūpam | [AB, 5, 5 17]
{AB, 5, 6}
gaur vai devatā pañcamam ahar vahati triṇavaḥ stomaḥ śākvaraṃ sāma paṅktiś chando yathādevatam enena yathāstomaṃ yathāsāma yathāchandasaṃ rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 6 1]
yad vai neti na preti yat sthitaṃ tat pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 2]
yaddhyeva dvitīyam ahas tad etat punar yat pañcamam | [AB, 5, 6 3]
yad ūrdhvavad yat prativad yad antarvad yad vṛṣaṇvad yad vṛdhanvad yan madhyame pade devatā nirucyate yad antarikṣam abhyuditam | [AB, 5, 6 4]
yad dugdhavad yad ūdhavad yad dhenumad yat pṛśnimad yan madvad yat paśurūpaṃ yad adhyāsavad vikṣudrā iva hi paśavo yaj jāgataṃ jāgatā hi paśavo yad bārhatam bārhatā hi paśavo yat pāṅktam pāṅktā hi paśavo yad vāmaṃ vāmam hi paśavo yaddhaviṣmaddhavir hi paśavo yad vapuṣmad vapur hi paśavo yacchākvaraṃ yat pāṅktaṃ yat kurvad yad dvitīyasyāhno rūpam etāni vai pañcamasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 6 5]
imam ū ṣu vo atithim uṣarbudham iti pañcamasyāhna ājyam bhavati jāgatam adhyāsavat paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 6]
ā no yajñaṃ divispṛśam ā no vāyo mahe tane rathena pṛthupājasā bahavaḥ sūracakṣasa imā u vāṃ diviṣṭayaḥ pibā sutasya rasino devaṃ devaṃ vo 'vase devaṃ devam bṛhad u gāyiṣe vaca iti bārhatam praugam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 7]
yat pāñcajanyayā viśeti marutvatīyasya pratipat pāñcajanyayeti pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 8]
indra it somapā eka indra nedīya ed ihy ut tiṣṭha brahmaṇaspate 'gnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apo bṛhad indrāya gāyateti dvitīyenāhnā samāna ātānaḥ pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 9]
avitāsi sunvato vṛktabarhiṣa iti sūktam madvat pāṅktam pañcapadam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 10]
itthā hi soma in mada iti sūktam madvat pāṅktam pañcapadam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 11]
indra piba tubhyaṃ suto madāyeti sūktam madvat traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 6 12]
marutvāṁ indra mīḍhva iti paryāso neti na preti pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 6 13]
tā u gāyatryo gāyatryo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmād gāyatrīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 6 14]
{AB, 5, 7}
mahānāmnīṣv atra stuvate śākvareṇa sāmnā rāthaṃtare 'hani pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 7 1]
indro vā etābhir mahān ātmānaṃ niramimīta tasmān mahānāmnyo 'tho ime vai lokā mahānāmnya ime mahāntaḥ | [AB, 5, 7 2]
imān vai lokān prajāpatiḥ sṛṣṭvedaṃ sarvam aśaknod yad idam kiṃca yad imāṃllokān prajāpatiḥ sṛṣṭvedaṃ sarvam aśaknod yad idaṃ kiṃca tac chakvaryo 'bhavaṃs tac chakvarīṇāṃ śakvarītvam | [AB, 5, 7 3]
tā ūrdhvāḥ sīmno 'bhyasṛjata yad ūrdhvāḥ sīmno 'bhyasṛjata tat simā abhavaṃs tat simānāṃ simātvam | [AB, 5, 7 4]
svādor itthā viṣūvata upa no haribhiḥ sutam indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity anurūpo vṛṣaṇvān pṛśnimān madvān vṛdhanvān pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 7 5]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 5, 7 6]
abhi tvā śūra nonuma iti rathaṃtarasya yonim anu nivartayati rāthaṃtaraṃ hy etad ahar āyatanena | [AB, 5, 7 7]
mo ṣu tvā vāghataś caneti sāmapragātho 'dhyāsavān paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 7 8]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 7 9]
{AB, 5, 8}
predam brahma vṛtratūryeṣv āvitheti sūktam pāṅktam pañcapadam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 1]
indro madāya vāvṛdha iti sūktam madvat pāṅktam pañcapadam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 2]
satrā madāsas tava viśvajanyā iti sūktam madvat traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 8 3]
tam indraṃ vājayāmasīti paryāsaḥ sa vṛṣā vṛṣabho bhuvad iti paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 4]
tā u gāyatryo gāyatryo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmād gāyatrīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 8 5]
tat savitur vṛṇīmahe 'dyā no deva savitar iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau rāthaṃtare 'hani pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 6]
ud u ṣya devaḥ savitā damūnā iti sāvitram ā dāśuṣe suvati bhūri vāmam iti vāmam paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 7]
mahī dyāvāpṛthivī iha jyeṣṭhe iti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ ruvaddhokṣeti paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 8]
ṛbhur vibhvā vāja indro no acchety ārbhavaṃ vājo vai paśavaḥ paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 9]
stuṣe janaṃ suvrataṃ navyasībhir iti vaiśvadevam adhyāsavat paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 10]
haviṣpāntam ajaraṃ svarvidīty āgnimārutasya pratipaddhaviṣmat pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 11]
vapur nu tac cikituṣe cid astv iti mārutaṃ vapuṣmat pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 12]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 8 13]
agnir hotā gṛhapatiḥ sa rājeti jātavedasyam adhyāsavat paśurūpam pañcame 'hani pañcamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 8 14]
{AB, 5, 9}
devakṣetraṃ vā etad yat ṣaṣṭham ahar devakṣetraṃ vā eta āgacchanti ye ṣaṣṭham ahar āgacchanti | [AB, 5, 9 1]
na vai devā anyonyasya gṛhe vasanti nartur ṛtor gṛhe vasatīty āhus tad yathāyatham ṛtvija ṛtuyājān yajanty asaṃpradāyaṃ tad yathartv ṛtūn kalpayanti yathāyathaṃ janatāḥ | [AB, 5, 9 2]
tad āhur nartupraiṣaiḥ preṣitavyaṃ nartupraiṣair vaṣaṭkṛtyaṃ vāg vā ṛtupraiṣā āpyate vai vāk ṣaṣṭhe 'hanīti | [AB, 5, 9 3]
yad ṛtupraiṣaiḥ preṣyeyur yad ṛtupraiṣair vaṣaṭkuryur vācam eva tad āptāṃ śrāntām ṛkṇavahīṃ vaharāviṇīm ṛccheyuḥ | [AB, 5, 9 4]
yad v ebhir na preṣyeyur yad v ebhir na vaṣaṭkuryur acyutād yajñasya cyaveran yajñāt prāṇāt prajāpateḥ paśubhyo jihmā īyuḥ | [AB, 5, 9 5]
tasmād ṛgmebhya evādhi preṣitavyam ṛgmebhyo 'dhi vaṣaṭkṛtyaṃ tan na vācam āptāṃ śrāntām ṛkṇavahīṃ vaharāviṇīm ṛcchanti nācyutād yajñasya cyavante na yajñāt prāṇāt prajāpateḥ paśubhyo jihmā yanti | [AB, 5, 9 6]
{AB, 5, 10}
pārucchepīr upadadhati pūrvayoḥ savanayoḥ purastāt prasthitayājyānāṃ rohitaṃ vai nāmaitac chando yat pārucchepam etena vā indraḥ sapta svargāṃllokān arohat | [AB, 5, 10 1]
rohati sapta svargāṃllokān ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 10 2]
tad āhur yat pañcapadā eva pañcamasyāhno rūpaṃ ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyātha kasmāt saptapadāḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hañchasyanta iti | [AB, 5, 10 3]
ṣaḍbhir eva padaiḥ ṣaṣṭham ahar āpnuvanty apacchidyevaitad ahar yat saptamaṃ tad eva saptamena padenābhyārabhya vasanti vācam eva tat punar upayanti saṃtatyai | [AB, 5, 10 4]
saṃtatais tryahair avyavacchinnair yanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃso yanti | [AB, 5, 10 5]
{AB, 5, 11}
devāsurā vā eṣu lokeṣu samayatanta te vai devāḥ ṣaṣṭhenaivāhnaibhyo lokebhyo 'surān prāṇudanta teṣāṃ yāny antarhastīnāni vasūny āsaṃs tāny ādāya samudram praupyanta ta etenaiva chandasānuhāyāntarhastīnāni vasūny ādadata tad yad etat padam punaḥpadaṃ sa evāṅkuśa āsañjanāya | [AB, 5, 11 1]
adviṣato vasu datte nir enam ebhyaḥ sarvebhyo lokebhyo nudate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 11 2]
{AB, 5, 12}
dyaur vai devatā ṣaṣṭham ahar vahati trayastriṃśaḥ stomo raivataṃ sāmātichandāś chando yathādevatam enena yathāstomaṃ yathāsāma yathāchandasaṃ rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 12 1]
yad vai samānodarkaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ yaddhyeva tṛtīyam ahas tad etat punar yat ṣaṣṭhaṃ yad aśvavad yad antavad yat punarāvṛttaṃ yat punarninṛttaṃ yad ratavad yat paryastavad yat trivad yad antarūpaṃ yad uttame pade devatā nirucyate yad asau loko 'bhyuditaḥ | [AB, 5, 12 2]
yat pārucchepaṃ yat saptapadaṃ yan nārāśaṃsaṃ yan nābhānediṣṭhaṃ yad raivataṃ yad atichandā yat kṛtaṃ yat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ etāni vai ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 12 3]
ayaṃ jāyata manuṣo dharīmaṇīti ṣaṣṭhasyāhna ājyam bhavati pārucchepam atichandāḥ saptapadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 4]
stīrṇam barhir upa no yāhi vītaya ā vāṃ ratho niyutvān vakṣad avase suṣumā yātam adribhir yuvāṃ stomebhir devayanto aśvinā var maha indra vṛṣann indrāstu śrauṣaﾱ o ṣū ṇo agne śṛṇuhi tvam īﾱito ye devāso divy ekādaśa stheyam adadād rabhasam ṛṇacyutam iti praugam pārucchepam atichandāḥ saptapadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 5]
sa pūrvyo mahānām iti marutvatīyasya pratipad anto vai mahad antaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 6]
traya indrasya somā indra nedīya ed ihi pra nūnam brahmaṇaspatir agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apo nakiḥ sudāso ratham iti tṛtīyenāhnā samāna ātānaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 7]
yaṃ tvaṃ ratham indra medhasātaya iti sūktam pārucchepam atichandāḥ saptapadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 8]
sa yo vṛṣā vṛṣṇyebhiḥ samokā iti sūktaṃ samānodarkaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 9]
indra marutva iha pāhi somam iti sūktaṃ tebhiḥ sākam pibatu vṛtrakhāda ity anto vai khādo 'ntaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 10]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 12 11]
ayaṃ ha yena vā idam iti paryāsaḥ svar marutvatā jitam ity anto vai jitam antaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 12]
tā u gāyatryo gāyatryo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhīyate tasmād gāyatrīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 12 13]
revatīr naḥ sadhamāde revāṁ id revata stoteti raivatam pṛṣṭham bhavati bārhate 'hani ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 14]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 5, 12 15]
tvām iddhi havāmaha iti bṛhato yonim anu nivartayati bārhataṃ hy etad ahar āyatanena | [AB, 5, 12 16]
indram id devatātaya iti sāmapragātho ninṛttavān ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 12 17]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 12 18]
{AB, 5, 13}
endra yāhy upa naḥ parāvata iti sūktam pārucchepam atichandāḥ saptapadaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 1]
pra ghā nv asya mahato mahānīti sūktaṃ samānodarkaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 2]
abhūr eko rayipate rayīṇām iti sūktaṃ ratham ā tiṣṭha tuvinṛmṇa bhīmam ity anto vai sthitam antaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 3]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 13 4]
upa no haribhiḥ sutam iti paryāsaḥ samānodarkaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 5]
tā u gāyatryo gāyatryo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhīyate tasmād gāyatrīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 13 6]
abhi tyaṃ devaṃ savitāram oṇyor iti vaiśvadevasya pratipad atichandāḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 7]
tat savitur vareṇyaṃ doṣo āgād ity anucaro 'nto vai gatam antaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 8]
ud u ṣya devaḥ savitā savāyeti sāvitraṃ śaśvattamaṃ tadapā vahnir asthād ity anto vai sthitam antaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 9]
katarā pūrvā katarāparāyor iti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ samānodarkaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 10]
kim u śreṣṭhaḥ kiṃ yaviṣṭho na ājagann upa no vājā adhvaram ṛbhukṣā ity ārbhavaṃ nārāśaṃsaṃ trivat ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 13 11]
idam itthā raudraṃ gūrtavacā ye yajñena dakṣiṇayā samaktā iti vaiśvadevam | [AB, 5, 13 12]
{AB, 5, 14}
nābhānediṣṭhaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 5, 14 1]
nābhānediṣṭhaṃ vai mānavam brahmacaryaṃ vasantam bhrātaro nirabhajan so 'bravīd etya kim mahyam abhāktety etam eva niṣṭhāvam avavaditāram ity abruvaṃs tasmāddhāpyetarhi pitaram putrā niṣṭhāvo 'vavaditety evācakṣate | [AB, 5, 14 2]
sa pitaram etyābravīt tvāṃ ha vāva mahyam tatābhākṣur iti tam pitābravīn mā putraka tad ādṛthā aṅgiraso vā ime svargāya lokāya satram āsate te ṣaṣṭhaṃ ṣaṣṭham evāhar āgatya muhyanti tān ete sūkte ṣaṣṭhe 'hani śaṃsaya teṣāṃ yat sahasraṃ satrapariveṣaṇaṃ tat te svar yanto dāsyantīti tatheti | [AB, 5, 14 3]
tān upait prati gṛbhṇīta mānavaṃ sumedhasa iti tam abruvan kiṃkāmo vadasītīdam eva vaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ prajñāpayānīty abravīd atha yad va etat sahasraṃ satrapariveṣaṇaṃ tan me svar yanto datteti tatheti tān ete sūkte ṣaṣṭhe 'hani aśaṃsayat tato vai te pra yajñam ajānan pra svargaṃ lokam | [AB, 5, 14 4]
tad yad ete sūkte ṣaṣṭhe 'hani śaṃsati yajñasya prajñātyai svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai | [AB, 5, 14 5]
taṃ svar yanto 'bruvann etat te brāhmaṇa sahasram iti tad enaṃ samākurvāṇam puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇaśavāsy uttarata upotthāyābravīn mama vā idam mama vai vāstuham iti so 'bravīn mahyaṃ vā idam adur iti tam abravīt tad vai nau tavaiva pitari praśna iti sa pitaram ait tam pitābravīn nanu te putrakādūr ity adur eva ma ity abravīt tat tu me puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇaśavāsy uttarata upodatiṣṭhan mama vā idam mama vai vāstuham ity āditeti tam pitābravīt tasyaiva putraka tat tat tu sa tubhyaṃ dāsyatīti sa punar etyābravīt tava ha vāva kila bhagava idam iti me pitāheti so 'bravīt tad ahaṃ tubhyam eva dadāmi ya eva satyam avādīr iti | [AB, 5, 14 6]
tasmād evaṃ viduṣā satyam eva vaditavyam | [AB, 5, 14 7]
sa eṣa sahasrasanir mantro yan nābhānediṣṭhaḥ | [AB, 5, 14 8]
upainaṃ sahasraṃ namati pra ṣaṣṭhenāhnā svargaṃ lokaṃ jānāti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 14 9]
{AB, 5, 15}
tāny etāni sahacarāṇy ity ācakṣate nābhānediṣṭhaṃ vālakhilyā vṛṣākapim evayāmarutaṃ tāni sahaiva śaṃset | [AB, 5, 15 1]
yad eṣām antariyāt tad yajamānasyāntariyāt | [AB, 5, 15 2]
yadi nābhānediṣṭhaṃ reto 'syāntariyād yadi vālakhilyāḥ prāṇān asyāntariyād yadi vṛṣākapim ātmānam asyāntariyād yady evayāmarutam pratiṣṭhāyā enaṃ cyāvayed daivyai ca mānuṣyai ca | [AB, 5, 15 3]
nābhānediṣṭhena eva retaḥ asiñcat | [AB, 5, 15 637520_1]
tat vālakhilyābhiḥ vyakarot | [AB, 5, 15 637520_2]
sukīrtinā kākṣīvatena yonim vyahāpayat | [AB, 5, 15 637520_3]
tasmāt jyāyān san garbhaḥ kanīyāṃsam santam yonim na hinasti | [AB, 5, 15 637520_4]
brahmaṇā hi sa kﾱptaḥ | [AB, 5, 15 637520_5]
ahaś ca kṛṣṇam ahar arjunaṃ cety āgnimārutasya pratipad ahaś cāhaś ceti punarāvṛttam punarninṛttaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 15 5]
madhvo vo nāma mārutaṃ yajatrā iti mārutam bahvabhivyāhṛtyam anto vai bahv antaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 15 6]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 15 7]
sa pratnathā sahasā jāyamāna iti jātavedasyaṃ samānodarkaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 15 8]
dhārayan dhārayann iti śaṃsati prasraṃsād vā antasya bibhāya tad yathā punarāgrantham punarnigrantham antam badhnīyān mayūkhaṃ vāntato dhāraṇāya nihanyāt tādṛk tad yad dhārayan dhārayann iti śaṃsati saṃtatyai | [AB, 5, 15 9]
saṃtatais tryahair avyavacchinnair yanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃso yanti yanti | [AB, 5, 15 10]
{AB, 5, 16}
yad vā eti ca preti ca tat saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 16 1]
yaddhyeva prathamam ahas tad evaitat punar yat saptamam | [AB, 5, 16 2]
yad yuktavad yad rathavad yad āśumad yat pibavad yat prathame pade devatā nirucyate yad ayaṃ loko 'bhyuditaḥ | [AB, 5, 16 3]
yaj jātavad yad aniruktam | [AB, 5, 16 4]
yat kariṣyad yat prathamasyāhno rūpam etāni vai saptamasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 16 5]
samudrād ūrmir madhumāṁ ud ārad iti saptamasyāhna ājyam bhavaty aniruktam saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 16 6]
vāg vai samudro na vai vāk kṣīyate na samudraḥ kṣīyate tad yad etat saptamasyāhna ājyam bhavati yajñād eva tad yajñaṃ tanvate vācam eva tat punar upayanti saṃtatyai | [AB, 5, 16 7]
saṃtatais tryahair avyavacchinnair yanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃso yanti | [AB, 5, 16 8]
āpyante vai stomā āpyante chandāṃsi ṣaṣṭhe 'hani tad yathaivāda ājyenāvadānāni punaḥ pratyabhighārayanty ayātayāmatāyā evam evaitat stomāṃś ca chandāṃsi ca punaḥ pratyupayanty ayātayāmatāyai yad etat saptamasyāhna ājyam bhavati | [AB, 5, 16 9]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ triṣṭupprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 16 10]
