ā vāyo bhūṣa śucipā upa naḥ pra yābhir yāsi dāśvāṃsam acchā no niyudbhiḥ śatinībhir adhvaraṃ pra sotā jīro adhvareṣv asthād ye vāyava indramādanāso yā vāṃ śataṃ niyuto yāḥ sahasraṃ pra yad vām mitrāvaruṇā spūrdhann ā gomatā nāsatyā rathenā no deva śavasā yāhi śuṣmin pra vo yajñeṣu devayanto arcan pra kṣodasā dhāyasā sasra eṣeti praugam eti ca preti ca saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpaṃ tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ triṣṭupprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 16 11]
ā tvā rathaṃ yathotaya idaṃ vaso sutam andha indra nedīya ed ihi praitu brahmaṇaspatir agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apaḥ pra va indrāya bṛhata iti prathamenāhnā samāna ātānaḥ saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 16 12]
kayā śubhā savayasaḥ sanīﾱā iti sūktaṃ na jāyamāno naśate na jāta iti jātavat saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 16 13]
tad u kayāśubhīyam etad vai saṃjñānaṃ saṃtani sūktaṃ yat kayāśubhīyam etena ha vā indro 'gastyo marutas te samajānata tad yat kayāśubhīyaṃ śaṃsati saṃjñātyā eva | [AB, 5, 16 14]
tad v āyuṣyaṃ tad yo 'sya priyaḥ syāt kuryād evāsya kayāśubhīyam | [AB, 5, 16 15]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 16 16]
tyaṃ su meṣam mahayā svarvidam iti sūktam atyaṃ na vājaṃ havanasyadaṃ ratham iti rathavat saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 16 17]
tad u jāgataṃ jagatyo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmāj jagatīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 16 18]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 16 19]
tvām iddhi havāmahe tvaṃ hy ehi cerava iti bṛhatpṛṣṭham bhavati saptame 'hani | [AB, 5, 16 20]
yad eva ṣaṣṭhasyāhnas tat | [AB, 5, 16 21]
yad vai rathaṃtaraṃ tad vairūpaṃ yad bṛhat tad vairājaṃ yad rathaṃtaraṃ tacchākvaraṃ yad bṛhat tad raivatam | [AB, 5, 16 22]
tad yad bṛhatpṛṣṭham bhavati bṛhataiva tad bṛhat pratyuttabhnuvanty astomakṛntatrāya | [AB, 5, 16 23]
yad rathaṃtaraṃ syāt kṛntatraṃ syāt | [AB, 5, 16 24]
tasmād bṛhad eva kartavyam | [AB, 5, 16 25]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 5, 16 26]
abhi tvā śūra nonuma iti rathaṃtarasya yonim anu nivartayati rāthaṃtaraṃ hy etad ahar āyatanena | [AB, 5, 16 27]
pibā sutasya rasina iti sāmapragāthaḥ pibavān saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 16 28]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 16 29]
{AB, 5, 17}
indrasya nu vīryāṇi pra vocam iti sūktam preti saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 1]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 17 2]
abhi tyam meṣam puruhūtam ṛgmiyam iti sūktaṃ yad vāva preti tad abhīti saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 3]
tad u jāgataṃ jagatyo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhīyate tasmāj jagatīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 17 4]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 17 5]
tat savitur vṛṇīmahe 'dyā no deva savitar iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau rāthaṃtare 'hani saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 6]
abhi tvā deva savitar iti sāvitraṃ yad vāva preti tad abhīti saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 7]
pretāṃ yajñasya śambhuveti dyāvāpṛthivīyam preti saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 8]
ayaṃ devāya janmana ity ārbhavaṃ jātavat saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 9]
ā yāhi vanasā saheti dvipadāḥ śaṃsati dvipād vai puruṣaś catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai tad yad dvipadāḥ śaṃsati yajamānam eva tad dvipratiṣṭhaṃ catuṣpātsu paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 5, 17 10]
aibhir agne duvo gira iti vaiśvadevam eti saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 11]
tāny u gāyatrāṇi gāyatratṛtīyasavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 17 12]
vaiśvānaro ājījanad ity āgnimārutasya pratipaj jātavat saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 13]
pra yat vas triṣṭubham iṣam iti mārutaṃ preti saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 14]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 17 15]
dūtaṃ vo viśvavedasam iti jātavedasyam aniruktaṃ saptame 'hani saptamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 17 16]
tāny u gāyatrāni gāyatratṛtīyasavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 17 17]
{AB, 5, 18}
yad vai neti na preti yat sthitaṃ tad aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 1]
yaddhy eva dvitīyam ahas tad evaitat punar yad aṣṭamam | [AB, 5, 18 2]
yad ūrdhvavad yat prativad yad antarvad yad vṛṣaṇvad yad vṛdhanvad yan madhyame pade devatā nirucyate yad antarikṣam abhyuditam | [AB, 5, 18 3]
yad dvyagni yan mahadvad yad dvihūtavad yat punarvad yat kurvat | [AB, 5, 18 4]
yad dvitīyasyāhno rūpam etāni vā aṣṭamasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 18 5]
agniṃ vo devam agnibhiḥ sajoṣā ity aṣṭamasyāhna ājyam bhavati dvyagny aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 6]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ triṣṭupprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 18 7]
kuvid aṅga namasā ye vṛdhāsaḥ pīvoannāṁ rayivṛdhaḥ sumedhā ucchann uṣasaḥ sudinā ariprā uśantā dūtā na dabhāya gopā yāvat taras tanvo yāvad ojaḥ prati vāṃ sūra udite sūktair dhenuḥ pratnasya kāmyaṃ duhānā brahmā ṇā indropa yāhi vidvān ūrdhvo agniḥ sumatiṃ vasvo aśred uta syā naḥ sarasvatī juṣāṇeti praugam prativad antarvad dvihūtavad ūrdhvavad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 8]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ triṣṭupprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 18 9]
viśvānarasya vas patim indra it somapā eka indra nedīya ed ihy uttiṣṭha brahmaṇaspate 'gnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apo bṛhad indrāya gāyateti dvitīyenāhnā samāna ātāno 'ṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 10]
śaṃsā mahām indraṃ yasmin viśvā iti sūktam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 11]
mahaś cit tvam indra yata etān iti sūktam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 12]
pibā somam abhi yam ugra tarda iti sūktam ūrvaṃ gavyam mahi gṛṇāna indreti mahadvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 13]
mahāṁ indro nṛvad ā carṣaṇiprā iti sūktam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 14]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 18 15]
tam asya dyāvāpṛthivī sacetaseti sūktaṃ yad ait kṛṇvāno mahimānam indriyam iti mahadvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 16]
tad u jāgataṃ jagatyo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhīyate tasmājjagatīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 18 17]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 18 18]
mahadvanti sūktāni śasyante mahad vā antarikṣam antarikṣasyāptyai | [AB, 5, 18 19]
pañca sūktāni śasyante pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 18 20]
abhi tvā śūra nonumo 'bhi tvā pūrvapītaya iti rathaṃtaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavaty aṣṭame 'hani | [AB, 5, 18 21]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutā | [AB, 5, 18 22]
tvām iddhi havāmaha iti bṛhato yonim anu nivartayati bārhataṃ hy etad ahar āyatanena | [AB, 5, 18 23]
ubhayaṃ śṛṇavacca na iti sāmapragātho yac cedam adya yad u ca hya āsīd iti bārhate 'hany aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 18 24]
tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 18 25]
{AB, 5, 19}
apūrvyā purutamāny asmā iti sūktam mahe vīrāya tavase turāyeti mahadvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpaṃ tāṃ su te kīrtim maghavan mahitveti sūktam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpaṃ tvam mahāṁ indra yo ha śuṣmair iti sūktam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpaṃ tvam mahāṁ indra tubhyaṃ ha kṣā iti sūktam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 1]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 19 2]
divaś cid asya varimā vi papratha iti sūktam indraṃ na mahneti mahadvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 3]
tad u jāgataṃ jagatyo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tacchando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmājjagatīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 19 4]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 19 5]
mahadvanti sūktāni śasyante mahad vā antarikṣam antarikṣasyāptyai pañca pañca sūktāni śasyante pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 19 6]
tāni dvedhā pañcānyāni pañcānyāni daśa sampadyante sā daśinī virāﾱ annam virāﾱ annam paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 19 7]
viśvo devasya netus tat savitur vareṇyam ā viśvadevaṃ satpatim iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau bārhate 'hani aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 8]
hiraṇyapāṇim ūtaya iti sāvitram ūrdhvavad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 9]
mahī dyauḥ pṛthivī ca na iti dyāvāpṛthivīyam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 10]
yuvānā pitarā punar ity ārbhavam punarvad aṣṭame 'hani aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 11]
imā nu kam bhuvanā sīṣadhāmeti dvipadāḥ śaṃsati dvipād vai puruṣaś catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaśchandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai tad yad dvipadāḥ śaṃsati yajamānam eva tad dvipratiṣṭhaṃ catuṣpātsu paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 5, 19 12]
devānām id avo mahad iti vaiśvadevam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 13]
tāny u gāyatrāṇi gāyatratṛtīyasavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 19 14]
ṛtāvānaṃ vaiśvānaram ity āgnimārutasya pratipad agnir vaiśvānaro mahān iti mahadvad aṣṭame 'hanyaṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 15]
krīﾱaṃ vaḥ śardho mārutam iti mārutaṃ jambhe rasasya vāvṛdha iti vṛdhanvad aṣṭame 'hany aṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 16]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 19 17]
agne mṛﾱa mahāṁ asīti jātavedasyam mahadvad aṣṭame 'hanyaṣṭamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 19 18]
tāny u gāyatrāṇi gāyatratṛtīyasavana eṣa tryaha eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 19 19]
{AB, 5, 20}
yad vai samānodarkaṃ tan navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 1]
yaddhyeva tṛtīyam ahas tad evaitat punar yannavamam | [AB, 5, 20 2]
yad aśvavad yad antavad yat punarāvṛttaṃ yat punarninṛttaṃ yad ratavad yat paryastavad yat trivad yad antarūpaṃ yad uttame pade devatā nirucyate yad asau loko 'bhyuditaḥ | [AB, 5, 20 3]
yacchucivad yat satyavad yat kṣetivad yad gatavad yad okavat | [AB, 5, 20 4]
yat kṛtaṃ yat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpam etāni vai navamasyāhno rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 20 5]
aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭham iti navamasyāhna ājyaṃ bhavati gatavan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 6]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ triṣṭupprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 20 7]
pra vīrayā śucayo dadrire te te satyena manasā dīdhyānā divi kṣayantā rajasaḥ pṛthivyām ā viśvavārāśvinā gataṃ no 'yaṃ soma indra tubhyaṃ sunva ā tu pra brahmāṇo aṅgiraso nakṣanta sarasvatīṃ devayanto havanta ā no divo bṛhataḥ parvatād ā sarasvaty abhi no neṣi vasya iti praugaṃ śucivat satyavat kṣetivad gatavad okavan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 8]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ triṣṭupprātaḥsavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 20 9]
taṃ tam id rādhase mahe traya indrasya somā indra nedīya ed ihi pra nūnam brahmaṇaspatir agnir netā tvaṃ soma kratubhiḥ pinvanty apo nakiḥ sudāso ratham iti tṛtīyenāhnā samāna ātāno navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 10]
indraḥ svāhā pibatu yasya soma iti sūktam anto vai svāhākāro 'nto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 11]
gāyat sāma nabhanyaṃ yathā ver iti sūktam arcāma tad vāvṛdhānaṃ svarvad ity anto vai svar anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 12]
tiṣṭhā harī ratha ā yujyamāneti sūktam anto vai sthitam anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 13]
imā u tvā purutamasya kāror iti sūktaṃ dhiyo ratheṣṭhām ity anto vai sthitam anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 14]
tad u traiṣṭubhaṃ tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 20 15]
pra mandine pitumad arcatā vaca iti sūktaṃ samānodarkaṃ navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 20 16]
tad u jāgataṃ jagatyo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nividdhīyate tasmāj jagatīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 20 17]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 20 18]
pañca sūktāni śasyante pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 20 19]
tvām iddhi havāmahe tvaṃ hy ehi cerava iti bṛhatpṛṣṭham bhavati navame 'hani | [AB, 5, 20 20]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyācyutābhi tvā śūra nonuma iti rathaṃtarasya yonim anu nivartayati rāthaṃtaraṃ hy etad ahar āyatanenendra tridhātu śaraṇam iti sāmapragāthas trivān navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpaṃ tyam ū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtam iti tārkṣyo 'cyutaḥ | [AB, 5, 20 21]
{AB, 5, 21}
saṃ ca tve jagmur gira indra pūrvīr iti sūktaṃ gatavan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 1]
kadā bhuvan rathakṣayāṇi brahmeti sūktaṃ kṣetivad antarūpaṃ kṣetīva vā antaṃ gatvā navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 2]
ā satyo yātu maghavāṁ ṛjīṣīti sūktaṃ satyavan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 3]
tat ta indriyam paramam parācair iti sūktam anto vai paramam anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 4]
tad u traiṣṭubham tena pratiṣṭhitapadena savanaṃ dādhārāyatanād evaitena na pracyavate | [AB, 5, 21 5]
aham bhuvaṃ vasunaḥ pūrvyas patir iti sūktam ahaṃ dhanāni saṃjayāmi śaśvata ity anto vai jitam anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 6]
tad u jāgataṃ jagatyo vā etasya tryahasya madhyaṃdinaṃ vahanti tad vai tac chando vahati yasmin nivid dhīyate tasmājjagatīṣu nividaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 5, 21 7]
mithunāni sūktāni śasyante traiṣṭubhāni ca jāgatāni ca mithunaṃ vai paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai pañca pañca sūktāni śasyante pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai tāni dvedhā pañcānyāni pañcānyāni daśa sampadyante sā daśinī virāﾱ annam virāﾱ annaṃ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 5, 21 8]
tat savitur vṛṇīmahe 'dyā no deva savitar iti vaiśvadevasya pratipadanucarau rāthaṃtare 'hani navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 9]
doṣo āgād iti sāvitram anto vai gatam anto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 10]
pra vām mahi dyavī abhīti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ śucī upa praśastaya iti śucivan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 11]
indra iṣe dadātu nas te no ratnāni dhattanety ārbhavaṃ trir ā sāptāni sunvata iti trivan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 12]
babhrur eko viṣuṇaḥ sūnaro yuveti dvipadāḥ śaṃsati dvipād vai puruṣaś catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai tad yad dvipadāḥ śaṃsati yajamānam eva tad dvipratiṣṭhaṃ catuṣpātsu paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 5, 21 13]
ye triṃśati trayas para iti vaiśvadevaṃ trivan navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 14]
tāny u gāyatrāṇi gāyatratṛtīyasavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 21 15]
vaiśvānaro na ūtaya ity āgnimārutasya pratipad ā pra yātu parāvata ity anto vai parāvato 'nto navamam ahar navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 16]
maruto yasya hi kṣaya iti mārutaṃ kṣetivad antarūpaṃ kṣetīva vā antaṃ gatvā navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 17]
jātavedase sunavāma somam iti jātavedasyācyutā | [AB, 5, 21 18]
prāgnaye vācam īrayeti jātavedasyaṃ samānodarkaṃ navame 'hani navamasyāhno rūpam | [AB, 5, 21 19]
sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣa iti śaṃsati bahu vā etasmin navarātre kiṃca kiṃca vāraṇaṃ kriyate śāntyā eva tad yat sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣaḥ sa naḥ parṣad ati dviṣa iti śaṃsati sarvasmād evaināṃs tad enasaḥ pramuñcati | [AB, 5, 21 20]
tāny u gāyatrāṇi gāyatratṛtīyasavana eṣa tryahaḥ | [AB, 5, 21 21]
{AB, 5, 22}
pṛṣṭhyaṃ ṣaﾱaham upayanti yathā vai mukham evam pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaﾱahas tad yathāntaram mukhasya jihvā tālu dantā evaṃ chandomā atha yenaiva vācaṃ vyākaroti yena svādu cāsvādu ca vijānāti tad daśamam ahaḥ | [AB, 5, 22 1]
yathā vai nāsike evam pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaﾱahas tad yathāntaram nāsikayor evaṃ chandomā atha yenaiva gandhān vijānāti tad daśamam ahaḥ | [AB, 5, 22 2]
yathā vā akṣy evam pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaﾱahas tad yathāntaram akṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇam evaṃ chandomā atha yaiva kanīnikā yena paśyati tad daśamam ahaḥ | [AB, 5, 22 3]
yathā vai karṇa evam pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaﾱahas tad yathāntaraṃ karṇasyaivaṃ chandomā atha yenaiva śṛṇoti tad daśamam ahaḥ | [AB, 5, 22 4]
śrīr vai daśamam ahaḥ śriyaṃ vā eta āgacchanti ye daśamam ahar āgacchanti tasmād daśamam ahar avivākyam bhavati mā śriyo 'vavādiṣmeti duravavadaṃ hi śreyasaḥ | [AB, 5, 22 5]
te tataḥ sarpanti | [AB, 5, 22 6]
te mārjayante | [AB, 5, 22 7]
te patnīśālāṃ samprapadyante | [AB, 5, 22 8]
teṣāṃ ya etām āhutiṃ vidyāt sa brūyāt samanvārabhadhvam iti sa juhuyāt | [AB, 5, 22 9]
iha rameha ramadhvam iha dhṛtir iha svadhṛtir agne vāṭ svāhā vāﾱ iti | [AB, 5, 22 10]
sa yad iha ramety āhāsminn evaināṃs tal loke ramayatīha ramadhvam iti yad āha prajām evaiṣu tad ramayatīha dhṛtir iha svadhṛtir iti yad āha prajāṃ caiva tad vācaṃ ca yajamāneṣu dadhāty agne vāﾱ iti rathaṃtaram svāhā vāﾱ iti bṛhat | [AB, 5, 22 11]
devānāṃ vā etan mithunaṃ yad bṛhadrathaṃtare devānām eva tan mithunena mithunam avarundhate devānām mithunena mithunam prajāyante prajātyai | [AB, 5, 22 12]
prajāyate prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 22 13]
te tataḥ sarpanti te mārjayante ta āgnīdhraṃ samprapadyante teṣāṃ ya etām āhutiṃ vidyāt sa brūyāt samanvārabhadhvam iti sa juhuyāt | [AB, 5, 22 14]
upasṛjan dharuṇam mātaraṃ dharuṇo dhayan rāyas poṣam iṣam ūrjam asmāsu dīdharat svāheti | [AB, 5, 22 15]
rāyas poṣam iṣam ūrjam avarunddha ātmane ca yajamānebhyaś ca yatraivaṃ vidvān etām āhutiṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 22 16]
{AB, 5, 23}
te tataḥ sarpanti te sadaḥ samprapadyante yathāyatham anya ṛtvijo vyutsarpanti saṃsarpanty udgātāras te sarparājñyā ṛkṣu stuvate | [AB, 5, 23 1]
iyaṃ vai sarparājñīyaṃ hi sarpato rājñīyaṃ vā alomikevāgra āsīt saitam mantram apaśyad āyaṃ gauḥ pṛśnir akramīd iti tām ayam pṛśnir varṇa āviśan nānārūpo yaṃ yaṃ kāmam akāmayata yad idaṃ kiṃcauṣadhayo vanaspatayaḥ sarvāṇi rūpāṇi | [AB, 5, 23 2]
pṛśnir enaṃ varṇa āviśati nānārūpo yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 23 3]
manasā prastauti manasodgāyati manasā pratiharati vācā śaṃsati | [AB, 5, 23 4]
vāk ca vai manaś ca devānām mithunaṃ devānām eva tan mithunena mithunam avarundhate devānām mithunena mithunam prajāyante prajātyai prajāyate prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 23 5]
atha caturhotṝn hotā vyācaṣṭe tad eva tat stutam anuśaṃsati | [AB, 5, 23 6]
devānāṃ vā etad yajñiyaṃ guhyaṃ nāma yac caturhotāras tad yac caturhotṝn hotā vyācaṣṭe devānām eva tad yajñiyaṃ guhyaṃ nāma prakāśaṃ gamayati tad enam prakāśaṃ gatam prakāśam gamayati | [AB, 5, 23 7]
gacchati prakāśaṃ ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 23 8]
yam brāhmaṇam anūcānaṃ yaśo narcched iti ha smāhāraṇyam paretya darbhastambān udgrathya dakṣiṇato brahmāṇam upaveśya caturhotṝn vyācakṣīta | [AB, 5, 23 9]
devānāṃ vā etad yajñiyaṃ guhyaṃ nāma yac caturhotāras tad yac caturhotṝn vyācakṣīta devānām eva tad yajñiyaṃ guhyaṃ nāma prakāśaṃ gamayati tad enam prakāśaṃ gatam prakāśaṃ gamayati gacchati prakāśaṃ ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 23 10]
{AB, 5, 24}
athaudumbarīṃ samanvārabhante | [AB, 5, 24 1]
iṣam ūrjam anvārabha iti | [AB, 5, 24 2]
ūrg vā annādyam udumbaraḥ | [AB, 5, 24 3]
yad vai tad devā iṣam ūrjaṃ vyabhajanta tata udumbaraḥ samabhavat tasmāt sa triḥ saṃvatsarasya pacyate | [AB, 5, 24 4]
tad yad audumbarīm samanvārabhanta iṣam eva tad ūrjam annādyaṃ samanvārabhante | [AB, 5, 24 5]
vācaṃ yacchanti vāg vai yajño yajñam eva tad yacchanti | [AB, 5, 24 6]
ahar niyacchanty ahar vai svargo lokaḥ svargam eva tal lokaṃ niyacchanti | [AB, 5, 24 7]
na divā vācaṃ visṛjeran yad divā vācaṃ visṛjerann ahar bhrātṛvyāya pariśiṃṣyuḥ | [AB, 5, 24 8]
na naktaṃ vācaṃ visṛjeran yan naktaṃ vācaṃ visṛjeran rātrīm bhrātṛvyāya pariśiṃṣyuḥ | [AB, 5, 24 9]
samayāviṣitaḥ sūryaḥ syād atha vācaṃ visṛjeraṃs tāvantam eva tad dviṣate lokam pariśiṃṣanti | [AB, 5, 24 10]
atho khalv astamita eva vācaṃ visṛjeraṃs tamobhājam eva tad dviṣantam bhrātṛvyaṃ kurvanti | [AB, 5, 24 11]
āhavanīyam parītya vācaṃ visṛjeran yajño vā āhavanīyaḥ svargo loka āhavanīyo yajñenaiva tat svargeṇa lokena svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti | [AB, 5, 24 12]
yad ihonam akarma yad atyarīricāma prajāpatiṃ tat pitaram apyetv iti vācaṃ visṛjante | [AB, 5, 24 13]
prajāpatiṃ vai prajā anuprajāyante prajāpatir ūnātiriktayoḥ pratiṣṭhā nainān ūnaṃ nātiriktaṃ hinasti | [AB, 5, 24 14]
prajāpatim evonātiriktāny abhyatyarjanti ya evaṃ vidvāṃsa etena vācaṃ visṛjante | [AB, 5, 24 15]
tasmād evaṃ vidvāṃsa etenaiva vācaṃ visṛjeran | [AB, 5, 24 16]
{AB, 5, 25}
adhvaryo ity āhvayate caturhotṛṣu vadiṣyamāṇas tad āhāvasya rūpam | [AB, 5, 25 1]
oṃ hotas tathā hotar ity adhvaryuḥ pratigṛṇāty avasite 'vasite daśasu padeṣu | [AB, 5, 25 2]
teṣāṃ cittiḥ srug āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 3]
cittam ājyam āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 4]
vāg vedir āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 5]
ādhītam barhir āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 6]
keto agnir āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 7]
vijñātam agnīd āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 8]
prāṇo havir āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 9]
sāmādhvaryur āsīt | [AB, 5, 25 10]
vācaspatir hotāsīt | [AB, 5, 25 11]
mana upavaktāsīt | [AB, 5, 25 12]
te vā etaṃ graham agṛhṇata vācaspate vidhe nāman vidhema te nāma vidhes tvam asmākaṃ nāmnā dyāṃ gaccha yāṃ devāḥ prajāpatigṛhapataya ṛddhim arādhnuvaṃs tām ṛddhiṃ rātsyāmaḥ | [AB, 5, 25 13]
atha prajāpates tanūr anudravati brahmodyaṃ ca | [AB, 5, 25 14]
annādā cānnapatnī cānnādā tad agnir annapatnī tad ādityaḥ | [AB, 5, 25 15]
bhadrā ca kalyāṇī ca bhadrā tat somaḥ kalyāṇī tat paśavaḥ | [AB, 5, 25 16]
anilayā cāpabhayā cānilayā tad vāyur na hy eṣa kadācanelayaty apabhayā tan mṛtyuḥ sarvaṃ hy etasmād bībhāya | [AB, 5, 25 17]
anāptā cānāpyā cānāptā tat pṛthivy anāpyā tad dyauḥ | [AB, 5, 25 18]
anādhṛṣyā cāpratidhṛṣyā cānādhṛṣyā tad agnir apratidhṛṣyā tad ādityaḥ | [AB, 5, 25 19]
apūrvā cābhrātṛvyā cāpūrvā tan mano 'bhrātṛvyā tat saṃvatsaraḥ | [AB, 5, 25 20]
etā vāva dvādaśa prajāpates tanva eṣa kṛtsnaḥ prajāpatis tat kṛtsnam prajāpatim āpnoti daśamam ahaḥ | [AB, 5, 25 21]
atha brahmodyam vadanty agnir gṛhapatir iti haika āhuḥ so 'sya lokasya gṛhapatir vāyur gṛhapatir iti haika āhuḥ so 'ntarikṣalokasya gṛhapatir asau vai gṛhapatir yo 'sau tapaty eṣa patir ṛtavo gṛhā yeṣāṃ vai gṛhapatiṃ devaṃ vidvān gṛhapatir bhavati rādhnoti sa gṛhapatī rādhnuvanti te yajamānā yeṣāṃ vā apahatapāpmānaṃ devaṃ vidvān gṛhapatir bhavaty apa sa gṛhapatiḥ pāpmānaṃ hate 'pa te yajamānāḥ pāpmānaṃ ghnate 'dhvaryo arātsmārātsma | [AB, 5, 25 22]
{AB, 5, 26}
uddharāhavanīyam ity aparāhṇa āha yad evāhnā sādhu karoti tad eva tat prāṅ uddhṛtya tadabhaye nidhatte | [AB, 5, 26 1]
uddharāhavanīyam iti prātar āha yad eva rātryā sādhu karoti tad eva tat prāṅ uddhṛtya tadabhaye nidhatte | [AB, 5, 26 2]
yajño vā āhavanīyaḥ svargo loka āhavanīyaḥ | [AB, 5, 26 3]
yajña eva tat svarge loke svargaṃ lokaṃ nidhatte ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 26 4]
yo vā agnihotraṃ vaiśvadevaṃ ṣoﾱaśakalam paśuṣu pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda vaiśvadevenāgnihotreṇa ṣoﾱaśakalena paśuṣu pratiṣṭhitena rādhnoti | [AB, 5, 26 5]
raudraṃ gavi sad vāyavyam upāvasṛṣṭam āśvinaṃ duhyamānaṃ saumyaṃ dugdhaṃ vāruṇam adhiśritam pauṣṇaṃ samudantam mārutaṃ viṣyandamānaṃ vaiśvadevam binduman maitraṃ śarogṛhītaṃ dyāvāpṛthivīyam udvāsitaṃ sāvitram prakrāntaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ hriyamāṇam bārhaspatyam upasannam agneḥ pūrvāhutiḥ prajāpater uttaraindraṃ hutam | [AB, 5, 26 6]
etad vā agnihotraṃ vaiśvadevaṃ ṣoﾱaśakalam paśuṣu pratiṣṭhitam | [AB, 5, 26 7]
vaiśvadevenāgnihotreṇa ṣoﾱaśakalena paśuṣu pratiṣṭhitena rādhnoti ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 26 8]
{AB, 5, 27}
yasyāgnihotry upāvasṛṣṭā duhyamānopaviśet kā tatra prāyaścittir iti tām abhimantrayeta | [AB, 5, 27 1]
yasmād bhīṣā niṣīdasi tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi paśūn naḥ sarvān gopāya namo rudrāya mīﾱhuṣa iti | [AB, 5, 27 2]
tām utthāpayet | [AB, 5, 27 3]
udasthād devy aditir āyur yajñapatāv adhāt indrāya kṛṇvatī bhāgam mitrāya varuṇāya ceti | [AB, 5, 27 4]
athāsyā udapātram ūdhasi ca mukhe copagṛhṇīyād athainām brāhmaṇāya dadyāt sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [AB, 5, 27 5]
yasyāgnihotry upāvasṛṣṭā duhyamānā vāśyeta kā tatra prāyaścittir ity aśanāyāṃ ha vā eṣā yajamānasya pratikhyāya vāśyate tām annam apy ādayecchāntyai śāntir vā annaṃ sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā iti sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [AB, 5, 27 6]
yasyāgnihotry upāvasṛṣṭā duhyamānā spandeta kā tatra prāyaścittir iti sā yat tatra skandayet tad abhimṛśya japet | [AB, 5, 27 7]
yad adya dugdham pṛthivīm asṛpta yad oṣadhīr atyasṛpad yad āpaḥ payo gṛheṣu payo aghnyāyāṃ payo vatseṣu payo astu tan mayīti | [AB, 5, 27 8]
tatra yat pariśiṣṭaṃ syāt tena juhuyād yad alaṃ homāya syāt | [AB, 5, 27 9]
yady u vai sarvaṃ siktaṃ syād athānyām āhūya tāṃ dugdhvā tena juhuyād ā tveva śraddhāyai hotavyaṃ sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ | [AB, 5, 27 10]
sarvaṃ vā asya barhiṣyaṃ sarvam parigṛhītaṃ ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 27 11]
{AB, 5, 28}
asau vā asyādityo yūpaḥ pṛthivī vedir oṣadhayo barhir vanaspataya idhmā āpaḥ prokṣaṇyo diśaḥ paridhayaḥ | [AB, 5, 28 1]
yaddha vā asya kiṃca naśyati yan mriyate yad apājanti sarvaṃ haivainaṃ tad amuṣmiṃlloke yathā barhiṣi dattam āgacched evam āgacchati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 28 2]
ubhayān vā eṣa devamanuṣyān viparyāsaṃ dakṣiṇā nayati sarvaṃ cedaṃ yad idaṃ kiṃca | [AB, 5, 28 3]
manuṣyān vā eṣa sāyamāhutyā devebhyo dakṣiṇā nayati sarvaṃ cedaṃ yad idaṃ kiṃca ta ete pralīnā nyokasa iva śere manuṣyā devebhyo dakṣiṇā nītāḥ | [AB, 5, 28 4]
devān vā eṣa prātarāhutyā manuṣyebhyo dakṣiṇā nayati sarvaṃ cedaṃ yad idaṃ kiṃca ta ete vividānā ivotpatanty ado 'haṃ kariṣye 'do 'haṃ gamiṣyāmīti vadantaḥ | [AB, 5, 28 5]
yāvantaṃ ha vai sarvam idaṃ dattvā lokaṃ jayati tāvantaṃ ha lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 28 6]
agnaye vā eṣa sāyamāhutyāśvinam upākaroti tad vāk pratigṛṇāti vāg vāg iti | [AB, 5, 28 7]
agninā hāsya rātryāśvinaṃ śastam bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 28 8]
ādityāya vā eṣa prātarāhutyā mahāvratam upākaroti tat prāṇaḥ pratigṛṇāty annam annam ity ādityena hāsyāhnā mahāvrataṃ śastam bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 28 9]
tasya vā etasyāgnihotrasya sapta ca śatāni viṃśatiś ca saṃvatsare sāyamāhutayaḥ sapta co eva śatāni viṃśatiś ca saṃvatsare prātarāhutayas tāvatyo 'gner yajuṣmatya iṣṭakāḥ | [AB, 5, 28 10]
saṃvatsareṇa hāsyāgninā cityeneṣṭam bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān agnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 28 11]
{AB, 5, 29}
vṛṣaśuṣmo ha vātāvata uvāca jātūkarṇyo vaktā smo vā idaṃ devebhyo yad vai tad agnihotram ubhayedyur ahūyatānyedyur vāva tad etarhi hūyata iti | [AB, 5, 29 1]
etad u hovāca kumārī gandharvagṛhītā vaktā smo vā idam pitṛbhyo yad vai tad agnihotram ubhayedyur ahūyatānyedyur vāva tad etarhi hūyata iti | [AB, 5, 29 2]
etad vā agnihotram anyedyur hūyate yad astamite sāyaṃ juhoty anudite prātar athaitad agnihotram ubhayedyur hūyate yad astamite sāyaṃ juhoty udite prātaḥ | [AB, 5, 29 3]
tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 29 4]
caturviṃśe ha vai saṃvatsare 'nuditahomī gāyatrīlokam āpnoti dvādaśa uditahomī sa yadā dvau saṃvatsarāv anudite juhoty atha hāsyaiko huto bhavaty atha ya udite juhoti saṃvatsareṇaiva saṃvatsaram āpnoti ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 29 5]
eṣa ha vā ahorātrayos tejasi juhoti yo 'stamite sāyaṃ juhoty udite prātar agninā vai tejasā rātris tejasvaty ādityena tejasāhas tejasvat | [AB, 5, 29 6]
ahorātrayor hāsya tejasi hutaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti | [AB, 5, 29 7]
tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 29 8]
{AB, 5, 30}
ete ha vai saṃvatsarasya cakre yad ahorātre tābhyām eva tat saṃvatsaram eti sa yo 'nudite juhoti yathaikataścakreṇa yāyāt tādṛk tad atha ya udite juhoti yathobhayataścakreṇa yān kṣipram adhvānaṃ samaśnuvīta tādṛk tat | [AB, 5, 30 1]
tad eṣābhi yajñagāthā gīyate | [AB, 5, 30 2]
bṛhadrathaṃtarābhyām idam eti yuktaṃ yad bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyac cāpi sarvaṃ tābhyām iyād agnīn ādhāya dhīro divaivānyaj juhuyān naktam anyad iti | [AB, 5, 30 3]
rāthaṃtarī vai rātry ahar bārhatam agnir vai rathaṃtaram ādityo bṛhad ete ha vā enaṃ devate bradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayato ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 30 4]
tad eṣābhi yajñagāthā gīyate | [AB, 5, 30 5]
yathā ha vā sthūriṇaikena yāyād akṛtvānyad upayojanāya evaṃ yanti te bahavo janāsaḥ purodayāj juhvati ye 'gnihotram iti | [AB, 5, 30 6]
tāṃ vā etāṃ devatām prayatīṃ sarvam idam anupraiti yad idaṃ kiṃcaitasyai hīdaṃ devatāyā anucaraṃ sarvaṃ yad idaṃ kiṃca saiṣānucaravatī devatā | [AB, 5, 30 7]
vindate ha vā anucaram bhavaty asyānucaro ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 5, 30 8]
sa vā eṣa ekātithiḥ sa eṣa juhvatsu vasati | [AB, 5, 30 9]
tad yad ado gāthā bhavati | [AB, 5, 30 10]
anenasam enasā so 'bhiśastād enasvato vāpaharād enaḥ ekātithim apa sāyaṃ ruṇaddhi bisāni steno apa so jahāreti | [AB, 5, 30 11]
eṣa ha vai sa ekātithiḥ sa eṣa juhvatsu vasaty etāṃ vāva sa devatām aparuṇaddhi yo 'lam agnihotrāya san nāgnihotraṃ juhoti tam eṣā devatāparoddhāparuṇaddhy asmāc ca lokād amuṣmāc cobhābhyāṃ yo 'lam agnihotrāya san nāgnihotraṃ juhoti | [AB, 5, 30 12]
tasmād yo 'lam agnihotrāya syāj juhuyāt | [AB, 5, 30 13]
tasmād āhur na sāyam atithir aparudhya iti | [AB, 5, 30 14]
etaddha sma vai tad vidvān nagarī jānaśruteya uditahominam aikādaśākṣam mānutantavyam uvāca prajāyām enaṃ vijñātā smo yadi vidvān vā juhoty avidvān veti tasyo haikādaśākṣe rāṣṭram iva prajā babhūva rāṣṭram iva ha vā asya prajā bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 30 15]
{AB, 5, 31}
udyann u khalu vā āditya āhavanīyena raśmīn saṃdadhāti sa yo 'nudite juhoti yathā kumārāya vā vatsāya vājātāya stanam pratidadhyāt tādṛk tad atha ya udite juhoti yathā kumārāya vā vatsāya vā jātāya stanam pratidadhyāt tādṛk tat tam asmai pratidhīyamānam ubhayor lokayor annādyam anu pratidhīyate 'smāc ca lokād amuṣmāc cobhābhyām | [AB, 5, 31 1]
sa yo 'nudite juhoti yathā puruṣāya vā hastine vāprayate hasta ādadhyāt tādṛk tad atha ya udite juhoti yathā puruṣāya vā hastine vā prayate hasta ādadhyāt tādṛk tat tam eṣa etenaiva hastenordhvaṃ hṛtvā svarge loka ādadhāti ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 31 2]
udyann u khalu vā ādityaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni praṇayati tasmād enam prāṇa ity ācakṣate prāṇe hāsya samprati hutam bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 31 3]
eṣa ha vai satyaṃ vadan satye juhoti yo 'stamite sāyaṃ juhoty udite prātar bhūr bhuvaḥ svar aum agnir jyotir jyotir agnir iti sāyaṃ juhoti bhūr bhuvaḥ svar auṃ sūryo jyotir jyotiḥ sūrya iti prātaḥ satyaṃ hāsya vadataḥ satye hutaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān udite juhoti tasmād udite hotavyam | [AB, 5, 31 4]
tad eṣābhi yajñagāthā gīyate | [AB, 5, 31 5]
prātaḥ prātar anṛtaṃ te vadanti purodayāj juhvati ye 'gnihotraṃ divā kīrtyam adivā kīrtayantaḥ sūryo jyotir na tadā jyotir eṣām iti | [AB, 5, 31 6]
{AB, 5, 32}
prajāpatir akāmayata prajāyeya bhūyān syām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa tapas taptvemāṃllokān asṛjata pṛthivīm antarikṣaṃ divaṃ tāṃllokān abhyatapat tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trīṇi jyotīṃṣy ajāyantāgnir eva pṛthivyā ajāyata vāyur antarikṣād ādityo divas tāni jyotīṃṣy abhyatapat tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trayo vedā ajāyanta ṛgveda evāgner ajāyata yajurvedo vāyoḥ sāmaveda ādityāt tān vedān abhyatapat tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trīṇi śukrāṇy ajāyanta bhūr ity eva ṛgvedād ajāyata bhuva iti yajurvedāt svar iti sāmavedāt | [AB, 5, 32 1]
tāni śukrāṇy abhyatapat tebhyo 'bhitaptebhyas trayo varṇā ajāyantākāra ukāro makāra iti tān ekadhā samabharat tad etad aum iti tasmād om om iti praṇauty om iti vai svargo loka om ity asau yo 'sau tapati | [AB, 5, 32 2]
sa prajāpatir yajñam atanuta tam āharat tenāyajata sa ṛcaiva hautram akarod yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnodgīthaṃ yad etat trayyai vidyāyai śukraṃ tena brahmatvam akarot | [AB, 5, 32 3]
sa prajāpatir yajñaṃ devebhyaḥ samprāyacchat te devā yajñam atanvata tam āharanta tenāyajanta ta ṛcaiva hautram akurvan yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnodgīthaṃ yad evaitat trayyai vidyāyai śukraṃ tena brahmatvam akurvan | [AB, 5, 32 4]
te devā abruvan prajāpatiṃ yadi no yajña ṛkta ārtiḥ syād yadi yajuṣṭo yadi sāmato yady avijñātā sarvavyāpad vā kā prāyaścittir iti sa prajāpatir abravīd devān yadi vo yajña ṛkta ārtir bhavati bhūr iti gārhapatye juhavātha yadi yajuṣṭo bhuva ity āgnīdhrīye 'nvāhāryapacane vā haviryajñeṣu yadi sāmataḥ svar ity āhavanīye yady avijñātā sarvavyāpad vā bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti sarvā anudrutyāhavanīya eva juhavātheti | [AB, 5, 32 5]
etāni ha vai vedānām antaḥśleṣaṇāni yad etā vyāhṛtayas tad yathātmanātmānaṃ saṃdadhyād yathā parvaṇā parva yathā śleṣmaṇā carmaṇyaṃ vānyad vā viśliṣṭam saṃśleṣayed evam evaitābhir yajñasya viśliṣṭaṃ saṃdadhāti saiṣā sarvaprāyaścittir yad etā vyāhṛtayas tasmād eṣaiva yajñe prāyaścittiḥ kartavyā | [AB, 5, 32 6]
{AB, 5, 33}
tad āhur mahāvadāḥ yad ṛcaiva hautraṃ kriyate yajuṣādhvaryavaṃ sāmnodgīthaṃ vyārabdhā trayī vidyā bhavaty atha kena brahmatvaṃ kriyata iti trayyā vidyayeti brūyāt | [AB, 5, 33 1]
ayaṃ vai yajño yo 'yaṃ pavate tasya vāk ca manaś ca vartanyau vācā ca hi manasā ca yajño vartata iyaṃ vai vāg ado manas tad vācā trayyā vidyayaikam pakṣaṃ saṃskurvanti manasaiva brahmā saṃskaroti | [AB, 5, 33 2]
te haike brahmāṇa upākṛte prātaranuvāke stomabhāgāñ japitvā bhāṣamāṇā upāsate taddhaitad uvāca brāhmaṇa upākṛte prātaranuvāke brahmāṇam bhāṣamāṇaṃ dṛṣṭvārdham asya yajñasyāntaragur iti tad yathaikapāt puruṣo yann ekataścakro vā ratho vartamāno bhreṣaṃ nyety evam eva sa yajño bhreṣaṃ nyeti yajñasya bhreṣam anu yajamāno bhreṣaṃ nyeti | [AB, 5, 33 3]
tasmād brahmopākṛte prātaranuvāke vācaṃyamaḥ syād opāṃśvantaryāmayor homād upākṛteṣu pavamāneṣv odṛco 'tha yāni stotrāṇi saśastrāṇy ā teṣāṃ vaṣaṭkārād vācaṃyama eva syāt tad yathobhayataḥpāt puruṣo yann ubhayataścakro vā ratho vartamāno na riṣyaty evam eva sa yajño na riṣyati yajñasyāriṣṭim anu yajamāno na riṣyati | [AB, 5, 33 4]
{AB, 5, 34}
tad āhur yad grahān me 'grahīt prācārīn ma āhutīr me 'hauṣīd ity adhvaryave dakṣiṇā nīyanta udagāsīn ma ity udgātre 'nvavocan me 'śaṃsīn me 'yākṣīn ma iti hotre kiṃ svid eva cakruṣe brahmaṇe dakṣiṇā nīyante 'kṛtvāho svid eva haratā iti | [AB, 5, 34 1]
yajñasya haiṣa bhiṣag yad brahmā yajñāyaiva tad bheṣajaṃ kṛtvā harati | [AB, 5, 34 2]
atho yad bhūyiṣṭhenaiva brahmaṇā chandasāṃ rasenārtvijyaṃ karoti yad brahmā tasmād brahmārdhabhāggha vā eṣa itareṣām ṛtvijām agra āsa yad brahmārdham eva brahmaṇa āsārdham itareṣām ṛtvijām | [AB, 5, 34 3]
tasmād yadi yajña ṛkta ārtiḥ syād yadi yajuṣṭo yadi sāmato yady avijñātā sarvavyāpad vā brahmaṇa eva nivedayante tasmād yadi yajña ṛkta ārtir bhavati bhūr iti brahmā gārhapatye juhuyād yadi yajuṣṭo bhuva ity āgnīdhrīye 'nvāhāryapacane vā haviryajñeṣu yadi sāmataḥ svar ity āhavanīye yady avijñātā sarvavyāpad vā bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti sarvā anudrutyāhavanīya eva juhuyāt | [AB, 5, 34 4]
sa prastotopākṛte stotra āha brahman stoṣyāmaḥ praśāstar iti sa bhūr iti brahmā prātaḥsavane brūyād indravantaḥ studhvam iti bhuva iti mādhyaṃdine savane brūyād indravantaḥ studhvam iti svar iti tṛtīyasavane brūyād indravantaḥ studhvam iti bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity ukthe vātirātre vā brūyād indravantaḥ studhvam iti | [AB, 5, 34 5]
sa yad āhendravantaḥ studhvam ity aindro vai yajña indro yajñasya devatā sendram eva tad udgīthaṃ karotīndrān mā gād indravantaḥ studhvam iti evaināṃs tad āha tad āha | [AB, 5, 34 6]
{AB, 6, 1}
devā ha vai sarvacarau satraṃ niṣedus te ha pāpmānaṃ nāpajaghnire tān hovācārbudaḥ kādraveyaḥ sarpaṛṣir mantrakṛd ekā vai vo hotrākṛtā tāṃ vo 'haṃ karavāṇy atha pāpmānam apahaniṣyadhva iti te ha tathety ūcus teṣāṃ ha sma sa madhyaṃdine madhyaṃdina evopodāsarpan grāvṇo 'bhiṣṭauti | [AB, 6, 1 1]
tasmān madhyaṃdine madhyaṃdina eva grāvṇo 'bhiṣṭuvanti tadanukṛti | [AB, 6, 1 2]
sa ha yenopodāsarpat taddhāpy etarhy arbudodāsarpaṇī nāma prapad asti | [AB, 6, 1 3]
tān ha rājā madayāṃcakāra te hocur āśīviṣo vai no rājānam avekṣate hantāsyoṣṇīṣeṇākṣyāv apinahyāmeti tatheti tasya hoṣṇīṣeṇākṣyāv apinehus tasmād uṣṇīṣam eva paryasya grāvṇo 'bhiṣṭuvanti tadanukṛti | [AB, 6, 1 4]
tān ha rājā madayām eva cakāra te hocuḥ svena vai no mantreṇa grāvṇo 'bhiṣṭautīti hantāsyānyābhir ṛgbhir mantram āpṛṇacāmeti tatheti tasya hānyābhir ṛgbhir mantram āpapṛcus tato hainān na madayāṃcakāra tad yad asyānyābhir ṛgbhir mantram āpṛñcanti śāntyā eva | [AB, 6, 1 5]
te ha pāpmānam apajaghnire teṣām anv apahatiṃ sarpāḥ pāpmānam apajaghnire ta ete 'pahatapāpmāno hitvā pūrvāṃ jīrṇāṃ tvacaṃ navayaiva prayanti | [AB, 6, 1 6]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 1 7]
{AB, 6, 2}
tad āhuḥ kiyatībhir abhiṣṭuyād iti śatenety āhuḥ śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ śatavīryaḥ śatendriya āyuṣy evainaṃ tad vīrya indriye dadhāti | [AB, 6, 2 1]
trayastriṃśatā vety āhus trayastriṃśato vai sa devānām pāpmano 'pāhaṃs trayastriṃśad vai tasya devā iti | [AB, 6, 2 2]
aparimitābhir abhiṣṭuyād aparimito vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpater vā eṣā hotrā yad grāvastotrīyā tasyāṃ sarve kāmā avarudhyante sa yad aparimitābhir abhiṣṭauti sarveṣāṃ kāmānām avaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 2 3]
sarvān kāmān avarunddhe ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 2 4]
tasmād aparimitābhir evābhiṣṭuyāt | [AB, 6, 2 5]
tad āhuḥ katham abhiṣṭuyād ity akṣaraśaḥ caturakṣaraśaḥ pacchaḥ ardharcaśaḥ ṛkśaḥ iti tad yad ṛkśo na tad avakalpate 'tha yat paccho no eva tad avakalpate 'tha yad akṣaraśaś caturakṣaraśo vi tathā chandāṃsi lupyeran bahūni tathākṣarāṇi hīyerann ardharcaśa evābhiṣṭuyāt pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 2 6]
dvipratiṣṭho vai puruṣaś catuṣpādāḥ paśavo yajamānam eva tad dvipratiṣṭhaṃ catuṣpātsu paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmād ardharcaśa evābhiṣṭuyāt | [AB, 6, 2 7]
tad āhur yan madhyaṃdine madhyaṃdina eva grāvṇo 'bhiṣṭauti katham asyetarayoḥ savanayor abhiṣṭutam bhavatīti yad eva gāyatrībhir abhiṣṭauti gāyatraṃ vai prātaḥsavanaṃ tena prātaḥsavane 'tha yaj jagatībhir abhiṣṭauti jāgataṃ vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ tena tṛtīyasavane | [AB, 6, 2 8]
evam u hāsya madhyaṃdine madhyaṃdina eva grāvṇo 'bhiṣṭuvataḥ sarveṣu savaneṣv abhiṣṭutam bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 2 9]
tad āhur yad adhvaryur evānyān ṛtvijaḥ saṃpreṣyaty atha kasmād eṣa etām asampreṣitaḥ pratipadyata iti mano vai grāvastotrīyāsampreṣitaṃ vā idaṃ manas tasmād eṣa etām asampreṣitaḥ pratipadyate | [AB, 6, 2 10]
{AB, 6, 3}
vāg vai subrahmaṇyā tasyai somo rājā vatsaḥ some rājani krīte subrahmaṇyām āhvayanti yathā dhenum upahvayet tena vatsena yajamānāya sarvān kāmān duhe | [AB, 6, 3 1]
sarvān hāsmai kāmān vāg duhe ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 3 2]
tad āhuḥ kiṃ subrahmaṇyāyai subrahmaṇyātvam iti vāg eveti brūyād vāg vai brahma ca subrahma ceti | [AB, 6, 3 3]
tad āhur atha kasmād enam pumāṃsaṃ santaṃ strīm ivācakṣata iti vāgghi subrahmaṇyeti brūyāt teneti | [AB, 6, 3 4]
tad āhur yad antarvedītara ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvanti bahirvedi subrahmaṇyā katham asyāntarvedy ārtvijyaṃ kṛtam bhavatīti veder vā utkaram utkiranti yad evotkare tiṣṭhann āhvayatīti brūyāt teneti | [AB, 6, 3 5]
tad āhur atha kasmād utkare tiṣṭhan subrahmaṇyām āhvayatīty ṛṣayo vai satram āsata teṣāṃ yo varṣiṣṭha āsīt tam abruvan subrahmaṇyām āhvaya tvaṃ no nediṣṭhād devān hvayiṣyasīti varṣiṣṭham evainaṃ tat kurvanty atho vedim eva tat sarvām prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 3 6]
tad āhuḥ kasmād asmā ṛṣabhaṃ dakṣiṇām abhyājantīti vṛṣā vā ṛṣabho yoṣā subrahmaṇyā tan mithunaṃ tasya mithunasya prajātyā iti | [AB, 6, 3 7]
upāṃśu pātnīvatasyāgnīdhro yajati reto vai pātnīvata upāṃśv iva vai retasaḥ siktiḥ | [AB, 6, 3 8]
nānuvaṣaṭkaroti saṃsthā vā eṣā yad anuvaṣaṭkāro nedretaḥ saṃsthāpayānīty asaṃsthitaṃ vai retasaḥ samṛddhaṃ tasmān nānuvaṣaṭkaroti | [AB, 6, 3 9]
neṣṭur upastha āsīno bhakṣayati patnībhājanaṃ vai neṣṭāgniḥ patnīṣu reto dadhāti prajātyā agninaiva tat patnīṣu reto dadhāti prajātyai | [AB, 6, 3 10]
prajāyate prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 3 11]
dakṣiṇā anu subrahmaṇyā saṃtiṣṭhate vāg vai subrahmaṇyānnaṃ dakṣiṇānnādya eva tad vāci yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti pratiṣṭhāpayanti | [AB, 6, 3 12]
{AB, 6, 4}
devā vai yajñam atanvata tāṃs tanvānān asurā abhyāyan yajñaveśasam eṣāṃ kariṣyāma iti tān dakṣiṇata upāyan yata eṣāṃ yajñasya taniṣṭham amanyanta te devāḥ pratibudhya mitrāvaruṇau dakṣiṇataḥ paryauhaṃs te mitrāvaruṇābhyām eva dakṣiṇataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata tathaivaitad yajamānā mitrāvaruṇābhyām eva dakṣiṇataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apaghnate tasmān maitrāvaruṇam maitrāvaruṇaḥ prātaḥsavane śaṃsati mitrāvaruṇābhyāṃ hi devā dakṣiṇataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata | [AB, 6, 4 1]
te vai dakṣiṇato 'pahatā asurā madhyato yajñam prāviśaṃs te devāḥ pratibudhyendram madhyato 'dadhus ta indreṇaiva madhyataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata tathaivaitad yajamānā indreṇaiva madhyataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apaghnate tasmād aindram brāhmaṇācchaṃsī prātaḥsavane śaṃsatīndreṇa hi devā madhyataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata | [AB, 6, 4 2]
te vai madhyato 'pahatā asurā uttarato yajñam prāviśaṃs te devāḥ pratibudhyendrāgnī uttarataḥ paryauhaṃs ta indrāgnibhyāṃ evottarataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata tathaivaitad yajamānā indrāgnibhyām evottarataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apaghnate tasmād aindrāgnam achāvākaḥ prātaḥsavane śaṃsatīndrāgnibhyāṃ hi devā uttarataḥ prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata | [AB, 6, 4 3]
te vā uttarato 'pahatā asurāḥ purastāt paryadravan samanīkatas te devāḥ pratibudhyāgnim purastāt prātaḥsavane paryauhaṃs te 'gninaiva purastāt prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata tathaivaitad yajamānā agninaiva purastāt prātaḥsavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apaghnate tasmād āgneyam prātaḥsavanam | [AB, 6, 4 4]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 4 5]
te vai purastād apahatā asurāḥ paścāt parītya prāviśaṃs te devāḥ pratibudhya viśvān devān ātmānaṃ paścāt tṛtīyasavane paryauhaṃs te viśvair eva devair ātmabhiḥ paścāt tṛtīyasavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apāghnata tathaivaitad yajamānā viśvair eva devair ātmabhiḥ paścāt tṛtīyasavane 'surarakṣāṃsy apaghnate tasmād vaiśvadevaṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [AB, 6, 4 6]
apa pāpmānaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 4 7]
te vai devā asurān evam apāghnata sarvasmād eva yajñāt tato vai devā abhavan parāsurāḥ | [AB, 6, 4 8]
bhavaty ātmanā parāsya dviṣan pāpmā bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 4 9]
te devā evaṃ kﾱptena yajñenāpāsurān pāpmānam aghnatājayan svargaṃ lokam | [AB, 6, 4 10]
apa ha vai dviṣantam pāpmānam bhrātṛvyaṃ hate jayati svargaṃ lokaṃ ya evaṃ veda yaś caivaṃ vidvān savanāni kalpayati | [AB, 6, 4 11]
{AB, 6, 5}
stotriyaṃ stotriyasyānurūpaṃ kurvanti prātaḥsavane 'har eva tad ahno 'nurūpaṃ kurvanty avareṇaiva tad ahnā param ahar abhyārabhante | [AB, 6, 5 1]
atha tathā na madhyaṃdine śrīr vai pṛṣṭhāni tāni tasmai na tasthānāni yat stotriyaṃ stotriyasyānurūpaṃ kuryuḥ | [AB, 6, 5 2]
tayaiva vibhaktyā tṛtīyasavane na stotriyaṃ stotriyasyānurūpaṃ kurvanti | [AB, 6, 5 3]
{AB, 6, 6}
athāta ārambhaṇīyā eva | [AB, 6, 6 1]
ṛjunītī no varuṇa iti maitrāvaruṇasya mitro nayatu vidvān iti praṇetā vā eṣa hotrakāṇāṃ yan maitrāvaruṇas tasmād eṣā praṇetṛmatī bhavati | [AB, 6, 6 2]
indraṃ vo viśvatas parīti brāhmaṇācchaṃsino havāmahe janebhya itīndram evaitayāhar ahar nihvayante | [AB, 6, 6 3]
na haiṣāṃ vihave 'nya indraṃ vṛṅkte yatraivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇācchaṃsy etām ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 6 4]
yat soma ā sute nara ity achāvākasyendrāgnī ajohavur itīndrāgnī evaitayāhar ahar nihvayante na haiṣāṃ vihave 'nya indrāgnī vṛṅkte yatraivaṃ vidvān achāvāka etām ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 6 5]
tā vā etāḥ svargasya lokasya nāvaḥ sampāriṇyaḥ svargam evaitābhir lokam abhisaṃtaranti | [AB, 6, 6 6]
{AB, 6, 7}
athātaḥ paridhānīyā eva | [AB, 6, 7 1]
te syāma deva varuṇeti maitrāvaruṇasyeṣaṃ svaś ca dhīmahīty ayaṃ vai loka iṣam ity asau lokaḥ svar ity ubhāv evaitayā lokāv ārabhante | [AB, 6, 7 2]
vy antarikṣam atirad iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsino vivattṛcaṃ svargam evaibhya etayā lokaṃ vivṛṇoti | [AB, 6, 7 3]
made somasya rocanā indro yad abhinad valamiti | [AB, 6, 7 4]
siṣāsavo vā ete yad dīkṣitās tasmād eṣā valavatī bhavati | [AB, 6, 7 5]
ud gā ājad aṅgirobhya āviṣkṛṇvan guhā satīḥ arvāñcaṃ nunude valam iti sanim evaibhya etayāvarunddhe | [AB, 6, 7 6]
indreṇa rocanā diva iti svargo vai loka indreṇa rocanā divaḥ | [AB, 6, 7 7]
dṛﾱhāni dṛṃhitāni ca sthirāṇi na parāṇuda iti | [AB, 6, 7 8]
svarga evaitayā loke 'harahaḥ pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 6, 7 9]
āhaṃ sarasvatīvator ity achāvākasya vāg vai sarasvatī vāgvator iti haitad āhendrāgnyor avo vṛṇa ity etaddha vā indrāgnyoḥ priyaṃ dhāma yad vāg iti priyeṇaivainau tad dhāmnā samardhayati | [AB, 6, 7 10]
priyeṇa dhāmnā samṛdhyate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 7 11]
{AB, 6, 8}
ubhayyaḥ paridhānīyā bhavanti hotrakāṇām prātaḥsavane ca mādhyaṃdine cāhīnāś caikāhikāś ca | [AB, 6, 8 1]
tata aikāhikābhir eva maitrāvaruṇaḥ paridadhāti tenāsmāllokānna pracyavate | [AB, 6, 8 2]
ahīnābhir achāvākaḥ svargasya lokasyāptyā | [AB, 6, 8 3]
ubhayībhir brāhmaṇācchaṃsī teno sa ubhau vyanvārabhamāṇa etīmaṃ cāmuṃ ca lokam atho maitrāvaruṇaṃ cāchāvākaṃ cātho ahīnaṃ caikāham cātho saṃvatsaraṃ cāgniṣṭomaṃ caivam u sa ubhau vyanvārabhamāṇa eti | [AB, 6, 8 4]
atha tata aikāhikā eva tṛtīyasavane hotrakāṇām paridhānīyā bhavanti pratiṣṭhā vā ekāhaḥ pratiṣṭhāyām eva tad yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti | [AB, 6, 8 5]
anavānam prātaḥsavane yajet | [AB, 6, 8 6]
ekāṃ dve na stomam atiśaṃset tad yathābhiheṣate pipāsate kṣipram prayacchet tādṛk tad atho kṣipraṃ devebhyo 'nnādyaṃ somapītham prayacchānīti kṣipraṃ hāsmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhati | [AB, 6, 8 7]
aparimitābhir uttarayoḥ savanayor aparimito vai svargo lokaḥ svargasya lokasyāptyai | [AB, 6, 8 8]
kāmaṃ taddhotā śaṃsed yaddhotrakāḥ pūrvedyuḥ śaṃseyur yad vā hotā taddhotrakāḥ prāṇo vai hotāṅgāni hotrakāḥ samāno vā ayam prāṇo 'ṅgāny anusaṃcarati tasmāt tat kāmaṃ hotā śaṃsed yaddhotrakāḥ pūrvedyuḥ śaṃseyur yad vā hotā taddhotrakāḥ | [AB, 6, 8 9]
sūktāntair hotā paridadhad ety atha samānya eva tṛtīyasavane hotrakāṇām paridhānīyā bhavanty ātmā vai hotāṅgāni hotrakāḥ samānā vā ime 'ṅgānām antās tasmāt samānya eva tṛtīyasavane hotrakāṇām paridhānīyā bhavanti bhavanti | [AB, 6, 8 10]
{AB, 6, 9}
ā tvā vahantu haraya iti prātaḥsavana unnīyamānebhyo 'nvāha vṛṣaṇvatīḥ pītavatīḥ sutavatīr madvatī rūpasamṛddhāḥ | [AB, 6, 9 1]
aindrīr anvāhaindro vai yajñaḥ | [AB, 6, 9 2]
gāyatrīr anvāha gāyatraṃ vai prātaḥsavanam | [AB, 6, 9 3]
nava nyūnāḥ prātaḥsavane 'nvāha nyūne vai retaḥ sicyate | [AB, 6, 9 4]
daśa madhyaṃdine 'nvāha nyūne vai retaḥ siktam madhyaṃ striyai prāpya sthaviṣṭham bhavati | [AB, 6, 9 5]
nava nyūnās tṛtīyasavane 'nvāha nyūnād vai prajāḥ prajāyante | [AB, 6, 9 6]
tad yad etāni kevalasūktāny anvāha yajamānam eva tad garbham bhūtam prajanayati yajñād devayonyai | [AB, 6, 9 7]
te haike sapta saptānvāhuḥ sapta prātaḥsavane sapta mādhyaṃdine sapta tṛtīyasavane yāvatyo vai puronuvākyās tāvatyo yājyāḥ sapta vai prāñco yajanti sapta vaṣaṭkurvanti tāsām etāḥ puronuvākyā iti vadantaḥ | [AB, 6, 9 8]
tat tathā na kuryād yajamānasya ha te reto vilumpanty atho yajamānam eva yajamāno hi sūktam | [AB, 6, 9 9]
navabhir vā etam maitrāvaruṇo 'smāl lokād antarikṣalokam abhi pravahati daśabhir antarikṣalokād amuṃ lokam abhy antarikṣaloko hi jyeṣṭho navabhir amuṣmāl lokāt svargaṃ lokam abhi | [AB, 6, 9 10]
na ha vai te yajamānaṃ svargaṃ lokam abhi voﾱhum arhanti ye sapta saptānvāhuḥ | [AB, 6, 9 11]
tasmāt kevalaśa eva sūktāny anubrūyāt | [AB, 6, 9 12]
{AB, 6, 10}
athāha yad aindro vai yajño 'tha kasmād dvāveva prātaḥsavane prasthitānām pratyakṣād aindrībhyāṃ yajato hotā caiva brāhmaṇācchaṃsī cedaṃ te somyam madhviti hotā yajatīndra tvā vṛṣabhaṃ vayaṃ iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsī nānādevatyābhir itare kathaṃ teṣām aindryo bhavantīti | [AB, 6, 10 1]
mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha iti maitrāvaruṇo yajati varuṇaṃ somapītaya iti yad vai kiṃca pītavat padaṃ tad aindraṃ rūpaṃ tenendram prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 10 2]
maruto yasya hi kṣaya iti potā yajati sa sugopātamo jana itīndro vai gopās tad aindraṃ rūpaṃ tenendram prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 10 3]
agne patnīr ihā vaheti neṣṭā yajati tvaṣṭāraṃ somapītaya itīndro vai tvaṣṭā tad aindraṃ rūpaṃ tenendram prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 10 4]
ukṣānnāya vaśānnāyety āgnīdhro yajati somapṛṣṭhāya vedhasa itīndro vai vedhās tad aindraṃ rūpaṃ tenendram prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 10 5]
prātaryāvabhir ā gataṃ devebhir jenyāvasū indrāgnī somapītaya iti svayaṃ samṛddhāchāvākasya | [AB, 6, 10 6]
evam u haitā aindryo bhavanti | [AB, 6, 10 7]
yan nānādevatyās tenānyā devatāḥ prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 10 8]
yad u gāyatryas tenāgneyyaḥ | [AB, 6, 10 9]
etad u haitābhis trayam upāpnoti | [AB, 6, 10 10]
{AB, 6, 11}
asāvi devaṃ goṛjīkam andha iti madhyaṃdina unnīyamānebhyo 'nvāha vṛṣaṇvatīḥ pītavatīḥ sutavatīr madvatī rūpasamṛddhāḥ | [AB, 6, 11 1]
aindrīr anvāhaindro vai yajñas triṣṭubho 'nvāha traiṣṭubham vai mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam | [AB, 6, 11 2]
tad āhur yat tṛtīyasavanasyaiva rūpam madvad atha kasmān madhyaṃdine madvatīr anu cāha yajanti cābhir iti | [AB, 6, 11 3]
mādyantīva vai madhyaṃdine devatāḥ sam eva tṛtīyasavane mādayante tasmān madhyaṃdine madvatīr anu cāha yajanti cābhiḥ | [AB, 6, 11 4]
te vai khalu sarva eva mādhyaṃdine prasthitānām pratyakṣād aindrībhir yajanti | [AB, 6, 11 5]
abhitṛṇṇavatībhir eke | [AB, 6, 11 6]
pibā somam abhi yam ugra tarda iti hotā yajati | [AB, 6, 11 7]
sa īṃ pāhi ya ṛjīṣī tarutra iti maitrāvaruṇo yajati | [AB, 6, 11 8]
evā pāhi pratnathā mandatu tveti brāhmaṇācchaṃsī yajati | [AB, 6, 11 9]
arvāṅ ehi somakāmaṃ tvāhur iti potā yajati | [AB, 6, 11 10]
tavāyaṃ somastvam ehy arvāṅ iti neṣṭā yajati | [AB, 6, 11 11]
indrāya somāḥ pradivo vidānā ity achāvāko yajati | [AB, 6, 11 12]
āpūrṇo asya kalaśaḥ svāhety āgnīdhro yajati | [AB, 6, 11 13]
tāsām etā abhitṛṇṇavatyo bhavantīndro vai prātaḥsavane na vyajayata sa etābhir eva mādhyaṃdinaṃ savanam abhyatṛṇad yad abhyatṛṇat tasmād etā abhitṛṇṇavatyo bhavanti | [AB, 6, 11 14]
{AB, 6, 12}
ihopa yāta śavaso napāta iti tṛtīyasavana unnīyamānebhyo 'nvāha vṛṣaṇvatīḥ pītavatīḥ sutavatīr madvatī rūpasamṛddhās tā aindrārbhavyo bhavanti | [AB, 6, 12 1]
tad āhur yan nārbhavīṣu stuvate 'tha kasmād ārbhavaḥ pavamāna ity ācakṣata iti | [AB, 6, 12 2]
prajāpatir vai pitarbhūn martyān sato 'martyān kṛtvā tṛtīyasavana ābhajat tasmān nārbhavīṣu stuvate 'thārbhavaḥ pavamāna ity ācakṣate | [AB, 6, 12 3]
athāha yad yathāchandasam pūrvayoḥ savanayor anvāha gāyatrīḥ prātaḥsavane triṣṭubho mādhyaṃdine 'tha kasmāj jāgate sati tṛtīyasavane triṣṭubho 'nvāheti | [AB, 6, 12 4]
dhītarasaṃ vai tṛtīyasavanam athaitad adhītarasaṃ śukriyaṃ chando yat triṣṭup savanasya sarasatāyā iti brūyād atho indraṃ evaitat savane 'nvābhajatīti | [AB, 6, 12 5]
athāha yad aindrārbhavaṃ vai tṛtīyasavanam atha kasmād eṣa eva tṛtīyasavane prasthitānām pratyakṣād aindrārbhavyā yajatīndra ṛbhubhir vājavadbhiḥ samukṣitam iti hotaiva nānādevatyābhir itare kathaṃ teṣām aindrārbhavyo bhavantīti | [AB, 6, 12 6]
indrāvaruṇā sutapāv imaṃ sutam iti maitrāvaruṇo yajati yuvo ratho adhvaraṃ devavītaya iti bahūni vāha tad ṛbhūṇām rūpam | [AB, 6, 12 7]
indraś ca somam pibatam bṛhaspata iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsī yajaty ā vāṃ viśantv indavaḥ svābhuva iti bahūni vāha tad ṛbhūṇāṃ rūpam | [AB, 6, 12 8]
ā vo vahantu saptayo raghuṣyada iti potā yajati raghupatvānaḥ pra jigāta bāhubhir iti bahūni vāha tad ṛbhūṇāṃ rūpam | [AB, 6, 12 9]
ameva naḥ suhavā ā hi gantaneti neṣṭā yajati gantaneti bahūni vāha tad ṛbhūṇāṃ rūpam | [AB, 6, 12 10]
indrāviṣṇū pibatam madhvo asyety achāvāko yajaty ā vām andhāṃsi madirāṇy agmann iti bahūni vāha tad ṛbhūṇāṃ rūpam | [AB, 6, 12 11]
imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedasa ity āgnīdhro yajati ratham iva saṃ mahemā manīṣayeti bahūni vāha tad ṛbhūṇāṃ rūpam | [AB, 6, 12 12]
evam u haitā aindrārbhavyo bhavanti | [AB, 6, 12 13]
yan nānādevatyās tenānyā devatāḥ prīṇāti | [AB, 6, 12 14]
yad u jagatprāsāhā jāgataṃ vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ tṛtīyasavanasyaiva samṛddhyai | [AB, 6, 12 15]
{AB, 6, 13}
athāha yad ukthinyo 'nyā hotrā anukthā anyāḥ katham asyaitā ukthinyaḥ sarvāḥ samāḥ samṛddhā bhavantīti | [AB, 6, 13 1]
yad evaināḥ saṃpragīrya hotrā ity ācakṣate tena samāḥ | [AB, 6, 13 2]
yad ukthinyo 'nyā hotrā anukthā anyās teno viṣamāḥ | [AB, 6, 13 3]
evam u hāsyaitā ukthinyaḥ sarvāḥ samāḥ samṛddhā bhavanti | [AB, 6, 13 4]
athāha śaṃsanti prātaḥsavane śaṃsanti mādhyaṃdine hotrakāḥ katham eṣāṃ tṛtīyasavane śastam bhavatīti | [AB, 6, 13 5]
yad eva mādhyaṃdine dve dve sūkte śaṃsantīti brūyāt teneti | [AB, 6, 13 6]
athāha yad dvyuktho hotā kathaṃ hotrakā dvyukthā bhavantīti | [AB, 6, 13 7]
yad eva dvidevatyābhir yajantīti brūyāt teneti | [AB, 6, 13 8]
{AB, 6, 14}
athāha yad etās tisra ukthinyo hotrāḥ katham itarā ukthinyo bhavantīti | [AB, 6, 14 1]
ājyam evāgnīdhrīyāyā uktham marutvatīyam potrīyāyai vaiśvadevaṃ neṣṭrīyāyai tā vā etā hotrā evaṃnyaṅgā eva bhavanti | [AB, 6, 14 2]
athāha yad ekapraiṣā anye hotrakā atha kasmād dvipraiṣaḥ potā dvipraiṣo neṣṭeti | [AB, 6, 14 3]
yatra adaḥ gāyatrī suparṇaḥ bhūtvā somam āharat tat etāsām hotrāṇām indraḥ ukthāni parilupya hotre pradadau | [AB, 6, 14 637930_1]
athāha yaddhotā yakṣaddhotā yakṣad iti maitrāvaruṇo hotre preṣyaty atha kasmād ahotṛbhyaḥ sadbhyo hotrāśaṃsibhyo hotā yakṣaddhotā yakṣad iti preṣyatīti | [AB, 6, 14 5]
prāṇo vai hotā prāṇaḥ sarva ṛtvijaḥ prāṇo yakṣat prāṇo yakṣad ity eva tad āha | [AB, 6, 14 6]
athāhāsty udgātṝṇām praiṣaḥ nāṁ iti astīti brūyād yad evaitat praśāstā japaṃ japitvā studhvam ity āha sa eṣām praiṣaḥ | [AB, 6, 14 7]
athāhāsty achāvākasya pravarāḥ nāṁ iti astīti brūyād yad evainam adhvaryur āhāchāvāka vadasva yat te vādyam ity eṣo 'sya pravaraḥ | [AB, 6, 14 8]
athāha yad aindrāvaruṇam maitrāvaruṇas tṛtīyasavane śaṃsaty atha kasmād asyāgneyau stotriyānurūpau bhavata ity agninā vai mukhena devā asurān ukthebhyo nirjaghnus tasmād asyāgneyau stotriyānurūpau bhavataḥ | [AB, 6, 14 9]
athāha yad aindrābārhaspatyam brāhmaṇācchaṃsī tṛtīyasavane śaṃsaty aindrāvaiṣṇavam achāvākaḥ katham enayor aindrāḥ stotriyānurūpā bhavantītīndro ha sma vā asurān ukthebhyaḥ prajigāya so 'bravīt kaś cāhaṃ cety ahaṃ cāhaṃ ceti ha sma devatā anvavayanti sa yad indraḥ pūrvaḥ prajigāya tasmād enayor aindrāḥ stotriyānurūpā bhavanti yad v ahaṃ cāhaṃ ceti ha sma devatā anvavayus tasmān nānādevatyāni śaṃsataḥ | [AB, 6, 14 10]
{AB, 6, 15}
athāha yad vaiśvadevaṃ vai tṛtīyasavanam atha kasmād etāny aindrāṇi jāgatāni sūktāni tṛtīyasavana ārambhaṇīyāni śasyanta itīndram evaitair ārabhya yantīti brūyād atho yaj jāgataṃ vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ taj jagatkāmyaiva tad yat kiṃcāta ūrdhvaṃ chandaḥ śasyate taddha sarvaṃ jāgatam bhavaty etāni ced aindrāṇi jāgatāni sūktāni tṛtīyasavana ārambhaṇīyāni śasyante | [AB, 6, 15 1]
atha traiṣṭubham achāvāko 'ntataḥ śaṃsati saṃ vāṃ karmaṇeti yad eva panāyyaṃ karma tad etad abhivadati | [AB, 6, 15 2]
sam iṣety annaṃ vā iṣo 'nnādyasyāvaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 15 3]
ariṣṭair naḥ pathibhiḥ pārayanteti svastitāyā evaitad aharahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 15 4]
athāha yaj jāgataṃ vai tṛtīyasavanam atha kasmād eṣāṃ triṣṭubhaḥ paridhānīyā bhavantīti vīryaṃ vai triṣṭub vīrya eva tad antataḥ pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 6, 15 5]
iyam indraṃ varuṇam aṣṭa me gīr iti maitrāvaruṇasya bṛhaspatir naḥ pari pātu paścād iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ubhā jigyathur ity achāvākasya | [AB, 6, 15 6]
ubhau hi tau jigyatuḥ | [AB, 6, 15 7]
na parā jayethe na parā jigya iti | [AB, 6, 15 8]
na hi tayoḥ kataraś cana parājigye | [AB, 6, 15 9]
indraś ca viṣṇo yad apaspṛdhethāṃ tredhā sahasraṃ vi tad airayethām iti | [AB, 6, 15 10]
indraś ca ha vai viṣṇuś cāsurair yuyudhāte tān ha sma jitvocatuḥ kalpāmahā iti te ha tathety asurā ūcuḥ so 'bravīd indro yāvad evāyaṃ viṣṇus trir vikramate tāvad asmākam atha yuṣmākam itarad iti sa imāṃllokān vicakrame 'tho vedān atho vācaṃ tad āhuḥ kiṃ tat sahasram itīme lokā ime vedā atho vāg iti brūyāt | [AB, 6, 15 11]
airayethām airayethām ity achāvāka ukthye 'bhyasyati sa hi tatrāntyo bhavati | [AB, 6, 15 12]
agniṣṭome hotātirātre ca sa hi tatrāntyo bhavati | [AB, 6, 15 13]
abhyasyet ṣoﾱaśini nābhyasyait iti abhyasyed ity āhuḥ katham anyeṣv ahaḥsv abhyasyati katham atra nābhyasyed iti tasmād abhyasyet | [AB, 6, 15 14]
{AB, 6, 16}
athāha yan nārāśaṃsaṃ vai tṛtīyasavanam atha kasmād achāvāko 'ntataḥ śilpeṣv anārāśaṃsīḥ śaṃsatīti | [AB, 6, 16 1]
vikṛtir vai nārāśaṃsaṃ kim iva ca vai kim ivaca reto vikriyate tat tadā vikṛtam prajātam bhavaty athaitan mṛdv iva chandaḥ śithiraṃ yan nārāśaṃsam athaiṣo 'ntyo yad achāvākas tad dṛﾱhatāyai dṛﾱhe pratiṣṭhāsyāma iti | [AB, 6, 16 2]
tasmād achāvāko 'ntataḥ śilpeṣv anārāśaṃsīḥ śaṃsati dṛﾱhatāyai dṛﾱhe pratiṣṭhāsyāma iti dṛﾱhe pratiṣṭhāsyāma iti | [AB, 6, 16 3]
{AB, 6, 17}
yaḥ śvaḥstotriyas tam anurūpaṃ kurvanti prātaḥsavane 'hīnasaṃtatyai | [AB, 6, 17 1]
yathā vā ekāhaḥ suta evam ahīnas tad yathaikāhasya sutasya savanāni saṃtiṣṭhamānāni yanty evam evāhīnasyāhāni saṃtiṣṭhamānāni yanti tad yacchvaḥstotriyam anurūpaṃ kurvanti prātaḥsavane 'hīnasaṃtatyā ahīnameva tat saṃtanvanti | [AB, 6, 17 2]
te vai devāś ca ṛṣayaś cādriyanta samānena yajñaṃ saṃtanavāmeti ta etat samānaṃ yajñasyāpaśyan samānān pragāthān samānīḥ pratipadaḥ samānāni sūktāni | [AB, 6, 17 3]
okaḥsārī vā indro yatra vā indraḥ pūrvaṃ gacchaty aiva tatrāparaṃ gacchati yajñasyaiva sendratāyai | [AB, 6, 17 4]
{AB, 6, 18}
tān vā etān sampātān viśvāmitraḥ prathamam apaśyat tān viśvāmitreṇa dṛṣṭān vāmadevo 'sṛjataiva tvām indra vajrinn atra yan na indro jujuṣe yacca vaṣṭi kathā mahām avṛdhat kasya hotur iti tān kṣipraṃ samapatad yat kṣipraṃ samapatat tat sampātānāṃ sampātatvam | [AB, 6, 18 1]
sa hekṣāṃcakre viśvāmitro yān vā ahaṃ sampātān apaśyaṃ tān vāmadevo 'sṛṣṭa kāni nv ahaṃ sūktāni sampātāṃs tatpratimān sṛjeyeti sa etāni sūktāni sampātāṃs tatpratimān asṛjata sadyo ha jāto vṛṣabhaḥ kanīna indraḥ pūrbhid ātirad dāsam arkair imām ū ṣu prabhṛtiṃ sātaye dhā icchanti tvā somyāsaḥ sakhāyaḥ śāsad vahnir duhitur naptyaṃ gād abhi taṣṭeva dīdhayā manīṣām iti | [AB, 6, 18 2]
ya eka iddhavyaś carṣaṇīnām iti bharadvājo yas tigmaśṛṅgo vṛṣabho na bhīma ud u brahmāṇy airata śravasyeti vasiṣṭho 'smā id u pra tavase turāyeti nodhāḥ | [AB, 6, 18 3]
ta ete prātaḥsavane ṣaﾱahastotriyāñchastvā mādhyaṃdine 'hīnasūktāni śaṃsanti | [AB, 6, 18 4]
tāny etāny ahīnasūktāny ā satyo yātu maghavān ṛjīṣīti satyavan maitrāvaruṇo 'smā id u pra tavase turāyendrāya brahmāṇi rātatamā indra brahmāṇi gotamāso akrann iti brahmaṇvad brāhmaṇācchaṃsī śāsad vahnir janayanta vahnim iti vahnivad achāvākaḥ | [AB, 6, 18 5]
tad āhuḥ kasmād achāvāko vahnivad etat sūktam ubhayatra śaṃsati parāñciṣu caivāhaḥsv abhyāvartiṣu ceti | [AB, 6, 18 6]
vīryavān vā eṣa bahvṛco vahnivad etat sūktaṃ vahati ha vai vahnir dhuro yāsu yujyate tasmād achāvāko vahnivad etat sūktam ubhayatra śaṃsati parāñciṣu caivāhaḥsv abhyāvartiṣu ca | [AB, 6, 18 7]
tāni pañcasv ahaḥsu bhavanti caturviṃśe 'bhijiti viṣuvati viśvajiti mahāvrate 'hīnāni ha vā etāny ahāni na hy eṣu kiṃcana hīyate parāñcīni ha vā etāny ahāny anabhyāvartīni tasmād enāny eteṣv ahaḥsu śaṃsanti | [AB, 6, 18 8]
yad enāni śaṃsanty ahīnān svargāṃllokān sarvarūpān sarvasamṛddhān avāpnavāmeti | [AB, 6, 18 9]
yad evaināni śaṃsantīndram evaitair nihvayante yatharṣabhaṃ vāśitāyai | [AB, 6, 18 10]
yad v evaināni śaṃsanty ahīnasya saṃtatyā ahīnam eva tat saṃtanvanti | [AB, 6, 18 11]
{AB, 6, 19}
tato vā etāṃs trīn sampātān maitrāvaruṇo viparyāsam ekaikam ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 19 1]
evā tvām indra vajrinn atreti prathame 'hani yan na indro jujuṣe yac ca vaṣṭīti dvitīye kathā mahām avṛdhat kasya hotur iti tṛtīye | [AB, 6, 19 2]
trīn eva sampātān brāhmaṇācchaṃsī viparyāsam ekaikam ahar ahaḥ śaṃsatīndraḥ pūrbhid ātirad dāsam arkair iti prathame 'hani ya eka iddhavyaś carṣaṇīnām iti dvitīye yas tigmaśṛṅgo vṛṣabho na bhīma iti tṛtīye | [AB, 6, 19 3]
trīn eva sampātān achāvāko viparyāsam ekaikam ahar ahaḥ śaṃsatīmām ū ṣu prabhṛtiṃ sātaye dhā iti prathame 'hanīcchanti tvā somyāsaḥ sakhāya iti dvitīye śāsad vahnir duhitur naptyaṃ gād iti tṛtīye | [AB, 6, 19 4]
tāni vā etāni nava | [AB, 6, 19 5]
trīṇi cāhar ahaḥ śasyāni | [AB, 6, 19 6]
tāni dvādaśa sampadyante dvādaśa vai māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāpatir yajñas tat saṃvatsaram prajāpatiṃ yajñam āpnuvanti tat saṃvatsare prajāpatau yajñe 'har ahaḥ pratitiṣṭhanto yanti | [AB, 6, 19 7]
tāny antareṇāvāpam āvaperan | [AB, 6, 19 8]
anyūṅkhyā virājo vaimadīś caturthe 'hani paṅktīḥ pañcame pārucchepīḥ ṣaṣṭhe | [AB, 6, 19 9]
atha yāny ahāni mahāstomāni syuḥ ko adya naryo devakāma iti maitrāvaruṇa āvapeta vane na vā yo ny adhāyi cākann iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsy ā yāhy arvāṅ upa vandhureṣṭhā ity achāvākaḥ | [AB, 6, 19 10]
etāni vā āvapanāny etair vā āvapanair devāḥ svargam lokam ajayann etair ṛṣayas tathaivaitad yajamānā etair āvapanaiḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ jayanti | [AB, 6, 19 11]
{AB, 6, 20}
sadyo ha jāto vṛṣabhaḥ kanīna iti maitrāvaruṇaḥ purastāt sūktānām ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 20 1]
tad etat sūktaṃ svargyam etena vai sūktena devāḥ svargaṃ lokam ajayann etena ṛṣayas tathaivaitad yajamānā etena sūktena svargaṃ lokaṃ jayanti | [AB, 6, 20 2]
tad u vaiśvāmitraṃ viśvasya ha vai mitraṃ viśvāmitra āsa | [AB, 6, 20 3]
viśvaṃ hāsmai mitram bhavati ya evaṃ veda yeṣāṃ caivaṃ vidvān etan maitrāvaruṇaḥ purastāt sūktānām ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 20 4]
tad ṛṣabhavat paśumad bhavati paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 20 5]
tat pañcarcam bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ paṅktir vā annam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 20 6]
ud u brahmāṇy airata śravasyeti brāhmaṇācchaṃsī brahmaṇvat samṛddhaṃ sūktam ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 20 7]
tad etat sūktaṃ svargyam etena vai sūktena devāḥ svargaṃ lokam ajayann etena ṛṣayas tathaivaitad yajamānā etena sūktena svargaṃ lokaṃ jayanti | [AB, 6, 20 8]
tad u vāsiṣṭham etena vai vasiṣṭha indrasya priyaṃ dhāmopāgacchat sa paramaṃ lokam ajayat | [AB, 6, 20 9]
upendrasya priyaṃ lokaṃ gacchati jayati paramaṃ lokaṃ ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 20 10]
tad vai ṣaﾱṛcaṃ ṣaḍ vā ṛtava ṛtūnām āptyai | [AB, 6, 20 11]
tad upariṣṭāt sampātānāṃ śaṃsaty āptvaiva tat svargaṃ lokaṃ yajamānā asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhanti | [AB, 6, 20 12]
abhi taṣṭeva dīdhayā manīṣām ity achāvāko 'har ahaḥ śaṃsaty abhivat tatyai rūpam | [AB, 6, 20 13]
abhi priyāṇi marmṛśat parāṇīti yāny eva parāṇy ahāni tāni priyāṇi tāny eva tad abhimarmṛśato yanty abhyārabhamāṇāḥ paro vā asmāl lokāt svargo lokas tam eva tad abhivadati | [AB, 6, 20 14]
kavīṃr icchāmi saṃdṛśe sumedhā iti | [AB, 6, 20 15]
ye vai te na ṛṣayaḥ pūrve pretās te vai kavayas tān eva tad abhyativadati | [AB, 6, 20 16]
tad u vaiśvāmitraṃ viśvasya ha vai mitraṃ viśvāmitra āsa viśvaṃ hāsmai mitram bhavati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 20 17]
tad aniruktam prājāpatyaṃ śaṃsaty anirukto vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai | [AB, 6, 20 18]
sakṛd indraṃ nirāha tenaindrād rūpān na pracyavate | [AB, 6, 20 19]
tad vai daśarcaṃ daśākṣarā virāﾱ annaṃ virāﾱ annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 20 20]
yad eva daśarcaṃ daśa vai prāṇāḥ prāṇān eva tad āpnuvanti prāṇān ātman dadhate | [AB, 6, 20 21]
tad upariṣṭāt sampātānāṃ śaṃsaty āptvaiva tat svargaṃ lokaṃ yajamānā asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhanti | [AB, 6, 20 22]
{AB, 6, 21}
kas tam indra tvāvasuṃ kan navyo atasīnāṃ kad ū nv asyākṛtam iti kadvantaḥ pragāthā ārambhaṇīyā ahar ahaḥ śasyante | [AB, 6, 21 1]
ko vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai | [AB, 6, 21 2]
yad eva kadvantaḥ annaṃ vai kam annādyasyāvaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 21 3]
yad v eva kadvantaḥ ahar ahar vā ete śāntāny ahīnasūktāny upayuñjānā yanti tāni kadvadbhiḥ pragāthaiḥ śamayanti tāny ebhyaḥ śāntāni kam bhavanti tāny enāñchāntāni svargaṃ lokam abhi vahanti | [AB, 6, 21 4]
triṣṭubhaḥ sūktapratipadaḥ śaṃseyuḥ | [AB, 6, 21 5]
tā haike purastāt pragāthānāṃ śaṃsanti dhāyyā iti vadantaḥ | [AB, 6, 21 6]
tat tathā na kuryāt | [AB, 6, 21 7]
kṣatraṃ vai hotā viśo hotrāśaṃsinaḥ kṣatrāyaiva tad viśam pratyudyāminīṃ kuryuḥ pāpavasyasam | [AB, 6, 21 8]
triṣṭubho ma imāḥ sūktapratipada ity eva vidyāt | [AB, 6, 21 9]
tad yathā samudram praplaverann evaṃ haiva te praplavante ye saṃvatsaraṃ vā dvādaśāhaṃ vāsate tad yathā sairāvatīṃ nāvam pārakāmāḥ samāroheyur evam evaitās triṣṭubhaḥ samārohanti | [AB, 6, 21 10]
na ha vā etac chando gamayitvā svargaṃ lokam upāvartate vīryavattamaṃ hi | [AB, 6, 21 11]
tābhyo na vyāhvayīta samānaṃ hi chando 'tho ned dhāyyāḥ karavāṇīti | [AB, 6, 21 12]
yad enāḥ śaṃsanti prajñātābhiḥ sūktapratipadbhiḥ sūktāni samārohāmeti | [AB, 6, 21 13]
yad evaināḥ śaṃsantīndram evaitābhir nihvayante yatharṣabhaṃ vāśitāyai yad v evaināḥ śaṃsanty ahīnasya saṃtatyā ahīnam eva tat saṃtanvanti | [AB, 6, 21 14]
{AB, 6, 22}
apa prāca indra viśvāṁ amitrān iti maitrāvaruṇaḥ purastāt sūktānām ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 22 1]
apāpāco abhibhūte nudasva apodīco apa śūrādharāca urau yathā tava śarman mademeti | [AB, 6, 22 2]
abhayasya rūpam abhayam iva hi yann icchati | [AB, 6, 22 3]
brahmaṇā te brahmayujā yunajmīti brāhmaṇācchaṃsy ahar ahaḥ śaṃsati yunajmīti yuktavatī yukta iva hy ahīno 'hīnasya rūpam | [AB, 6, 22 4]
uruṃ no lokam anu neṣi vidvān ity achāvāko 'harahaḥ śaṃsaty anu neṣīty etīva hy ahīno 'hīnasya rūpam | [AB, 6, 22 5]
neṣīti sattrāyaṇarūpam | [AB, 6, 22 6]
tā vā etā ahar ahaḥ śasyante | [AB, 6, 22 7]
samānībhiḥ paridadhyuḥ | [AB, 6, 22 8]
okaḥsārī haiṣām indro yajñam bhavatī3ṃ yatharṣabho vāśitāṃ yathā vā gauḥ prajñātaṃ goṣṭham evaṃ haiṣām indro yajñam aiva gacchati | [AB, 6, 22 9]
na śunaṃhuvīyayāhīnasya paridadhyāt kṣatriyo ha rāṣṭrāccyavate yo haiva paro bhavati tam abhihvayati | [AB, 6, 22 10]
{AB, 6, 23}
athāto 'hīnasya yuktiś ca vimuktiś ca | [AB, 6, 23 1]
vy antarikṣam atirad ity ahīnaṃ yuṅkta eved indram iti vimuñcati | [AB, 6, 23 2]
āhaṃ sarasvatīvator nūnaṃ sā ta ity ahīnaṃ yuṅkte | [AB, 6, 23 3]
te syāma deva varuṇa nū ṣṭuta iti vimuñcati | [AB, 6, 23 4]
eṣa ha vā ahīnaṃ tantum arhati ya enaṃ yoktuṃ ca vimoktuṃ ca veda | [AB, 6, 23 5]
tad yac caturviṃśe 'han yujyante sā yuktir atha yat purastād udayanīyasyātirātrasya vimucyante sa vimuktiḥ | [AB, 6, 23 6]
tad yac caturviṃśe 'hann aikāhikābhiḥ paridadhyur atrāhaiva yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayeyur nāhīnakarma kuryur atha yad ahīnaparidhānīyābhiḥ paridadhyur yathā śrānto 'vimucyamāna utkṛtyetaivaṃ yajamānā utkṛtyerann ubhayībhiḥ paridadhyuḥ | [AB, 6, 23 7]
tad yathā dīrghādhva upavimokaṃ yāyāt tādṛk tat | [AB, 6, 23 8]
saṃtato haiṣāṃ yajño bhavatīṃ vy ū muñcante | [AB, 6, 23 9]
ekāṃ dve na dvayoḥ savanayoḥ stomam atiśaṃset | [AB, 6, 23 10]
dīrghāraṇyāni ha vai bhavanti yatra bahvībhiḥ stomo 'tiśasyate | [AB, 6, 23 11]
aparimitābhiḥ tṛtīyasavane 'parimito vai svargo lokaḥ svargasya lokasyāptyai | [AB, 6, 23 12]
saṃtato hāsyābhyārabdho 'visrasto 'hīno bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān ahīnaṃ tanute | [AB, 6, 23 13]
{AB, 6, 24}
devā vai vale gāḥ paryapaśyaṃs tā yajñenaivepsaṃs tāḥ ṣaṣṭhenāhnāpnuvaṃs te prātaḥsavane nabhākena valam anabhayaṃs taṃ yad anabhayān aśrathayann evainaṃ tat ta u tṛtīyasavane vajreṇa vālakhilyābhir vācaḥ kūṭenaikapadayā valaṃ virujya gā udājan | [AB, 6, 24 1]
tathaivaitad yajamānāḥ prātaḥsavane nabhākena valaṃ nabhayanti taṃ yan nabhayantīṃ śrathayanty evainaṃ tat tasmāddhotrakāḥ prātaḥsavane nābhākāṃs tṛcāñchaṃsanti | [AB, 6, 24 2]
yaḥ kakubho nidhāraya iti maitrāvaruṇaḥ pūrvīṣṭa indropamātaya iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsī tā hi madhyam bharāṇām ity achāvākaḥ | [AB, 6, 24 3]
ta u tṛtīyasavane vajreṇa vālakhilyābhir vācaḥ kūṭenaikapadayā valaṃ virujya gā āpnuvanti | [AB, 6, 24 4]
pacchaḥ prathamaṃ ṣaḍ vālakhilyānāṃ sūktāni viharaty ardharcaśo dvitīyam ṛkśas tṛtīyaṃ sa paccho viharan pragāthe pragātha evaikapadāṃ dadhyāt sa vācaḥ kūṭaḥ | [AB, 6, 24 5]
tā etāḥ pañcaikapadāś catasro daśamād ahna ekā mahāvratāt | [AB, 6, 24 6]
athāṣṭākṣarāṇi māhānāmanāni padāni teṣāṃ yāvadbhiḥ saṃpadyeta tāvanti śaṃsen netarāṇy ādriyeta | [AB, 6, 24 7]
athārdharcaśo viharaṃs tāś caivaikapadāḥ śaṃset tāni caivāṣṭākṣarāṇi māhānāmanāni padāni | [AB, 6, 24 8]
atha ṛkśo viharaṃs tāś caivaikapadāḥ śaṃset tāni caivāṣṭākṣarāṇi māhānāmanāni padāni | [AB, 6, 24 9]
sa yat prathamaṃ ṣaḍ vālakhilyānāṃ sūktāni viharati prāṇaṃ ca tad vācaṃ ca viharati yad dvitīyaṃ cakṣuś ca tan manaś ca viharati yat tṛtīyaṃ śrotraṃ ca tad ātmānaṃ ca viharati tad upāpto vihāre kāma upāpto vajre vālakhilyāsūpāpto vācaḥ kūṭa ekapadāyām upāptaḥ prāṇakﾱptyām | [AB, 6, 24 10]
avihṛtān eva caturtham pragāthāñchaṃsati paśavo vai pragāthāḥ paśūnām avaruddhyai | [AB, 6, 24 11]
nātraikapadāṃ vyavadadhyāt | [AB, 6, 24 12]
yad atraikapadāṃ vyavadadhyād vācaḥ kūṭena yajamānāt paśūn nirhaṇyād ya enaṃ tatra brūyād vācaḥ kūṭena yajamānāt paśūn niravadhīr apaśum enam akar iti śaśvat tathā syāt | [AB, 6, 24 13]
tasmāt tatraikapadāṃ na vyavadadhyāt | [AB, 6, 24 14]
vy evottame sūkte paryasyati sa eva tayor vihāraḥ | [AB, 6, 24 15]
tad etat saubalāya sarpir vātsiḥ śaśaṃsa sa hovāca bhūyiṣṭhān ahaṃ yajamāne paśūn paryagrahaiṣam akaniṣṭhā u mām āgamiṣyantīti tasmai ha yathā mahadbhya ṛtvigbhya evaṃ nināya tad etat paśavyaṃ ca svargyaṃ ca śastraṃ tasmād etacchaṃsati | [AB, 6, 24 16]
{AB, 6, 25}
dūrohaṇaṃ rohati tasyoktam brāhmaṇam | [AB, 6, 25 1]
aindre paśukāmasya rohed aindrā vai paśavaḥ | [AB, 6, 25 2]
taj jāgataṃ syāj jāgatā vai paśavaḥ | [AB, 6, 25 3]
tan mahāsūktaṃ syād bhūyiṣṭheṣv eva tat paśuṣu yajamānam pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 6, 25 4]
barau rohet tan mahāsūktaṃ ca jāgataṃ ca | [AB, 6, 25 5]
aindrāvaruṇe pratiṣṭhākāmasya rohed etaddevatā vā eṣā hotraitatpratiṣṭhā yad aindrāvaruṇā tad enat svāyām eva pratiṣṭhāyām antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 6, 25 6]
yad evaindrāvaruṇaiṣā ha vā atra nivin nividā vai kāmā āpyante sa yady aindrāvaruṇe rohet sauparṇe rohet tad upāpta aindrāvaruṇe kāma upāptaḥ sauparṇe | [AB, 6, 25 7]
{AB, 6, 26}
tad āhuḥ saṃśaṃset ṣaṣṭhe 'hān na samśaṃsait iti | [AB, 6, 26 1]
saṃśaṃsed ity āhuḥ | [AB, 6, 26 2]
katham anyeṣv ahaḥsu saṃśaṃsati katham atra na saṃśaṃsed iti | [AB, 6, 26 3]
atho khalv āhur naiva saṃśaṃset | [AB, 6, 26 4]
svargo vai lokaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahar asamāyī vai svargo lokaḥ kaścid vai svarge loke sametīti sa yat saṃśaṃset samānaṃ tat kuryād atha yan na saṃśaṃsatīṁ tat svargasya lokasya rūpaṃ tasmān na saṃśaṃsed yad eva na saṃśaṃsatīṁ | [AB, 6, 26 5]
ātmā vai stotriyaḥ prāṇā vālakhilyāḥ sa yat saṃśaṃsed etābhyāṃ devatābhyāṃ yajamānasya prāṇān vīyād ya enaṃ tatra brūyād etābhyāṃ devatābhyāṃ yajamānasya prāṇān vyagāt prāṇa enaṃ hāsyatīti śaśvat tathā syāt tasmān na saṃśaṃset | [AB, 6, 26 6]
sa yad īkṣetāśaṃsiṣaṃ vālakhilyā hanta purastād dūrohaṇasya saṃśaṃsānīti no eva tasyāśām iyāt | [AB, 6, 26 7]
taṃ yadi darpa eva vinded upariṣṭād dūrohaṇasyāpi bahūni śatāni śaṃsed yasyo tat kāmāya tathā kuryād atraiva tad upāptam | [AB, 6, 26 8]
aindryo vālakhilyās tāsāṃ dvādaśākṣarāṇi padāni tatra sa kāma upāpto ya aindre jāgate 'thedam aindrāvaruṇaṃ sūktam aindrāvaruṇī paridhānīyā tasmān na saṃśaṃset | [AB, 6, 26 9]
tad āhur yathā vāva stotram evaṃ śastraṃ vihṛtā vālakhilyāḥ śasyante vihṛtāṃ stotrām avihṛtām iti | [AB, 6, 26 10]
vihṛtam iti brūyād aṣṭākṣareṇa dvādaśākṣaram iti | [AB, 6, 26 11]
tad āhur yathā vāva śastram evaṃ yājyā tisro devatāḥ śasyante 'gnirindro varuṇa ity athaindrāvaruṇyā yajati katham agnir anantarita iti | [AB, 6, 26 12]
yo vā agniḥ sa varuṇas tad apy etad ṛṣiṇoktaṃ tvam agne varuṇo jāyase yad iti tad yad evaindrāvaruṇyā yajati tenāgnir anantarito 'nantaritaḥ | [AB, 6, 26 13]
{AB, 6, 27}
śilpāni śaṃsanti | [AB, 6, 27 1]
devaśilpāny eteṣām vai śilpānām anukṛtīha śilpam adhigamyate hastī kaṃso vāso hiraṇyam aśvatarīrathaḥ śilpam | [AB, 6, 27 2]
śilpaṃ hāsminn adhigamyate ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 27 3]
yad eva śilpānīn | [AB, 6, 27 4]
ātmasaṃskṛtir vāva śilpāni chandomayaṃ vā etair yajamāna ātmānaṃ saṃskurute | [AB, 6, 27 5]
nābhānediṣṭhaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 27 6]
reto vai nābhānediṣṭho retas tat siñcati | [AB, 6, 27 7]
tam aniruktaṃ śaṃsaty aniruktaṃ vai reto guhā yonyāṃ sicyate | [AB, 6, 27 8]
sa retomiśro bhavati kṣmayā retaḥ saṃjagmāno niṣiñcad iti retaḥsamṛddhyā eva | [AB, 6, 27 9]
taṃ sanārāśaṃsaṃ śaṃsati prajā vai naro vāk śaṃsaḥ prajāsv eva tad vācaṃ dadhāti tasmād imāḥ prajā vadantyo jāyante | [AB, 6, 27 10]
taṃ haike purastāc chaṃsanti purastādāyatanā vāg iti vadantaḥ | [AB, 6, 27 11]
upariṣṭād eka upariṣṭādāyatanā vāg iti vadantaḥ | [AB, 6, 27 12]
madhya eva śaṃsen madhyāyatanā vā iyaṃ vāk | [AB, 6, 27 13]
upariṣṭānnedīyasīvopariṣṭān nedīyasīva vā iyaṃ vāk | [AB, 6, 27 14]
taṃ hotā retobhūtaṃ siktvā maitrāvaruṇāya samprayacchaty etasya tvam prāṇān kalpayeti | [AB, 6, 27 15]
{AB, 6, 28}
vālakhilyāḥ śaṃsati prāṇā vai vālakhilyāḥ prāṇān evāsya tat kalpayati | [AB, 6, 28 1]
tā vihṛtāḥ śaṃsati vihṛtā vā ime prāṇāḥ prāṇenāpāno 'pānena vyānaḥ | [AB, 6, 28 2]
sa pacchaḥ prathame sūkte viharaty ardharcaśo dvitīye ṛkśas tṛtīye | [AB, 6, 28 3]
sa yat prathame sūkte viharati prāṇaṃ ca tad vācaṃ ca viharati yad dvitīye cakṣuśca tan manaś ca viharati yat tṛtīye śrotraṃ ca tad ātmānaṃ ca viharati | [AB, 6, 28 4]
te haike saha bṛhatyau saha satobṛhatyau viharanti tad upāpto vihāre kāmo net tu pragāthāḥ kalpante | [AB, 6, 28 5]
atimarśam eva viharet tathā vai pragāthāḥ kalpante pragāthā vai vālakhilyās tasmād atimarśam eva vihared yad evātimarśām | [AB, 6, 28 6]
ātmā vai bṛhatī prāṇāḥ satobṛhatī sa bṛhatīm aśaṃsīt sa ātmātha satobṛhatīṃ te prāṇā atha bṛhatīm atha satobṛhatīṃ tad ātmānam prāṇaiḥ paribṛhann eti tasmād atimarśam eva viharet | [AB, 6, 28 7]
yad v evātimarśām ātmā vai bṛhatī paśavaḥ satobṛhatī sa bṛhatīm aśaṃsīt sa ātmātha satobṛhatīṃ te paśavo 'tha bṛhatīm atha satobṛhatīṃ tad ātmānam paśubhiḥ paribṛhann eti tasmād atimarśam eva viharet | [AB, 6, 28 8]
vy evottame sūkte paryasyati sa eva tayor vihāraḥ | [AB, 6, 28 9]
tasya maitrāvaruṇaḥ prāṇān kalpayitvā brāhmaṇācchaṃsine samprayacchaty etaṃ tvam prajanayeti | [AB, 6, 28 10]
{AB, 6, 29}
sukīrtiṃ śaṃsati devayonir vai sukīrtis tad yajñād devayonyai yajamānam prajanayati | [AB, 6, 29 1]
vṛṣākapiṃ śaṃsaty ātmā vai vṛṣākapir ātmānam evāsya tat kalpayati | [AB, 6, 29 2]
taṃ nyūṅkhayaty annaṃ vai nyūṅkhas tad asmai jātāyānnādyam pratidadhāti yathā kumārāya stanam | [AB, 6, 29 3]
sa pāṅkto bhavati pāṅkto 'yam puruṣaḥ pañcadhā vihito lomāni tvaṅ māṃsam asthi majjā sa yāvān eva puruṣas tāvantaṃ yajamānaṃ saṃskaroti | [AB, 6, 29 4]
tam brāhmaṇācchaṃsī janayitvāchāvākāya samprayacchaty etasya tvam pratiṣṭhāṃ kalpayeti | [AB, 6, 29 5]
{AB, 6, 30}
evayāmarutaṃ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhā vā evayāmarut pratiṣṭhām evāsya tat kalpayati | [AB, 6, 30 1]
taṃ nyūṅkhayaty annaṃ vai nyūṅkho 'nnādyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti | [AB, 6, 30 2]
sa jāgato vātijāgato vā sarvaṃ vā idaṃ jāgataṃ vātijāgataṃ vā | [AB, 6, 30 3]
sa u māruta āpo vai maruta āpo 'nnam abhipūrvam evāsmiṃs tad annādyaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 6, 30 4]
tāny etāni sahacarāṇīty ācakṣate nābhānediṣṭhaṃ vālakhilyā vṛṣākapim evayāmarutaṃ tāni saha vā śaṃset saha vā na śaṃset | [AB, 6, 30 5]
yad enāni nānā śaṃsed yathā puruṣaṃ vā reto vā vicchindyāt tādṛk tat tasmād enāni saha vā śaṃset saha vā na śaṃset | [AB, 6, 30 6]
sa ha bulila āśvatara āśvir vaiśvajito hotā sann īkṣāṃcakra eṣāṃ vā eṣāṃ śilpānāṃ viśvajiti sāṃvatsarike dve madhyaṃdinam abhi pratyetor hantāham ittham evayāmarutaṃ śaṃsayānīti taddha tathā śaṃsayāṃcakāra | [AB, 6, 30 7]
taddha tathā śasyamāne gauśla ājagāma sa hovāca hotaḥ kathā te śastraṃ vicakram plavata iti | [AB, 6, 30 8]
kiṃ hy abhūd iti | [AB, 6, 30 9]
evayāmarud ayam uttarataḥ śasyata iti sa hovācaindro vai madhyaṃdinaḥ kathendram madhyaṃdinān ninīṣasīti | [AB, 6, 30 10]
nendram madhyaṃdinān ninīṣāmīti hovāca | [AB, 6, 30 11]
chandas tv idam amadhyaṃdinasācy ayaṃ jāgato vātijāgato vā sarvaṃ vā idaṃ jāgataṃ vātijāgataṃ vā sa u māruto maiva śaṃsiṣṭeti | [AB, 6, 30 12]
sa hovācāramāchāvākety atha hāsminn anuśāsanam īṣe | [AB, 6, 30 13]
sa hovācaindram eṣa viṣṇunyaṅgaṃ śaṃsatv atha tvam etaṃ hotar upariṣṭād raudryai dhāyyāyai purastān mārutasyāpy asyāthā iti | [AB, 6, 30 14]
taddha tathā śaṃsayāṃcakāra tad idam apy etarhi tathaiva śasyate | [AB, 6, 30 15]
{AB, 6, 31}
tad āhur yad asmin viśvajity atirātra evaṃ ṣaṣṭhe 'hani kalpate yajñaḥ kalpate yajamānasya prajātiḥ katham atrāśasta eva nābhānediṣṭho bhavaty atha maitrāvaruṇo vālakhilyāḥ śaṃsati te prāṇā reto vā agre 'tha prāṇā evam brāhmaṇācchaṃsy aśasta eva nābhānediṣṭho bhavaty atha vṛṣākapiṃ śaṃsati sa ātmā reto vā agre 'thātmā katham atra yajamānasya prajātiḥ katham prāṇā avikﾱptā bhavantīti | [AB, 6, 31 1]
yajamānaṃ ha vā etena sarveṇa yajñakratunā saṃskurvanti sa yathā garbho yonyām antar evaṃ sambhavañchete na vai sakṛd evāgre sarvaḥ sambhavaty ekaikaṃ vā aṅgaṃ sambhavataḥ sambhavatīti | [AB, 6, 31 2]
sarvāṇi cet samāne 'han kriyeran kalpata eva yajñaḥ kalpate yajamānasya prajātir athaitaṃ hotaivayāmarutaṃ tṛtīyasavane śaṃsati tad yāsya pratiṣṭhā tasyām evainaṃ tad antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 6, 31 3]
{AB, 6, 32}
chandasāṃ vai ṣaṣṭhenāhnāptānāṃ raso 'tyanedat sa prajāpatir abibhet parāṅ ayaṃ chandasāṃ raso lokān atyeṣyatīti tam parastāc chandobhiḥ paryagṛhṇān nārāśaṃsyā gāyatryā raibhyā triṣṭubhaḥ pārikṣityā jagatyāḥ kāravyayānuṣṭubhas tat punaś chandassu rasam adadhāt | [AB, 6, 32 1]
sarasair hāsya chandobhir iṣṭam bhavati sarasaiś chandobhir yajñaṃ tanute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 32 2]
nārāśaṃsīḥ śaṃsati prajā vai naro vāk śaṃsaḥ prajāsv eva tad vācaṃ dadhāti tasmād imāḥ prajā vadantyo jāyante ya evaṃ veda yad eva nārāśaṃsīḥ | [AB, 6, 32 3]
śaṃsanto vai devāś ca ṛṣayaś ca svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānāḥ śaṃsanta eva svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti | [AB, 6, 32 4]
tāḥ pragrāhaṃ śaṃsati yathā vṛṣākapiṃ vārṣākapaṃ hi vṛṣākapes tan nyāyam eti | [AB, 6, 32 5]
tāsu na nyūṅkhayen nīvaiva nardet sa hi tāsāṃ nyūṅkhaḥ | [AB, 6, 32 6]
raibhīḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 32 7]
rebhanto vai devāś ca ṛṣayaś ca svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā rebhanta eva svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti | [AB, 6, 32 8]
tāḥ pragrāhaṃ śaṃsati yathā vṛṣākapiṃ vārṣākapaṃ hi vṛṣākapes tan nyāyam eti tāsu na nyūṅkhayen nīvaiva nardet sa hi tāsāṃ nyūṅkhaḥ | [AB, 6, 32 9]
pārikṣitīḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 32 10]
agnir vai parikṣid agnir hīmāḥ prajāḥ parikṣety agniṃ hīmāḥ prajāḥ parikṣiyanti | [AB, 6, 32 11]
agner eva sāyujyaṃ sarūpatāṃ salokatām aśnute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 32 12]
yad eva pārikṣitīḥ | [AB, 6, 32 13]
saṃvatsaro vai parikṣit saṃvatsaro hīmāḥ prajāḥ parikṣeti saṃvatsaraṃ hīmāḥ prajāḥ parikṣiyanti | [AB, 6, 32 14]
saṃvatsarasyaiva sāyujyaṃ sarūpatāṃ salokatām aśnute ya evaṃ veda tāḥ pragrāhaṃ śaṃsati yathā vṛṣākapiṃ vārṣākapaṃ hi vṛṣākapes tan nyāyam eti tāsu na nyūṅkhayen nīvaiva nardet sa hi tāsāṃ nyūṅkhaḥ | [AB, 6, 32 15]
kāravyāḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 32 16]
devā vai yat kiṃca kalyāṇaṃ karmākurvaṃs tat kāravyābhir āpnuvaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā yat kiṃca kalyāṇaṃ karma kurvanti tat kāravyābhir āpnuvanti | [AB, 6, 32 17]
tāḥ pragrāhaṃ śaṃsati yathā vṛṣākapiṃ vārṣākapaṃ hi vṛṣākapes tan nyāyam eti tāsu na nyūṅkhayet nīvīva nardet sa hi tāsāṃ nyūṅkhaḥ | [AB, 6, 32 18]
diśāṃ kﾱptīḥ śaṃsati diśa eva tat kalpayati | [AB, 6, 32 19]
tāḥ pañca śaṃsati pañca vā imā diśaś catasras tiraścya ekordhvā | [AB, 6, 32 20]
tāsu na nyūṅkhayen nevaiva ca ninarden ned imā diśo nyūṅkhayānīti | [AB, 6, 32 21]
tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 32 22]
janakalpāḥ śaṃsati prajā vai janakalpā diśa eva tat kalpayitvā tāsu prajāḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati | [AB, 6, 32 23]
tāsu na nyūṅkhayen nevaiva ca ninarden ned imāḥ prajā nyūṅkhayānīti tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 32 24]
indragāthāḥ śaṃsatīndragāthābhir vai devā asurān abhigāyāthainān atyāyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā indragāthābhir evāpriyam bhrātṛvyam abhigāyāthainam atiyanti | [AB, 6, 32 25]
tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 32 26]
{AB, 6, 33}
aitaśapralāpaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 33 1]
aitaśo ha vai munir agner āyur dadarśa yajñasyāyātayāmam iti haika āhuḥ so 'bravīt putrān putrakā agner āyur adarśaṃ tad abhilapiṣyāmi yat kiṃca vadāmi tan me mā parigāteti sa pratyapadyataitā aśvā āplavante pratīpam prātisatvanam iti | [AB, 6, 33 2]
tasyābhyagnir aitaśāyana etyākāle 'bhihāya mukham apyagṛhṇād adṛpan naḥ piteti | [AB, 6, 33 3]
taṃ hovācāpehy alaso 'bhūr yo me vācam avadhīḥ śatāyuṃ gām akariṣyaṃ sahasrāyum puruṣam pāpiṣṭhāṃ te prajāṃ karomi yo mettham asakthā iti | [AB, 6, 33 4]
tasmād āhur abhyagnaya aitaśāyanā aurvāṇām pāpiṣṭhā iti | [AB, 6, 33 5]
taṃ haike bhūyāṃsaṃ śaṃsanti | [AB, 6, 33 6]
sa na niṣedhed yāvatkāmaṃ śaṃsety eva brūyād āyur vā aitaśapralāpaḥ | [AB, 6, 33 7]
āyur eva tad yajamānasya pratārayati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 33 8]
yad evaitaśapralāpāḥ | [AB, 6, 33 9]
chandasāṃ haiṣa raso yad aitaśapralāpaś chandassv eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 6, 33 10]
sarasair hāsya chandobhir iṣṭam bhavati sarasaiś chandobhir yajñaṃ tanute ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 6, 33 11]
yad v evaitaśapralāpāḥ | [AB, 6, 33 12]
ayātayāmā vā akṣitir aitaśapralāpo 'yātayāmā me yajñe 'sad akṣitir me yajñe 'saditi | [AB, 6, 33 13]
taṃ vā etam aitaśapralāpaṃ śaṃsati padāvagrāhaṃ yathā nividam | [AB, 6, 33 14]
tasyottamena padena praṇauti yathā nividaḥ | [AB, 6, 33 15]
pravalhikāḥ śaṃsati pravalhikābhir vai devā asurān pravalhyāthainān atyāyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānāḥ pravalhikābhir evāpriyam bhrātṛvyam pravalhyāthainam atiyanti | [AB, 6, 33 16]
tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 33 17]
ājijñāsenyāḥ śaṃsaty ājijñāsenyābhir vai devā asurān ājñāyāthainān atyāyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā ājijñāsenyābhir evāpriyam bhrātṛvyam ājñāyāthainam atiyanti tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 33 18]
