pratirādhaṃ śaṃsati pratirādhena vai devā asurān pratirādhyāthainān atyāyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānāḥ pratirādhenaivāpriyam bhrātṛvyam pratirādhyāthainam atiyanti | [AB, 6, 33 19]
ativādaṃ śaṃsaty ativādena vai devā asurān atyudyāthainān atyāyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā ativādenaivāpriyam bhrātṛvyam atyudyāthainam atiyanti tam ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 33 20]
{AB, 6, 34}
deyanīthaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 34 1]
ādityāś ca ha vā aṅgirasaś ca svarge loke 'spardhanta vayam pūrva eṣyāmo vayam iti te hāṅgirasaḥ pūrve śvaḥsutyāṃ svargasya lokasya dadṛśus te 'gnim prajighyur aṅgirasāṃ vā eko 'gniḥ parehy ādityebhyaḥ śvaḥsutyāṃ svargasya lokasya prabrūhīti te hādityā agnim eva dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥsutyāṃ svargasya lokasya dadṛśus tān etyābravīc chvaḥsutyāṃ vaḥ svargasya lokasya prabrūma iti te hocur atha vayaṃ tubhyaṃ sadyaḥsutyāṃ svargasya lokasya prabrūmas tvayaiva vayaṃ hotrā svargaṃ lokam eṣyāma iti sa tathety uktvā pratyuktaḥ punar ājagāma | [AB, 6, 34 2]
te hocuḥ prāvocāḥ iti prāvocam iti hovācātho me pratiprāvocann iti no hi na pratyajñāsthāḥ iti prati vā ajñāsam iti hovāca | [AB, 6, 34 3]
yaśasā vā eṣo 'bhyaiti ya ārtvijyena taṃ yaḥ pratirundhed yaśaḥ sa pratirundhet tasmān na pratyarautsīti | [AB, 6, 34 4]
yadi tv asmād apojjigāṃsed yajñenāsmād apodiyāt yadi yadi tv ayājyaḥ svayam apoditaṃ tasmāt | [AB, 6, 34 5]
{AB, 6, 35}
te hādityān aṅgiraso 'yājayaṃs tebhyo yājayadbhya imām pṛthivīm pūrṇāṃ dakṣiṇānām adadus tān iyam pratigṛhītātapat tāṃ nyavṛñjan sā siṃhī bhūtvā vijṛmbhantī janān acarat tasyāḥ śocatyā ime pradarāḥ prādīryanta ye 'syā ime pradarāḥ sameva haiva tataḥ purā | [AB, 6, 35 1]
tasmād āhur na nivṛttadakṣiṇām pratigṛhṇīyān nenmā śucā viddhā śucā vidhyād iti | [AB, 6, 35 2]
yadi tv enām pratigṛhṇīyād apriyāyainām bhrātṛvyāya dadyāt parā haiva bhavati | [AB, 6, 35 3]
atha yo 'sau tapatīṁ eṣo 'śvaḥ śveto rūpaṃ kṛtvāśvābhidhānyapihitenātmanā praticakrama imaṃ vo nayāma iti sa eṣa devanītho 'nūcyate | [AB, 6, 35 4]
ādityā ha jaritar aṅgirobhyo dakṣiṇām anayan | [AB, 6, 35 5]
tāṃ ha jaritar na pratyāyann iti na hi ta imām pratyāyan | [AB, 6, 35 6]
tām u ha jaritaḥ pratyāyann iti prati hi te 'mum āyan | [AB, 6, 35 7]
tāṃ ha jaritar na pratyagṛbhṇann iti na hi ta imām pratyagṛbhṇan | [AB, 6, 35 8]
tām u ha jaritaḥ pratyagṛbhṇann iti prati hi te 'mum agṛbhṇan | [AB, 6, 35 9]
ahā ned asann avicetanānīty eṣa ha vā ahnāṃ vicetayitā | [AB, 6, 35 10]
yajñā ned asann apurogavāsa iti dakṣiṇā vai yajñānām purogavī yathā ha vā idam ano 'purogavaṃ riṣyaty evaṃ haiva yajño 'dakṣiṇo riṣyati tasmād āhur dātavyaiva yajñe dakṣiṇā bhavaty apy alpikāpi | [AB, 6, 35 11]
uta śveta āśupatvā | [AB, 6, 35 12]
uto padyābhir javiṣṭhaḥ | [AB, 6, 35 13]
utem āśu mānam piparti | [AB, 6, 35 14]
ādityā rudrā vasavas tveﾱate | [AB, 6, 35 15]
idaṃ rādhaḥ pratigṛbhṇīhy aṅgira iti pratigraham eva tad rādhasa aicchan | [AB, 6, 35 16]
idaṃ rādho bṛhat pṛthu | [AB, 6, 35 17]
devā dadatv ā varam | [AB, 6, 35 18]
tad vo astu sucetanam | [AB, 6, 35 19]
yuṣme astu dive dive | [AB, 6, 35 20]
praty eva gṛbhāyateti praty evainaṃ tad ajagrabhaiṣan | [AB, 6, 35 21]
taṃ vā etaṃ devanīthaṃ śaṃsati padāvagrāhaṃ yathā nividaṃ tasyottamena padena praṇauti yathā nividaḥ | [AB, 6, 35 22]
{AB, 6, 36}
bhūtechadaḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 36 1]
bhūtechadbhir vai devā asurān upāsacantoteva yuddhenoteva māyayā teṣāṃ vai devā asurāṇām bhūtechadbhir eva bhūtaṃ chādayitvāthainān atyāyaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā bhūtechadbhir evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya bhūtaṃ chādayitvāthainam atiyanti | [AB, 6, 36 2]
tā ardharcaśaḥ śaṃsati pratiṣṭhāyā eva | [AB, 6, 36 3]
ahanasyāḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 36 4]
āhanasyād vai retaḥ sicyate retasaḥ prajāḥ prajāyante prajātim eva tad dadhāti | [AB, 6, 36 5]
tā daśa śaṃsati daśākṣarā virāﾱ annaṃ virāﾱ annād retaḥ sicyate retasaḥ prajāḥ prajāyante prajātim eva tad dadhāti | [AB, 6, 36 6]
tā nyūṅkhayaty annaṃ vai nyūṅkho 'nnād retaḥ sicyate retasaḥ prajāḥ prajāyante prajātim eva tad dadhāti | [AB, 6, 36 7]
dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣam iti dādhikrīṃ śaṃsati devapavitraṃ vai dadhikrā idaṃ vā idaṃ vyāhanasyāṃ vācam avādīt tad devapavitreṇa vācam punīte | [AB, 6, 36 8]
sānuṣṭub bhavati vāg vā anuṣṭup tat svena chandasā vācam punīte | [AB, 6, 36 9]
sutāso madhumattamā iti pāvamānīḥ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 36 10]
devapavitraṃ vai pāvamānya idaṃ vā idaṃ vyāhanasyāṃ vācam avādīt tad devapavitreṇaiva vācam punīte tā anuṣṭubho bhavanti vāg vā anuṣṭup tat svenaiva chandasā vācam punīte | [AB, 6, 36 11]
ava drapso aṃśumatīm atiṣṭhad ity aindrābārhaspatyaṃ tṛcaṃ śaṃsati | [AB, 6, 36 12]
viśo adevīr abhy ācarantīr bṛhaspatinā yujendraḥ sasāha iti | [AB, 6, 36 13]
asuraviśaṃ ha vai devān abhy udācārya āsīt sa indro bṛhaspatinaiva yujāsuryaṃ varṇam abhidāsantam apāhaṃs tathaivaitad yajamānā indrābṛhaspatibhyām eva yujāsuryaṃ varṇam abhidāsantam apaghnate | [AB, 6, 36 14]
tad āhuḥ saṃśaṃset ṣaṣṭhe 'hān na saṃśaṃsait iti saṃśaṃsed ity āhuḥ katham anyeṣv ahassu saṃśaṃsati katham atra na saṃśaṃsed ity atho khalv āhur naiva saṃśaṃset svargo vai lokaḥ ṣaṣṭham ahar asamāyī vai svargo lokaḥ kaścid vai svarge loke sametīti sa yat saṃśaṃset samānaṃ tat kuryād atha yan na saṃśaṃsatīṁ tat svargasya lokasya rūpaṃ tasmān na saṃśaṃsed yad eva na saṃśaṃsatīṁ | [AB, 6, 36 15]
etāni vā atrokthāni nābhānediṣṭho vālakhilyā vṛṣākapir evayāmarut sa yat saṃśaṃsed apaiva sa eteṣu kāmaṃ rādhnuyāt | [AB, 6, 36 16]
aindro vṛṣākapiḥ sarvāṇi chandāṃsy aitaśapralāpas tatra sa kāma upāpto ya aindre jāgate 'thedam aindrābārhaspatyaṃ sūktam aindrābārhaspatyā paridhānīyā tasmān na saṃśaṃsen na saṃśaṃset | [AB, 6, 36 17]

cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti | [AB, 7, 15 638315_1]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti ha tṛtīyam saṃvatsaram araṇye cacāra | [AB, 7, 15 638315_2]
saḥ araṇyāt grāmam eyāya | [AB, 7, 15 638315_3]
tam indraḥ puruṣa rūpeṇa paryetya uvāca āste bhagaḥ āsīnasya ūrdhvaḥ tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhataḥ śete nipadyamānasya carāti carataḥ bhagaḥ cara eva iti | [AB, 7, 15 638315_4]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti | [AB, 7, 15 638316_1]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti ha caturtham saṃvatsaram araṇye cacāra | [AB, 7, 15 638316_2]
saḥ araṇyāt grāmam eyāya | [AB, 7, 15 638316_3]
tam indraḥ puruṣa rūpeṇa paryetya uvāca kaliḥ śayānaḥ bhavati saṃjihānaḥ tu dvāparaḥ uttiṣṭhan tretā bhavati kṛtam sampadyate caran cara eva iti | [AB, 7, 15 638316_4]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti | [AB, 7, 15 638317_1]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti ha pañcamam saṃvatsaram araṇye cacāra | [AB, 7, 15 638317_2]
saḥ araṇyāt grāmam eyāya | [AB, 7, 15 638317_3]
tam indraḥ puruṣa rūpeṇa paryetya uvāca caran vai madhu vindati caran svādum udumbaram sūryasya paśya śremāṇam yaḥ na tandrayate caran cara eva iti | [AB, 7, 15 638317_4]
cara eva iti | [AB, 7, 15 638317_5]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti | [AB, 7, 15 638318_1]
cara eva iti vai mā brāhmaṇaḥ avocat iti ha ṣaṣṭham saṃvatsaram araṇye cacāra | [AB, 7, 15 638318_2]
saḥ ajīgartam sauyavasim ṛṣim aśanāyā parītam araṇye upeyāya | [AB, 7, 15 638318_3]
tasya ha trayaḥ putrāḥ āsuḥ śunaḥpucchaḥ śunaḥśepaḥ śunolāṅgūlaḥ iti | [AB, 7, 15 638319_1]
tam ha uvāca ṛṣe aham te śatam dadāmi aham eṣām ekena ātmānam niṣkrīṇai iti | [AB, 7, 15 638319_2]
sa jyeṣṭham putram nigṛhṇānaḥ uvāca na nu imam iti na u eva imam iti kaniṣṭham mātā | [AB, 7, 15 638319_3]
tau ha madhyame saṃpādayāṃcakratuḥ śunaḥśepe | [AB, 7, 15 638319_4]
tasya ha śatam dattvā sa tam ādāya saḥ araṇyāt grāmam eyāya | [AB, 7, 15 638319_5]
sa pitaram etya uvāca tata hanta aham anena ātmānam niṣkrīṇai iti | [AB, 7, 15 638320_1]
sa varuṇam rājānam upasasāra anena tvā yajai iti | [AB, 7, 15 638320_2]
anena tvā yajai iti | [AB, 7, 15 638320_3]
tathā iti bhūyān vai brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyāt iti varuṇaḥ uvāca | [AB, 7, 15 638320_4]
tasmai etam rājasūyam yajña kratum provāca | [AB, 7, 15 638320_5]
tam etam abhiṣecanīye puruṣam paśum ālebhe | [AB, 7, 15 638320_6]
{AB, 7, 16}

tasmai upākṛtāya niyoktāram na vividuḥ | [AB, 7, 16 638321_2]

{AB, 7, 17}
tam ṛtvijaḥ ūcuḥ tvam eva naḥ asya ahnaḥ saṃsthām adhigaccha iti | [AB, 7, 17 638334_1]
atha ha etam śunaḥśepaḥ añjaḥsavam dadarśa | [AB, 7, 17 638334_2]
tam etābhiḥ catasṛbhiḥ abhisuṣāva yat cit hi tvam gṛhe gṛhe iti | [AB, 7, 17 638334_3]

atha ha śunaḥśepaḥ viśvāmitrasya aṅkam āsasāda | [AB, 7, 17 638335_1]

tasya ete kāpileya bābhravāḥ | [AB, 7, 17 638335_5]
sa ha uvāca ajīgartaḥ sauyavasiḥ vihvayāvahai iti | [AB, 7, 17 638336_1]
sa ha uvāca ajīgartaḥ sauyavasiḥ āṅgirasaḥ janmanā asi ājīgartiḥ śrutaḥ kaviḥ ṛṣe paitāmahāt tantoḥ mā apagāḥ punar ehi mām iti | [AB, 7, 17 638336_2]
sa ha uvāca śunaḥśepaḥ adarśuḥ tvā śāsa hastam na yat śūdreṣu alapsata gavām trīṇi śatāni tvam avṛṇīthāḥ mat aṅgiraḥ iti | [AB, 7, 17 638336_3]
sa ha uvāca ajīgartaḥ sauyavasiḥ tat vai mā tāta tapati pāpam karma mayā kṛtam tat aham nihnave tubhyam pratiyantu śatāḥ gavām iti | [AB, 7, 17 638337_1]
sa ha uvāca śunaḥśepaḥ yaḥ sakṛt pāpakam kuryāt kuryāt enat tatas aparam na apāgāḥ śaudrāt nyāyāt asaṃdheyam tvayā kṛtam iti | [AB, 7, 17 638337_2]
asaṃdheyam iti ha viśvāmitraḥ upapapāda | [AB, 7, 17 638338_1]

sa ha uvāca śunaḥśepaḥ sa vai yathā naḥ jñapaya rāja putra tathā vada yathā eva āṅgirasaḥ san upeyām tava putra tām iti | [AB, 7, 17 638339_1]
sa ha uvāca viśvāmitraḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ me tvam putrāṇām syāḥ tava śreṣṭhā prajā syāt upeyāḥ daivam me dāyam tena vai tvā upamantraye iti | [AB, 7, 17 638339_2]
sa ha uvāca śunaḥśepaḥ saṃjānāneṣu vai brūyāḥ sauhardyāya me śriyai yathā aham bharata ṛṣabha upeyām tava putra tām iti | [AB, 7, 17 638340_1]
atha ha viśvāmitraḥ putrān āmantrayāmāsa madhuchandāḥ śṛṇotana ṛṣabhaḥ reṇuḥ aṣṭakaḥ ye ke ca bhrātaraḥ sthana asmai jyaiṣṭhyāya kalpadhvam iti | [AB, 7, 17 638340_2]
{AB, 7, 18}

tathā iti mānuṣam | [AB, 7, 18 638353_3]

tasmāt yaḥ rājā vijitī syāt api a yajamānaḥ ākhyāpayeta eva etat śaunaḥśepam ākhyānam | [AB, 7, 18 638354_1]

{AB, 7, 19}
prajāpatiḥ yajñam asṛjata | [AB, 7, 19 638357_1]
yajñam sṛṣṭam anu brahma kṣatre asṛjyetām | [AB, 7, 19 638357_2]
brahma kṣatre anu dvayyaḥ prajāḥ asṛjyanta hutādaḥ ca a huta adaḥ ca brahma eva anu hutādaḥ kṣatram anu a huta adaḥ | [AB, 7, 19 638357_3]

tam kṣatram an anvāpya nyavartata | [AB, 7, 19 638359_1]

atha enam brahma anvait | [AB, 7, 19 638359_3]
tam āpnot | [AB, 7, 19 638359_4]
tam āptvā parastāt nirudhya atiṣṭhat | [AB, 7, 19 638359_5]

atha enat kṣatram anvāgacchat | [AB, 7, 19 638360_1]

tat tathā iti abravīt | [AB, 7, 19 638360_3]

tathā iti | [AB, 7, 19 638360_5]

{AB, 7, 20}
atha atas devayajanasya eva yācñyaḥ | [AB, 7, 20 638361_1]
tat āhuḥ yat brāhmaṇaḥ rājanyaḥ vaiśyaḥ dīkṣiṣyamāṇam kṣatriyam devayajanam yācati kam kṣatriyaḥ yācet iti | [AB, 7, 20 638361_2]
daivam kṣatram yācet iti āhuḥ | [AB, 7, 20 638362_1]
ādityaḥ vai daivam kṣatram | [AB, 7, 20 638362_2]
ādityaḥ eṣām bhūtānām adhipatiḥ | [AB, 7, 20 638362_3]
sa yat ahar dīkṣiṣyamāṇaḥ bhavati tat ahar pūrvāhṇe eva udyantam ādityam upatiṣṭheta idam śreṣṭham jyotiṣām jyotiḥ uttamam | [AB, 7, 20 638363_1]
deva savitar devayajanam me dehi deva yajanam iti devayajanam yācati | [AB, 7, 20 638363_2]

om tathā dadāmi iti ha eva tat āha | [AB, 7, 20 638364_2]
tasya ha na kācana riṣṭiḥ bhavati | [AB, 7, 20 638365_1]
devena savitrā prasūtasya uttarottariṇīm ha śriyam aśnute | [AB, 7, 20 638365_2]
aśnute ha prajānām aiśvaryam ādhipatyam yaḥ evam upasthāya yācitvā devayajanam adhyavasāya dīkṣate kṣatriyaḥ san | [AB, 7, 20 638365_3]
{AB, 7, 21}
atha atas iṣṭāpūrtasya a parijyāniḥ kṣatriyasya yajamānasya | [AB, 7, 21 638366_1]
sa purastāt dīkṣāyāḥ āhutim juhuyāt caturgṛhītam ājyam āhavanīye iṣṭāpūrtasya a parijyānyai punar naḥ indraḥ maghavā dadātu brahma punar iṣṭam pūrtam dāt svāhā iti | [AB, 7, 21 638366_2]
atha anūbandhyāyai samiṣṭa yajuṣām upariṣṭāt punar naḥ agniḥ jātavedāḥ dadātu kṣatram punar iṣṭam pūrtam dāt svāhā iti | [AB, 7, 21 638368_1]
sā eṣā iṣṭāpūrtasya a parijyāniḥ kṣatriyasya yajamānasya yat ete āhutī | [AB, 7, 21 638369_1]
tasmāt ete hotavye | [AB, 7, 21 638369_2]
{AB, 7, 22}
tat u ha sma āha saujātaḥ ārāḍhiḥ ajītapunarvaṇyam vai etat yat ete āhutī iti yathā ha kāmayeta tathā ete kuryāt yaḥ itas anuśāsanam kuryāt iti | [AB, 7, 22 638370_1]
ime tu eva juhuyāt brahma prapadye brahma mā kṣatrāt gopāyatu brahmaṇe svāhā iti | [AB, 7, 22 638370_2]
tat tat iti | [AB, 7, 22 638372_1]
brahma vai eṣa prapadyate yaḥ yajñam prapadyate | [AB, 7, 22 638373_1]
brahma vai yajñaḥ yajñāt u ha vai eṣa punar jāyate yaḥ dīkṣate | [AB, 7, 22 638373_2]
tam brahma prapannam kṣatram na parijināti | [AB, 7, 22 638373_3]
brahma mā kṣatrāt gopāyatu iti āha yathā enam brahma kṣatrāt gopāyet | [AB, 7, 22 638373_4]
brahmaṇe svāhā iti tat enat prīṇāti | [AB, 7, 22 638373_5]
tat enat prītam kṣatrāt gopāyati | [AB, 7, 22 638373_6]
atha anūbandhyāyai samiṣṭa yajuṣām upariṣṭāt kṣatram prapadye kṣatram mā brahmaṇaḥ gopāyatu kṣatrāya svāhā iti | [AB, 7, 22 638374_1]
tat tat iti | [AB, 7, 22 638375_1]
kṣatram vai eṣa prapadyate yaḥ rāṣṭram prapadyate | [AB, 7, 22 638375_2]
kṣatram hi rāṣṭram | [AB, 7, 22 638375_3]
tam kṣatram prapannam brahma na parijināti | [AB, 7, 22 638375_4]
kṣatram mā brahmaṇaḥ gopāyatu iti āha yathā enam kṣatram brahmaṇaḥ gopāyet | [AB, 7, 22 638375_5]
kṣatrāya svāhā iti tat enat prīṇāti | [AB, 7, 22 638375_6]
tat enat prītam brahmaṇaḥ gopāyati | [AB, 7, 22 638375_7]
sā eṣā iṣṭāpūrtasya eva a parijyāniḥ kṣatriyasya yajamānasya yat ete āhutī | [AB, 7, 22 638376_1]
tasmāt ete eva hotavye | [AB, 7, 22 638376_2]
{AB, 7, 23}
atha aindraḥ vai devatayā kṣatriyaḥ bhavati traiṣṭubhaḥ chandasā pañcadaśaḥ stomena somaḥ rājyena rājanyaḥ bandhunā | [AB, 7, 23 638377_1]
sa ha dīkṣamāṇaḥ eva brāhmaṇa tām abhyupaiti yat kṛṣṇājinam adhyūhati yat dīkṣita vratam carati yat enam brāhmaṇāḥ abhisaṃgacchante | [AB, 7, 23 638377_2]
tasya ha dīkṣamāṇasya indraḥ eva indriyam ādatte triṣṭubh vīryam pañcadaśaḥ stomaḥ āyuḥ somaḥ rājyam pitaraḥ yaśaḥ kīrtim anyaḥ vai ayam asmat bhavati brahma vai ayam bhavati brahma vai ayam upāvartate iti vadantaḥ | [AB, 7, 23 638377_3]
sa purastāt dīkṣāyāḥ āhutim hutvā āhavanīyam upatiṣṭheta na indrāt devatāyāḥ emi na triṣṭubhaḥ chandasaḥ na pañcadaśāt stomāt na somāt rājñaḥ na pitryāt bandhoḥ mā me indraḥ indriyam ādita mā triṣṭubh vīryam mā pañcadaśaḥ stomaḥ āyuḥ mā somaḥ rājyam mā pitaraḥ yaśaḥ kīrtim saha indriyeṇa vīryeṇa āyuṣā rājyena yaśasā bandhunā agnim upaimi gāyatrīm chandaḥ trivṛtam stomam somam rājānam brahma prapadye brāhmaṇaḥ bhavāmi iti | [AB, 7, 23 638378_1]
tasya ha na indraḥ indriyam ādatte na triṣṭubh vīryam na pañcadaśaḥ stomaḥ āyuḥ na somaḥ rājyam na pitaraḥ yaśaḥ kīrtim ye evam etām āhutim hutvā āhavanīyam upasthāya dīkṣate kṣatriyaḥ san | [AB, 7, 23 638380_1]
{AB, 7, 24}
atha āgneyaḥ vai devatayā kṣatriyaḥ dīkṣitaḥ bhavati gāyatraḥ chandasā trivṛt stomena brāhmaṇaḥ bandhunā | [AB, 7, 24 638381_1]
sa ha udavasyan eva kṣatriya tām abhyupaiti | [AB, 7, 24 638381_2]
tasya ha udavasyataḥ agniḥ eva tejaḥ ādatte gāyatrī vīryam trivṛt stomaḥ āyuḥ brāhmaṇāḥ brahma yaśaḥ kīrtim anyaḥ vai ayam asmat bhavati kṣatram vai ayam bhavati kṣatram vai ayam upāvartate iti vadantaḥ | [AB, 7, 24 638381_3]
saḥ hutvā āhutim āhavanīyam upatiṣṭheta na agneḥ devatāyāḥ emi na gāyatryāḥ chandasaḥ na trivṛtaḥ stomāt na brahmaṇaḥ bandhoḥ mā me agniḥ tejaḥ ādita mā gāyatrī vīryam mā trivṛt stomaḥ āyuḥ mā brāhmaṇāḥ brahma yaśaḥ kīrtim saha tejasā vīryeṇa āyuṣā brahmaṇā yaśasā kīrtyā indram devatām upaimi triṣṭubham chandaḥ pañcadaśam stomam somam rājānam kṣatram prapadye kṣatriyaḥ bhavāmi devāḥ pitaraḥ pitaraḥ devāḥ yaḥ asmi sa san yaje svam me idam iṣṭam svam pūrtam svam śrāntam svam hutam tasya me ayam agniḥ upadraṣṭā ayam vāyuḥ upaśrotā asau ādityaḥ anukhyātā idam aham yaḥ eva asmi saḥ asmi iti | [AB, 7, 24 638382_1]
tasya ha na agniḥ tejaḥ ādatte na gāyatrī vīryam na trivṛt stomaḥ āyuḥ na brāhmaṇāḥ brahma yaśaḥ kīrtim yaḥ evam etām āhutim hutvā āhavanīyam upasthāya udavasyati kṣatriyaḥ san | [AB, 7, 24 638384_1]
{AB, 7, 25}
atha atas dīkṣāyāḥ āvedanasya eva tat āhuḥ yat brāhmaṇasya dīkṣitasya brāhmaṇaḥ adīkṣiṣṭa iti dīkṣām āvedayanti katham kṣatriyasya āvedayet iti | [AB, 7, 25 638385_1]
yathā eva etat brāhmaṇasya dīkṣitasya brāhmaṇaḥ adīkṣiṣṭa iti dīkṣām āvedayanti evam eva etat kṣatriyasya āvedayet purohitasya ārṣeyeṇa iti | [AB, 7, 25 638386_1]
tat tat iti | [AB, 7, 25 638387_1]
nidhāya vai eṣa svāni āyudhāni brahmaṇaḥ eva āyudhaiḥ brahmaṇaḥ rūpeṇa brahma bhūtvā yajñam upāvartata | [AB, 7, 25 638388_1]
tasmāt tasya purohitasya ārṣeyeṇa dīkṣām āvedayeyuḥ | [AB, 7, 25 638388_2]
purohitasya ārṣeyeṇa pravaram pravṛṇīran | [AB, 7, 25 638388_3]
{AB, 7, 26}
atha atas yajamāna bhāgasya eva tat āhuḥ prāśnīyāt kṣatriyaḥ yajamāna bhāgam na prāśnīyāt iti | [AB, 7, 26 638389_1]
yat prāśnīyāt ahutāt hutam prāśya pāpīyān syāt | [AB, 7, 26 638390_1]
yat na prāśnīyāt yajñāt ātmānam antariyāt | [AB, 7, 26 638390_2]
yajñaḥ vai yajamāna bhāgaḥ | [AB, 7, 26 638390_3]
sa brahmaṇe parihṛtyaḥ | [AB, 7, 26 638391_1]
purohita āyatanam vai etat kṣatriyasya yat brahmā | [AB, 7, 26 638392_1]
ardha ātmā u ha vai eṣa yat purohitaḥ | [AB, 7, 26 638392_2]
upa aha parokṣeṇa eva prāśita rūpam āpnoti | [AB, 7, 26 638392_3]
na asya pratyakṣam bhakṣitaḥ bhavati | [AB, 7, 26 638392_4]
yajñaḥ u ha vai eṣa pratyakṣam yat brahmā | [AB, 7, 26 638393_1]
brahmaṇi hi sarvaḥ yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ yajñe yajamānaḥ | [AB, 7, 26 638393_2]
yajñe eva tat yajñam apyatyarjanti yathā apsu āpaḥ yathā agnau agnim | [AB, 7, 26 638393_3]
tat vai na atiricyate | [AB, 7, 26 638393_4]
tat enam na hinasti | [AB, 7, 26 638393_5]
tasmāt sa brahmaṇe parihṛtyaḥ | [AB, 7, 26 638393_6]
agnau ha eke juhvati prajāpateḥ vibhāt nāma lokaḥ tasmin tvā dadhāmi saha yajamānena svāhā iti | [AB, 7, 26 638394_1]
tat tathā na kuryāt | [AB, 7, 26 638394_2]
yajamānaḥ vai yajamāna bhāgaḥ | [AB, 7, 26 638394_3]
yajamānam ha saḥ agnau pravṛṇakti | [AB, 7, 26 638394_4]
yaḥ enam tatra brūyāt yajamānam agnau prāvārkṣīḥ pra asya agniḥ prāṇān dhakṣyati mariṣyati yajamānaḥ iti śaśvat tathā syāt | [AB, 7, 26 638394_5]
tasmāt tasya āśām na īyāt | [AB, 7, 26 638394_6]
āśām na iyāt | [AB, 7, 26 638394_7]
{AB, 7, 27}
viśvaṃtaraḥ ha sauṣadmanaḥ śyāparṇān paricakṣāṇaḥ viśyāparṇam yajñam ājahre | [AB, 7, 27 638395_1]
tat ha anubudhya śyāparṇāḥ tam yajñam ājagmuḥ | [AB, 7, 27 638395_2]
te ha tat antarvedi āsāṃcakrire | [AB, 7, 27 638395_3]
tān ha dṛṣṭvā uvāca pāpasya vai ime karmaṇaḥ kartāraḥ āsate apūtāyai vācaḥ vaditāraḥ yat śyāparṇāḥ imān utthāpayata ime me antarvedi mā āsiṣata iti | [AB, 7, 27 638395_4]
tathā iti | [AB, 7, 27 638395_5]
tān utthāpayāṃcakruḥ | [AB, 7, 27 638395_6]
te ha utthāpyamānāḥ ruruvire ye tebhyaḥ bhūta vīrebhyaḥ asitamṛgāḥ kaśyapānām soma pītham abhijigyuḥ pārikṣitasya janamejayasya vikaśyape yajñe taiḥ te tatra vīravantaḥ āsuḥ kaḥ svid saḥ asmākaḥ asti vīraḥ yaḥ imam soma pītham abhijeṣyati iti | [AB, 7, 27 638396_1]
ayam aham asmi vaḥ vīraḥ iti ha uvāca rāmaḥ mārgaveyaḥ | [AB, 7, 27 638397_1]
rāmaḥ ha āsa mārgaveyaḥ anūcānaḥ śyāparṇīyaḥ | [AB, 7, 27 638398_1]
teṣām ha uttiṣṭhatām uvāca api nu rājan itthaṃvidam vedeḥ utthāpayanti iti | [AB, 7, 27 638398_2]
yaḥ tvam katham vettha brahmabandho | [AB, 7, 27 638398_3]
{AB, 7, 28}
yatra indram devatāḥ paryavṛñjan viśvarūpam tvāṣṭram abhyamaṃsta vṛtram astṛta yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prādāt arurmaghān avadhīt bṛhaspateḥ pratyavadhīt iti tatra indraḥ soma pīthena vyārdhyata indrasya anu vyṛddhim kṣatram soma pīthena vyārdhyata api indraḥ soma pīthe abhavat tvaṣṭuḥ āmuṣya somam tat vyṛddham adya api kṣatram soma pīthena sa yaḥ tam bhakṣam vidyāt yaḥ kṣatrasya soma pīthena vyṛddhasya yena kṣatram samṛdhyate katham tam vedeḥ utthāpayanti iti | [AB, 7, 28 638399_1]
vettha brāhmaṇa tvam tam bhakṣam | [AB, 7, 28 638400_1]
veda hi iti | [AB, 7, 28 638400_2]
tam vai naḥ brāhmaṇa brūhi iti | [AB, 7, 28 638400_3]
tasmai vai te rājan iti ha uvāca | [AB, 7, 28 638400_4]
{AB, 7, 29}
trayāṇām bhakṣāṇām ekam āhariṣyanti somam vā dadhi vā apaḥ vā | [AB, 7, 29 638401_1]
sa yadi somam brāhmaṇānām sa bhakṣaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638402_1]
brāhmaṇān tena bhakṣeṇa jinviṣyasi | [AB, 7, 29 638402_2]
brāhmaṇa kalpaḥ te prajāyām ājaniṣyate ādāyī āpāyī āvasāyī yathākāma prayāpyaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638402_3]
yadā vai kṣatriyāya pāpam bhavati brāhmaṇa kalpaḥ asya prajāyām ājāyate | [AB, 7, 29 638402_4]
īśvaraḥ ha asmāt dvitīyaḥ vā tṛtīyaḥ vā brāhmaṇa tām abhyupaitoḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638402_5]
sa brahmabandhavena jijyūṣitaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638402_6]
atha yadi dadhi vaiśyānām sa bhakṣaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638403_1]
vaiśyān tena bhakṣeṇa jinviṣyasi | [AB, 7, 29 638403_2]
vaiśya kalpaḥ te prajāyām ājaniṣyate anyasya bali kṛt anyasya adyaḥ yathākāma jyeyaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638403_3]
yadā vai kṣatriyāya pāpam bhavati vaiśya kalpaḥ asya prajāyām ājāyate | [AB, 7, 29 638403_4]
īśvaraḥ ha asmāt dvitīyaḥ vā tṛtīyaḥ vā vaiśya tām abhyupaitoḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638403_5]
sa vaiśya tayā jijyūṣitaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638403_6]
atha yadi apaḥ śūdrāṇām sa bhakṣaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638404_1]
śūdrān tena bhakṣeṇa jinviṣyasi | [AB, 7, 29 638404_2]
śūdra kalpaḥ te prajāyām ājaniṣyate anyasya preṣyaḥ kāma utthāpyaḥ yathākāma vadhyaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638404_3]
yadā vai kṣatriyāya pāpam bhavati śūdra kalpaḥ asya prajāyām ājāyate | [AB, 7, 29 638404_4]
īśvaraḥ ha asmāt dvitīyaḥ vā tṛtīyaḥ vā śūdra tām abhyupaitoḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638404_5]
sa śūdra tayā jijyūṣitaḥ | [AB, 7, 29 638404_6]
{AB, 7, 30}
ete vai te trayaḥ bhakṣāḥ rājan iti ha uvāca yeṣām āśām na iyāt kṣatriyaḥ yajamānaḥ atha asya eṣa svaḥ bhakṣaḥ nyagrodhasya avarodhāḥ ca phalāni ca audumbarāṇi āśvatthāni plākṣāṇi abhiṣuṇuyāt tāni bhakṣayet saḥ asya svaḥ bhakṣaḥ yatas vai adhi devāḥ yajñena iṣṭvā svargam lokam āyan tatra etān camasān nyubjan te nyagrodhāḥ abhavan nyubjāḥ iti ha api enān etarhi ācakṣate kurukṣetre te ha prathama jāḥ nyagrodhānām tebhyaḥ ha anye adhijātāḥ te yat nyañcaḥ arohan tasmāt nyaṅ rohati nyak rohaḥ nyak rohaḥ vai nāma tam nyak roham santam nyagrodhaḥ iti ācakṣate parokṣeṇa parokṣa priyāḥ iva hi devāḥ | [AB, 7, 30 638405_1]
{AB, 7, 31}
teṣām yaḥ camasānām rasaḥ avāṅ ait te avarodhāḥ abhavan atha yaḥ ūrdhvaḥ tāni phalāni eṣa ha vāva kṣatriyaḥ svāt bhakṣāt na eti yaḥ nyagrodhasya avarodhān ca phalāni ca bhakṣayati upa aha parokṣeṇa eva soma pītham āpnoti na asya pratyakṣam bhakṣitaḥ bhavati parokṣam iva ha vai eṣa somaḥ rājā yat nyagrodhaḥ parokṣam iva eṣa brahmaṇaḥ rūpam upanigacchati yat kṣatriyaḥ purodhayā eva dīkṣayā eva pravareṇa eva kṣatram vai etat vanaspatīnām yat nyagrodhaḥ kṣatram rājanyaḥ nitataḥ iva hi iha kṣatriyaḥ rāṣṭre vasan bhavati pratiṣṭhitaḥ iva nitataḥ iva nyagrodhaḥ avarodhaiḥ bhūmyām pratiṣṭhitaḥ iva tat yat kṣatriyaḥ yajamānaḥ nyagrodhasya avarodhān ca phalāni ca bhakṣayati ātmani eva tat kṣatram vanaspatīnām pratiṣṭhāpayati kṣatre ātmānam ha vai ātmani kṣatram vanaspatīnām pratiṣṭhāpayati nyagrodhaḥ iva avarodhaiḥ bhūmyām prati rāṣṭre tiṣṭhati ugram ha asya rāṣṭram a vyathyam bhavati yaḥ evam etam bhakṣam bhakṣayati kṣatriyaḥ yajamānaḥ | [AB, 7, 31 638409_1]
{AB, 7, 32}
atha yat audumbarāṇi ūrjaḥ vai eṣaḥ annādyāt vanaspatiḥ ajāyata yat udumbaraḥ bhaujyam vai etat vanaspatīnām ūrjam eva asmin tat annādyam ca bhaujyam ca vanaspatīnām kṣatre dadhāti atha yat āśvatthāni tejasaḥ vai eṣa vanaspatiḥ ajāyata yat aśvatthaḥ sāmrājyam vai etat vanaspatīnām tejaḥ eva asmin tat sāmrājyam ca vanaspatīnām kṣatre dadhāti atha yat plākṣāṇi yaśasaḥ vai eṣa vanaspatiḥ ajāyata yat plakṣaḥ svārājyam ca ha vai etat vairājyam ca vanaspatīnām yaśaḥ eva asmin tat svārājya vairājye ca vanaspatīnām kṣatre dadhāti etāni asya purastāt upakﾱptāni bhavanti atha somam rājānam krīṇanti te rājñaḥ eva āvṛtā upavasathāt prativeśaiḥ caranti atha aupavasathyam ahar etāni adhvaryuḥ purastāt upakalpayeta adhiṣavaṇam carma adhiṣavaṇe phalake droṇakalaśam daśāpavitram adrīn pūtabhṛtam ca ādhavanīyam ca sthālīm udañcanam camasam ca tat yat etat rājānam prātar abhiṣuṇvanti tat enāni dvedhā vigṛhṇīyāt abhi anyāni sunuyāt mādhyaṃdināya anyāni pariśiṃṣyāt | [AB, 7, 32 638414_1]
{AB, 7, 33}
tat yatra etān camasān unnayeyuḥ tat etam yajamāna camasam unnayet tasmin dve darbha taruṇake prāste syātām tayoḥ vaṣaṭkṛte antaḥparidhi pūrvam prāsyet dadhikrāvṇaḥ akāriṣam iti etayā ṛcā sa svāhākārayā anuvaṣaṭkṛte aparam ā dadhikrāḥ śavasā pañca kṛṣṭīḥ iti tat yatra etān camasān āhareyuḥ tat etam yajamāna camasam āharet tān yatra udgṛhṇīyuḥ tat enam upodgṛhṇīyāt tat yadā iḍām hotā upahvayeta yadā camasam bhakṣayet atha enam etayā bhakṣayet yat atra śiṣṭam rasinaḥ sutasya yat indraḥ apibat śacībhiḥ idam tat asya manasā śivena somam rājānam iha bhakṣayāmi iti śivaḥ ha vai asmai eṣa vānaspatyaḥ śivena manasā bhakṣitaḥ bhavati ugram ha asya rāṣṭram avyathyam bhavati yaḥ evam etam bhakṣam bhakṣayati kṣatriyaḥ yajamānaḥ śam naḥ edhi hṛde pītaḥ pra naḥ āyuḥ jīvase soma tārīḥ iti ātmanaḥ pratyabhimarśaḥ īśvaraḥ ha vai eṣaḥ a pratyabhimṛṣṭaḥ manuṣyasya āyuḥ pratyavahartoḥ an arhan mā bhakṣayati iti tat yat etena ātmānam abhimṛśati āyuḥ eva tat pratirate āpyāyasva sametu te sam te payāṃsi sam u yantu vājāḥ iti camasam āpyāyayati abhirūpābhyām yat yajñe abhirūpam tat samṛddham | [AB, 7, 33 638418_1]
{AB, 7, 34}
tat yatra etān camasān sādayeyuḥ tat etam yajamāna camasam sādayet tān yatra prakampayeyuḥ tat enam anuprakampayet atha enam āhṛtam bhakṣayet narāśaṃsa pītasya deva soma te mati vidaḥ ūmaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ bhakṣitasya bhakṣayāmi iti prātaḥsavane nārāśaṃsaḥ bhakṣaḥ ūrvaiḥ iti mādhyaṃdine kāvyaiḥ iti tṛtīyasavane ūmāḥ vai pitaraḥ prātaḥsavane ūrvāḥ mādhyaṃdine kāvyāḥ tṛtīyasavane tat etat pitṝn eva amṛtān savana bhājaḥ karoti sarvaḥ ha eva saḥ amṛtaḥ iti ha sma āha priyavrataḥ somāpaḥ yaḥ kaḥ ca savana bhāj iti amṛtāḥ ha vai asya pitaraḥ savana bhājaḥ bhavanti ugram ha asya rāṣṭram avyathyam bhavati yaḥ evam etam bhakṣam bhakṣayati kṣatriyaḥ yajamānaḥ samānaḥ ātmanaḥ pratyabhimarśaḥ samānam āpyāyanam camasasya prātaḥsavanasya eva āvṛtā prātaḥsavane careyuḥ mādhyaṃdinasya mādhyaṃdine tṛtīyasavanasya tṛtīyasavane | [AB, 7, 34 638425_1]
tam evam etam bhakṣam provāca rāmaḥ mārgaveyaḥ viśvaṃtarāya sauṣadmanāya | [AB, 7, 34 638431_1]
tasmin ha uvāca prokte sahasram u ha brāhmaṇa tubhyam dadmaḥ saśyāparṇaḥ u me yajñaḥ iti | [AB, 7, 34 638432_1]
etam u ha eva provāca turaḥ kāvaṣeyaḥ janamejayāya pārikṣitāya etam u ha eva procatuḥ parvata nāradau somakāya sāhadevyāya sahadevāya sārñjayāya babhrave daivāvṛdhāya bhīmāya vaidarbhāya nagnajite gāndhārāya etam u ha eva provāca agniḥ sanaśrutāya ariṃdamāya kratuvide jānakaye etam u ha eva provāca vasiṣṭhaḥ sudāse paijavanāya | [AB, 7, 34 638433_1]
te ha te sarve eva mahat jagmuḥ etam bhakṣam bhakṣayitvā | [AB, 7, 34 638433_2]
sarve ha eva mahā rājā āsuḥ | [AB, 7, 34 638433_3]
ādityaḥ iva ha sma śriyām pratiṣṭhitāḥ tapanti sarvābhyaḥ digbhyaḥ balim āvahantaḥ | [AB, 7, 34 638433_4]
ādityaḥ iva ha vai śriyām pratiṣṭhitaḥ tapati | [AB, 7, 34 638434_1]
sarvābhyaḥ digbhyaḥ balim āvahati | [AB, 7, 34 638434_2]
ugram ha asya rāṣṭram avyathyam bhavati yaḥ evam etam bhakṣam bhakṣayati kṣatriyaḥ yajamānaḥ yajamānaḥ | [AB, 7, 34 638434_3]
{AB, 8, 1}
athātaḥ stutaśastrayor eva | [AB, 8, 1 1]
aikāhikam prātaḥsavanam aikāhikaṃ tṛtīyasavanam ete vai śānte kﾱpte pratiṣṭhite savane yad aikāhike śāntyai kﾱptyai pratiṣṭhityā apracyutyai | [AB, 8, 1 2]
ukto mādhyaṃdinaḥ pavamāno ya ubhayasāmno bṛhatpṛṣṭhasyobhe hi sāmanī kriyete | [AB, 8, 1 3]
ā tvā rathaṃ yathotaya idaṃ vaso sutam andha iti rāthaṃtarī pratipad rāthaṃtaro 'nucaraḥ pavamānokthaṃ vā etad yan marutvatīyam pavamāne vā atra rathaṃtaraṃ kurvanti bṛhat pṛṣṭhaṃ savīvadhatāyai tad idaṃ rathaṃtaraṃ stutam ābhyām pratipadanucarābhyām anuśaṃsati | [AB, 8, 1 4]
atho brahma vai rathaṃtaraṃ kṣatraṃ bṛhad brahma khalu vai kṣatrāt pūrvam brahmapurastān ma ugraṃ rāṣṭram avyathyam asad ity athānnaṃ vai rathaṃtaram annam evāsmai tat purastāt kalpayaty atheyaṃ vai pṛthivī rathaṃtaram iyaṃ khalu vai pratiṣṭhā pratiṣṭhām evāsmai tat purastāt kalpayati | [AB, 8, 1 5]
samāna indranihavo 'vibhaktaḥ so 'hnām udvān brāhmaṇaspatya ubhayasāmno rūpam ubhe hi sāmanī kriyete | [AB, 8, 1 6]
samānyo dhāyyā avibhaktās tā ahnām | [AB, 8, 1 7]
aikāhiko marutvatīyaḥ pragāthaḥ | [AB, 8, 1 8]
{AB, 8, 2}
janiṣṭhā ugraḥ sahase turāyeti sūktam ugravat sahasvat tat kṣatrasya rūpam mandra ojiṣṭha ity ojasvat tat kṣatrasya rūpam bahulābhimāna ity abhivad abhibhūtyai rūpaṃ tad ekādaśarcam bhavaty ekādaśākṣarā vai triṣṭup traiṣṭubho vai rājanya ojo vā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ triṣṭub ojaḥ kṣatraṃ vīryaṃ rājanyas tad enam ojasā kṣatreṇa vīryeṇa samardhayati tad gaurivītam bhavaty etad vai marutvatīyaṃ samṛddhaṃ yad gaurivītaṃ tasyoktam brāhmaṇam | [AB, 8, 2 1]
tvām iddhi havāmaha iti bṛhatpṛṣṭham bhavati kṣatraṃ vai bṛhat kṣatreṇaiva tat kṣatraṃ samardhayaty atho kṣatraṃ vai bṛhad ātmā yajamānasya niṣkevalyaṃ tad yad bṛhatpṛṣṭham bhavati kṣatraṃ vai bṛhat kṣatreṇaivainaṃ tat samardhayaty atho jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vai bṛhaj jyaiṣṭhyenaivainaṃ tat samardhayaty atho śraiṣṭhyaṃ vai bṛhac chraiṣṭhyenaivainaṃ tat samardhayati | [AB, 8, 2 2]
abhi tvā śūra nonuma iti rathaṃtaram anurūpaṃ kurvanty ayaṃ vai loko rathaṃtaram asau loko bṛhad asya vai lokasyāsau loko 'nurūpo 'muṣya lokasyāyaṃ loko 'nurūpas tad yad rathaṃtaram anurūpaṃ kurvanty ubhāv eva tallokau yajamānāya sambhoginau kurvanty atho brahma vai rathaṃtaraṃ kṣatram bṛhad brahmaṇi khalu vai kṣatram pratiṣṭhitaṃ kṣatre brahmātho sāmna eva sayonitāyai | [AB, 8, 2 3]
yad vāvāneti dhāyyā tasyā uktam brāhmaṇam | [AB, 8, 2 4]
ubhayaṃ śṛṇavac ca na iti sāmapragātha ubhayasāmno rūpam ubhe hi sāmanī kriyete | [AB, 8, 2 5]
{AB, 8, 3}
tam u ṣṭuhi yo abhibhūtyojā iti sūktam abhivad abhibhūtyai rūpam | [AB, 8, 3 1]
aṣāﾱham ugraṃ sahamānam ābhir ity ugravat sahamānavat tat kṣatrasya rūpam | [AB, 8, 3 2]
tat pañcadaśarcam bhavaty ojo vā indriyaṃ vīryam pañcadaśa ojaḥ kṣatraṃ vīryam rājanyas tad enam ojasā kṣatreṇa vīryeṇa samardhayati | [AB, 8, 3 3]
tad bhāradvājam bhavati bhāradvājaṃ vai bṛhad ārṣeyeṇa saloma | [AB, 8, 3 4]
eṣa ha vāva kṣatriyayajñaḥ samṛddho yo bṛhatpṛṣṭhas tasmād yatra kvaca kṣatriyo yajeta bṛhad eva tatra pṛṣṭhaṃ syāt tatsamṛddham | [AB, 8, 3 5]
{AB, 8, 4}
aikāhikā hotrā etā vai śāntāḥ kﾱptāḥ pratiṣṭhitā hotrā yad aikāhikāḥ śāntyai kﾱptyai pratiṣṭhityā apracyutyai tāḥ sarvarūpā bhavanti sarvasamṛddhāḥ sarvarūpatāyai sarvasamṛddhyai sarvarūpābhir hotrābhiḥ sarvasamṛddhābhiḥ sarvān kāmān avāpnavāmeti tasmād yatra kvacaikāhā asarvastomā asarvapṛṣṭhā aikāhikā eva tatra hotrāḥ syus tat samṛddham | [AB, 8, 4 1]
ukthya evāyam pañcadaśaḥ syād ity āhur ojo vā indriyaṃ vīryam pañcadaśa ojaḥ kṣatraṃ vīryaṃ rājanyas tad enam ojasā kṣatreṇa vīryeṇa samardhayati | [AB, 8, 4 2]
tasya triṃśat stutaśastrāṇi bhavanti triṃśadakṣarā vai virāḍ virāḍ annādyaṃ virājy evainaṃ tad annādye pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmāt tadukthyaḥ pañcadaśaḥ syād ity āhuḥ | [AB, 8, 4 3]
jyotiṣṭoma evāgniṣṭomaḥ syāt | [AB, 8, 4 4]
brahma vai stomānāṃ trivṛt kṣatram pañcadaśo brahma khalu vai kṣatrāt pūrvaṃ brahma purastān ma ugraṃ rāṣṭram avyathyam asad iti viśaḥ saptadaśaḥ śaudro varṇa ekaviṃśo viśaṃ caivāsmai tac chaudraṃ ca varṇam anuvartmānau kurvanty atho tejo vai stomānāṃ trivṛd vīryam pañcadaśaḥ prajātiḥ saptadaśaḥ pratiṣṭhaikaviṃśas tad enaṃ tejasā vīryeṇa prajātyā pratiṣṭhayāntataḥ samardhayati tasmāj jyotiṣṭomaḥ syāt | [AB, 8, 4 5]
tasya caturviṃśatiḥ stutaśastrāṇi bhavanti caturviṃśatyardhamāso vai saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsare kṛtsnam annādyaṃ kṛtsna evainaṃ tad annādye pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmāj jyotiṣṭoma evāgniṣṭomaḥ syād agniṣṭomaḥ syāt | [AB, 8, 4 6]
{AB, 8, 5}
athātaḥ punarabhiṣekasyaiva | [AB, 8, 5 1]
sūyate ha vā asya kṣatraṃ yo dīkṣate kṣatriyaḥ san sa yadāvabhṛthād udetyānūbandhyayeṣṭvodavasyaty athainam udavasānīyāyāṃ saṃsthitāyām punar abhiṣiñcanti | [AB, 8, 5 2]
tasyaite purastād eva sambhārā upakﾱptā bhavanty audumbary āsandī tasyai prādeśamātrāḥ pādāḥ syur aratnimātrāṇi śīrṣaṇyānūcyāni mauñjaṃ vivayanaṃ vyāghracarmāstaraṇam audumbaraś camasa udumbaraśākhā tasminn etasmiṃś camase 'ṣṭātayāni niṣutāni bhavanti dadhi madhu sarpir ātapavarṣyā āpaḥ śaṣpāṇi ca tokmāni ca surā dūrvā | [AB, 8, 5 3]
tad yaiṣā dakṣiṇā sphyavartanir veder bhavati tatraitām prācīm āsandīm pratiṣṭhāpayati tasyā antarvedi dvau pādau bhavato bahirvedi dvāv iyaṃ vai śrīs tasyā etat parimitaṃ rūpaṃ yad antarvedy athaiṣa bhūmāparimito yo bahirvedi tad yad asyā antarvedi dvau pādau bhavato bahirvedi dvā ubhayoḥ kāmayor upāptyai yaś cāntarvedi yaś ca bahirvedi | [AB, 8, 5 4]
{AB, 8, 6}
vyāghracarmaṇāstṛṇāty uttaralomnā prācīnagrīveṇa kṣatraṃ vā etad āraṇyānām paśūnāṃ yad vyāghraḥ kṣatraṃ rājanyaḥ kṣatreṇaiva tat kṣatraṃ samardhayati | [AB, 8, 6 1]
tām paścāt prāṅ upaviśyācya jānu dakṣiṇam abhimantrayata ubhābhyām pāṇibhyām ālabhya | [AB, 8, 6 2]
agniṣ ṭvā gāyatryā sayuk chandasārohatu savitoṣṇihā somo 'nuṣṭubhā bṛhaspatir bṛhatyā mitrāvaruṇau paṅktyendras triṣṭubhā viśve devā jagatyā tān aham anu rājyāya sāmrājyāya bhaujyāya svārājyāya vairājyāya pārameṣṭhyāya rājyāya māhārājyāyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyātiṣṭhāyārohāmi | [AB, 8, 6 3]
ity etām āsandīm ārohed dakṣiṇenāgre jānunātha savyena | [AB, 8, 6 4]
tat tad itīṁ | [AB, 8, 6 5]
caturuttarair vai devāś chandobhiḥ sayug bhūtvaitāṃ śriyam ārohan yasyām eta etarhi pratiṣṭhitā agnir gāyatryā savitoṣṇihā somo 'nuṣṭubhā bṛhaspatir bṛhatyā mitrāvaruṇau paṅktyendras triṣṭubhā viśve devā jagatyā | [AB, 8, 6 6]
te ete abhyanūcyete agner gāyatry abhavat sayugveti | [AB, 8, 6 7]
kalpate ha vā asmai yogakṣema uttarottariṇīṃ ha śriyam aśnute 'śnute ha prajānām aiśvaryam ādhipatyaṃ ya evam etā anu devatā etām āsandīm ārohati kṣatriyaḥ san | [AB, 8, 6 8]
athainam abhiṣekṣyann apāṃ śāntiṃ vācayati | [AB, 8, 6 9]
śivena mā cakṣuṣā paśyatāpaḥ śivayā tanvopaspṛśata tvacam me sarvāṁ agnīṃr apsuṣado huve vo mayi varco balam ojo nidhatteti | [AB, 8, 6 10]
naitasyābhiṣiṣicānasyāśāntā āpo vīryaṃ nirhaṇann iti | [AB, 8, 6 11]
{AB, 8, 7}
athainam udumbaraśākhām antardhāyābhiṣiñcati | [AB, 8, 7 1]
imā āpaḥ śivatamā imāḥ sarvasya bheṣajīḥ imā rāṣṭrasya vardhanīr imā rāṣṭrabhṛto 'mṛtāḥ | [AB, 8, 7 2]
yābhir indram abhyaṣiñcat prajāpatiḥ somaṃ rājānaṃ varuṇaṃ yamam manum tābhir adbhir abhiṣiñcāmi tvām ahaṃ rājñāṃ tvam adhirājo bhaveha | [AB, 8, 7 3]
mahāntaṃ tvā mahīnāṃ samrājaṃ carṣaṇīnāṃ devī janitry ajījanad bhadrā janitry ajījanat | [AB, 8, 7 4]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyām pūṣṇo hastābhyām agnes tejasā sūryasya varcasendrasyendriyeṇābhiṣiñcāmi balāya śriyai yaśase 'nnādyāya | [AB, 8, 7 5]
bhūr iti ya icched imam eva praty annam adyād ity atha ya icched dvipuruṣam bhūr bhuva ity atha ya icchet tripuruṣaṃ vāpratimaṃ vā bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti | [AB, 8, 7 6]
taddhaika āhuḥ sarvāptir vā eṣā yad etā vyāhṛtayo 'tisarveṇa hāsya parasmai kṛtam bhavatīti tam etenābhiṣiñced devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyām pūṣṇo hastābhyām agnes tejasā sūryasya varcasendrasyendriyeṇābhiṣiñcāmi balāya śriyai yaśase 'nnādyāyeti | [AB, 8, 7 7]
tad u punaḥ paricakṣate yad asarveṇa vāco 'bhiṣikto bhavatīśvaro ha tu purāyuṣaḥ praitor iti ha smāha satyakāmo jābālo yam etābhir vyāhṛtibhir nābhiṣiñcantīti | [AB, 8, 7 8]
īśvaro ha sarvam āyur aitoḥ sarvam āpnod vijayenety u ha smāhoddālaka āruṇir yam etābhir vyāhṛtibhir abhiṣiñcantīti tam etenaivābhiṣiñced devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyām pūṣṇo hastābhyām agnes tejasā sūryasya varcasendrasyendriyeṇābhiṣiñcāmi balāya śriyai yaśase 'nnādyāya bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti | [AB, 8, 7 9]
athaitāni ha vai kṣatriyād ījānād vyutkrāntāni bhavanti brahmakṣatre ūrg annādyam apām oṣadhīnāṃ raso brahmavarcasam irā puṣṭiḥ prajātiḥ kṣatrarūpaṃ tad atho annasya rasa oṣadhīnāṃ kṣatram pratiṣṭhā tad yad evāmū purastād āhutī juhoti tad asmin brahmakṣatre dadhāti | [AB, 8, 7 10]
{AB, 8, 8}
atha yad audumbary āsandī bhavaty audumbaraś camasa udumbaraśākhorg vā annādyam udumbara ūrjam evāsmiṃs tad annādyaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 8, 8 1]
atha yad dadhi madhu ghṛtam bhavaty apāṃ sa oṣadhīnāṃ raso 'pām evāsmiṃs tad oṣadhīnāṃ rasaṃ dadhāti | [AB, 8, 8 2]
atha yad ātapavarṣyā āpo bhavanti tejaś ca ha vai brahmavarcasaṃ cātapavarṣyā āpas teja evāsmiṃs tad brahmavarcasaṃ ca dadhāti | [AB, 8, 8 3]
atha yacchaṣpāṇi ca tokmāni ca bhavantīrāyai tat puṣṭyai rūpam atho prajātyā irām evāsmiṃs tat puṣṭiṃ dadhāty atho prajātim | [AB, 8, 8 4]
atha yat surā bhavati kṣatrarūpaṃ tad atho annasya rasaḥ kṣatrarūpam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāty atho annasya rasam | [AB, 8, 8 5]
atha yad dūrvā bhavati kṣatraṃ vā etad oṣadhīnāṃ yad dūrvā kṣatraṃ rājanyo nitata iva hīha kṣatriyo rāṣṭre vasan bhavati pratiṣṭhita iva nitateva dūrvāvarodhair bhūmyām pratiṣṭhiteva tad yad dūrvā bhavaty oṣadhīnām evāsmiṃs tat kṣatraṃ dadhāty atho pratiṣṭhām | [AB, 8, 8 6]
etāni ha vai yāny asmād ījānād vyutkrāntāni bhavanti tāny evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti tair evainaṃ tat samardhayati | [AB, 8, 8 7]
athāsmai surākaṃsaṃ hasta ādadhāti | [AB, 8, 8 8]
svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayā pavasva soma dhārayā indrāya pātave sutaḥ | [AB, 8, 8 9]
ity ādhāya śāntiṃ vācayati | [AB, 8, 8 10]
nānā hi vāṃ devahitaṃ sadas kṛtam mā saṃsṛkṣāthām parame vyomani surā tvam asi śuṣmiṇī soma eṣa rājā mainaṃ hiṃsiṣṭaṃ svāṃ yonim āviśantāv iti | [AB, 8, 8 11]
somapīthasya caiṣā surāpīthasya ca vyāvṛttiḥ | [AB, 8, 8 12]
pītvā yaṃ rātim manyeta tasmā enām prayacchet taddhi mitrasya rūpaṃ mitra evaināṃ tad antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayati tathā hi mitre pratitiṣṭhati | [AB, 8, 8 13]
pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda | [AB, 8, 8 14]
{AB, 8, 9}
athodumbaraśākhām abhi pratyavarohaty ūrg vā annādyam udumbara ūrjam eva tad annādyam abhi pratyavarohati | [AB, 8, 9 1]
upary evāsīno bhūmau pādau pratiṣṭhāpya pratyavaroham āha | [AB, 8, 9 2]
pratitiṣṭhāmi dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ pratitiṣṭhāmi prāṇāpānayoḥ pratitiṣṭhāmy ahorātrayoḥ pratitiṣṭhāmy annapānayoḥ prati brahman prati kṣatre praty eṣu triṣu lokeṣu tiṣṭhāmīti | [AB, 8, 9 3]
antataḥ sarveṇātmanā pratitiṣṭhati sarvasmin ha vā etasmin pratitiṣṭhaty uttarottariṇīṃ ha śriyam aśnute 'śnute ha prajānām aiśvaryam ādhipatyaṃ ya evam etena punarabhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ kṣatriyaḥ pratyavarohati | [AB, 8, 9 4]
etena pratyavaroheṇa pratyavarūhyopasthaṃ kṛtvā prāṅ āsīno namo brahmaṇe namo brahmaṇe namo brahmaṇa iti triṣkṛtvo brahmaṇe namaskṛtya varaṃ dadāmi jityā abhijityai vijityai saṃjityā iti vācaṃ visṛjate | [AB, 8, 9 5]
sa yan namo brahmaṇe namo brahmaṇe namo brahmaṇa iti triṣkṛtvo brahmaṇe namaskaroti brahmaṇa eva tat kṣatraṃ vaśam eti tad yatra vai brahmaṇaḥ kṣatraṃ vaśam eti tad rāṣṭraṃ samṛddhaṃ tad vīravad ā hāsmin vīro jāyate | [AB, 8, 9 6]
atha yad varaṃ dadāmi jityā abhijityai vijityai saṃjityā iti vācaṃ visṛjata etad vai vāco jitaṃ yad dadāmīty āha yad eva vāco jitam tan ma idam anu karma saṃtiṣṭhātā iti | [AB, 8, 9 7]
visṛjya vācam upotthāyāhavanīye samidham abhyādadhāti | [AB, 8, 9 8]
samid asi sam v eṅkṣvendriyeṇa vīryeṇa svāheti | [AB, 8, 9 9]
indriyeṇaiva tad vīryeṇātmānam antataḥ samardhayati | [AB, 8, 9 10]
ādhāya samidhaṃ trīṇi padāni prāṅ udaṅṅ abhyutkrāmati | [AB, 8, 9 11]
kﾱptir asi diśām mayi devebhyaḥ kalpata kalpatām me yogakṣemo'bhayam me 'stu | [AB, 8, 9 12]
ity aparājitāṃ diśam upatiṣṭhate jitasyaivāpunaḥparājayāya tat tad itīṁ | [AB, 8, 9 13]
{AB, 8, 10}
devāsurā vā eṣu lokeṣu saṃyetire ta etasyām prācyāṃ diśi yetire tāṃs tato 'surā ajayaṃs te dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi yetire tāṃs tato 'surā ajayaṃs te pratīcyāṃ diśi yetire tāṃs tato 'surā ajayaṃs ta udīcyāṃ diśi yetire tāṃs tato 'surā ajayaṃs ta etasminn avāntaradeśe yetire ya eṣa prāṅ udaṅ te ha tato jigyuḥ | [AB, 8, 10 1]
taṃ yadi kṣatriya upadhāvet senayoḥ samāyatyos tathā me kuru yathāham imāṃ senāṃ jayānīti sa yadi tatheti brūyād vanaspate vīḍvaṅgo hi bhūyā ity asya rathopastham abhimṛśyāthainam brūyāt | [AB, 8, 10 2]
ātiṣṭhasvaitāṃ te diśam abhimukhaḥ saṃnaddho ratho 'bhipravartatāṃ sa udaṅ sa pratyaṅ sa dakṣiṇā sa prāṅ so 'bhy amitraṃ iti | [AB, 8, 10 3]
abhīvartena haviṣety evainam āvartayed athainam anvīkṣetāpratirathena śāsena sauparṇeneti | [AB, 8, 10 4]
jayati ha tāṃ senām | [AB, 8, 10 5]
yady u vā enam upadhāvet saṃgrāmaṃ saṃyatiṣyamāṇas tathā me kuru yathāham imaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ saṃjayānīty etasyām evainaṃ diśi yātayej jayati ha taṃ saṃgrāmam | [AB, 8, 10 6]
yady u vā enam upadhāved rāṣṭrād aparudhyamānas tathā me kuru yathāham idaṃ rāṣṭram punar avagacchānīty etām evainaṃ diśam upaniṣkramayet tathā ha rāṣṭram punar avagacchati | [AB, 8, 10 7]
upasthāyāmitrāṇāṃ vyapanuttim bruvan gṛhān abhyety apa prāca indra viśvāṁ amitrān iti sarvato hāsmā anamitram abhayam bhavaty uttarottariṇīṃ ha śriyam aśnute 'śnute ha prajānām aiśvaryam ādhipatyaṃ ya evam etām amitrāṇāṃ vyapanuttim bruvan gṛhān abhyeti | [AB, 8, 10 8]
etya gṛhān paścād gṛhyasyāgner upaviṣṭāyānvārabdhāya ṛtvig antataḥ kaṃsena caturgṛhītas tisra ājyāhutīr aindrīḥ prapadaṃ juhoty anārtyā ariṣṭyā ajyānyā abhayāya | [AB, 8, 10 9]
{AB, 8, 11}
pary ū ṣu pradhanva vājasātaye pari vṛtrā bhūr brahma prāṇam amṛtam prapadyate 'yam asau śarma varmābhayaṃ svastaye saha prajayā saha paśubhir ṇi sakṣaṇir dviṣas taradhyā ṛṇayā na īyase svāhā | [AB, 8, 11 1]
anu hi tvā sutaṃ soma madāmasi mahe sama bhuvo brahma prāṇam amṛtam prapadyate 'yam asau śarma varmābhayaṃ svastaye saha prajayā saha paśubhi ryarājye vājāṁ abhi pavamāna pra gāhase svāhā | [AB, 8, 11 2]
ajījano hi pavamāna sūryaṃ vidhāre śa svar brahma prāṇam amṛtam prapadyate 'yam asau śarma varmābhayaṃ svastaye saha prajayā saha paśubhiḥ kmanā payo gojīrayā raṃhamāṇaḥ puraṃdhyā svāheti | [AB, 8, 11 3]
anārto ha vā ariṣṭo 'jītaḥ sarvato guptas trayyai vidyāyai rūpeṇa sarvā diśo 'nusaṃcaraty aindre loke pratiṣṭhito yasmā etā ṛtvig antataḥ kaṃsena caturgṛhītās tisra ājyāhutīr aindrīḥ prapadaṃ juhoti | [AB, 8, 11 4]
athāntataḥ prajātim āśāste gavām aśvānām puruṣāṇām iha gāvaḥ prajāyadhvam ihāśvā iha pūruṣāḥ iho sahasradakṣiṇo vīras trātā niṣīdatv iti | [AB, 8, 11 5]
bahur ha vai prajayā paśubhir bhavati ya evam etām antataḥ prajātim āśāste gavām aśvānām puruṣāṇām | [AB, 8, 11 6]
eṣa ha vāva kṣatriyo 'vikṛṣṭo yam evaṃvido yājayanti | [AB, 8, 11 7]
atha ha taṃ vy eva karṣante yathā ha vā idaṃ niṣādā vā selagā vā pāpakṛto vā vittavantam puruṣam araṇye gṛhītvā kartam anvasya vittam ādāya dravanty evam eva ta ṛtvijo yajamānaṃ kartam anvasya vittam ādāya dravanti yam anevaṃvido yājayanti | [AB, 8, 11 8]
etaddha sma vai tad vidvān āha janamejayaḥ pārikṣita evaṃvidaṃ hi vai mām evaṃvido yājayanti tasmād aham jayāmy abhītvarīṃ senāṃ jayāmy abhītvaryā senayā na mā divyā na mānuṣya iṣava ṛcchanty eṣyāmi sarvam āyuḥ sarvabhūmir bhaviṣyāmīti | [AB, 8, 11 9]
na ha vā enaṃ divyā na mānuṣya iṣava ṛcchanty eti sarvam āyuḥ sarvabhūmir bhavati yam evaṃvido yājayanti yājayanti | [AB, 8, 11 10]
{AB, 8, 12}
athāta aindro mahābhiṣekaḥ | [AB, 8, 12 1]
te devā abruvan saprajāpatikā ayaṃ vai devānām ojiṣṭho baliṣṭhaḥ sahiṣṭhaḥ sattamaḥ pārayiṣṇutama imam evābhiṣiñcāmahā iti tatheti tad vai tad indram eva | [AB, 8, 12 2]
tasmā etām āsandīṃ samabharann ṛcaṃ nāma tasyai bṛhac ca rathaṃtaraṃ ca pūrvau pādāv akurvan vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cāparau śākvararaivate śīrṣaṇye naudhasaṃ ca kāleyaṃ cānūcye ṛcaḥ prācīnātānān sāmāni tiraścīnavāyān yajūṃṣy atīkāśān yaśa āstaraṇaṃ śriyam upabarhaṇaṃ tasyai savitā ca bṛhaspatiś ca pūrvau pādāv adhārayatāṃ vāyuś ca pūṣā cāparau mitrāvaruṇau śīrṣaṇye aśvināv anūcye sa etām āsandīm ārohat | [AB, 8, 12 3]
vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā trivṛtā stomena rathaṃtareṇa sāmnārohantu tān anv ārohāmi sāmrājyāya rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā pañcadaśena stomena bṛhatā sāmnārohantu tān anv ārohāmi bhaujyāyādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā saptadaśena stomena vairūpeṇa sāmnārohantu tān anv ārohāmi svārājyāya viśve tvā devā ānuṣṭubhena chandasaikaviṃśena stomena vairājena sāmnārohantu tān anv ārohāmi vairājyāya sādhyāś ca tvāptyāś ca devāḥ pāṅktena chandasā triṇavena stomena śākvareṇa sāmnārohantu tān anv ārohāmi rājyāya marutaś ca tvāṅgirasaś ca devā atichandasā chandasā trayastriṃśena stomena raivatena sāmnārohantu tān anv ārohāmi pārameṣṭhyāya māhārājyāyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyātiṣṭhāyārohāmīty etām āsandīm ārohat | [AB, 8, 12 4]
tam etasyām āsandyām āsīnaṃ viśve devā abruvan na vā anabhyutkruṣṭa indro vīryaṃ kartum arhaty abhy enam utkrośāmeti tatheti taṃ viśve devā abhyudakrośann imaṃ devā abhyutkrośata samrājaṃ sāmrājyam bhojam bhojapitaraṃ svarājaṃ svārājyaṃ virājaṃ vairājyaṃ rājānaṃ rājapitaram parameṣṭhinam pārameṣṭhyaṃ kṣatram ajani kṣatriyo 'jani viśvasya bhūtasyādhipatir ajani viśām attājani purām bhettājany asurāṇāṃ hantājani brahmaṇo goptājani dharmasya goptājanīti | [AB, 8, 12 5]
tam abhyutkruṣṭam prajāpatir abhiṣekṣyann etayarcābhyamantrayata | [AB, 8, 12 6]
{AB, 8, 13}
niṣasāda dhṛtavrato varuṇaḥ pastyāsv ā sāmrājyāya bhaujyāya svārājyāya vairājyāya pārameṣṭhyāya rājyāya māhārājyāyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyātiṣṭhāya sukratur iti | [AB, 8, 13 1]
tam etasyām āsandyām āsīnam prajāpatiḥ purastāt tiṣṭhan pratyaṅmukha audumbaryārdrayā śākhayā sapalāśayā jātarūpamayena ca pavitreṇāntardhāyābhyaṣiñcad imā āpaḥ śivatamā ity etena tṛcena devasya tveti ca yajuṣā bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity etābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ | [AB, 8, 13 2]
{AB, 8, 14}
athainam prācyāṃ diśi vasavo devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhyaṣiñcann etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ sāmrājyāya | [AB, 8, 14 1]
tasmād etasyām prācyāṃ diśi ye keca prācyānāṃ rājānaḥ sāmrājyāyaiva te 'bhiṣicyante samrāﾱ ity enān abhiṣiktān ācakṣata etām eva devānāṃ vihitim anu | [AB, 8, 14 2]
athainaṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi rudrā devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhyaṣiñcann etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhir bhaujyāya tasmād etasyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi ye keca satvatāṃ rājāno bhaujyāyaiva te 'bhiṣicyante bhojety enān abhiṣiktān ācakṣata etām eva devānāṃ vihitim anv athainam pratīcyāṃ diśy ādityā devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhyaṣiñcann etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ svārājyāya tasmād etasyām pratīcyāṃ diśi ye keca nīcyānāṃ rājāno ye 'pācyānāṃ svārājyāyaiva te 'bhiṣicyante svarāﾱ ity enān abhiṣiktān ācakṣata etām eva devānāṃ vihitim anv athainam udīcyāṃ diśi viśve devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhyaṣiñcann etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhir vairājyāya tasmād etasyām udīcyāṃ diśi ye keca pareṇa himavantaṃ janapadā uttarakurava uttaramadrā iti vairājyāyaiva te 'bhiṣicyante virāﾱ ity enān abhiṣiktān ācakṣata etām eva devānāṃ vihitim anv athainam asyāṃ dhruvāyām madhyamāyām pratiṣṭhāyāṃ diśi sādhyāś cāptyāś ca devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhyaṣiñcann etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhī rājyāya tasmād asyāṃ dhruvāyām madhyamāyām pratiṣṭhāyāṃ diśi ye keca kurupañcālānāṃ rājānaḥ savaśośīnarāṇāṃ rājyāyaiva te 'bhiṣicyante rājety enān abhiṣiktān ācakṣata etām eva devānāṃ vihitim anv athainam ūrdhvāyāṃ diśi marutaś cāṅgirasaś ca devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhyaṣiñcann etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ pārameṣṭhyāya māhārājyāyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyātiṣṭhāyeti sa parameṣṭhī prājāpatyo 'bhavat | [AB, 8, 14 3]
sa etena mahābhiṣekeṇābhiṣikta indraḥ sarvā jitīr ajayat sarvāṃllokān avindat sarveṣāṃ devānāṃ śraiṣṭhyam atiṣṭhām paramatām agacchat sāmrājyam bhaujyaṃ svārājyaṃ vairājyam pārameṣṭhyaṃ rājyam māhārājyam ādhipatyaṃ jitvāsmiṃlloke svayambhūḥ svarāﾱ amṛto 'muṣmin svarge loke sarvān kāmān āptvāmṛtaḥ samabhavat samabhavat | [AB, 8, 14 4]
{AB, 8, 15}
sa ya icched evaṃvit kṣatriyam ayaṃ sarvā jitīr jayetāyaṃ sarvāṃllokān vindetāyaṃ sarveṣāṃ rājñāṃ śraiṣṭhyam atiṣṭhām paramatāṃ gaccheta sāmrājyam bhaujyaṃ svārājyaṃ vairājyam pārameṣṭhyaṃ rājyam māhārājyam ādhipatyam ayaṃ samantaparyāyī syāt sārvabhaumaḥ sārvāyuṣa āntād ā parārdhāt pṛthivyai samudraparyantāyā ekarāﾱ iti taṃ etenaindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa kṣatriyaṃ śāpayitvā 'bhiṣiñcet | [AB, 8, 15 1]
yāṃ ca rātrīm ajāyathā yāṃ ca pretāsi tad ubhayam antareṇeṣṭāpūrtaṃ te lokaṃ sukṛtam āyuḥ prajāṃ vṛñjīya yadi me druhyer iti | [AB, 8, 15 2]
sa ya icched evaṃvit kṣatriyo 'haṃ sarvā jitīr jayeyam ahaṃ sarvāṃllokān vindeyam ahaṃ sarveṣāṃ rājñāṃ śraiṣṭhyam atiṣṭhām paramatāṃ gaccheyaṃ sāmrājyam bhaujyaṃ svārājyam vairājyam pārameṣṭhyaṃ rājyam māhārājyam ādhipatyam ahaṃ samantaparyāyī syāṃ sārvabhaumaḥ sārvāyuṣa āntād ā parārdhāt pṛthivyai samudraparyantāyā ekarāﾱ iti sa na vicikitset sa brūyāt saha śraddhayā yāṃ ca rātrīm ajāye 'haṃ yāṃ ca pretāsmi tad ubhayam antareṇeṣṭāpūrtam me lokaṃ sukṛtam āyuḥ prajāṃ vṛñjīthā yadi te druhyeyam iti | [AB, 8, 15 3]
{AB, 8, 16}
atha tato brūyāc catuṣṭayāni vānaspatyāni saṃbharata naiyagrodhāny audumbarāṇy āśvatthāni plākṣāṇīti | [AB, 8, 16 1]
kṣatraṃ vā etad vanaspatīnāṃ yan nyagrodho yan naiyagrodhāni saṃbharanti kṣatram evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti bhaujyaṃ vā etad vanaspatīnāṃ yad udumbaro yad audumbarāṇi saṃbharanti bhaujyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti sāmrājyaṃ vā etad vanaspatīnāṃ yad aśvattho yad āśvatthāni saṃbharanti sāmrājyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti svārājyaṃ ca ha vā etad vairājyaṃ ca vanaspatīnāṃ yat plakṣo yat plākṣāṇi saṃbharanti svārājyavairājye evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti | [AB, 8, 16 2]
atha tato brūyāc catuṣṭayāny auṣadhāni saṃbharata tokmakṛtāni vrīhīṇām mahāvrīhīṇām priyaṃgūnāṃ yavānām iti | [AB, 8, 16 3]
kṣatraṃ vā etad oṣadhīnāṃ yad vrīhayo yad vrīhīṇāṃ tokma saṃbharanti kṣatram evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti sāmrājyaṃ vā etad oṣadhīnāṃ yan mahāvrīhayo yan mahāvrīhīṇāṃ tokma saṃbharanti sāmrājyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti bhaujyaṃ vā etad oṣadhīnāṃ yat priyaṃgavo yat priyaṃgūnāṃ tokma saṃbharanti bhaujyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti sainānyaṃ vā etad oṣadhīnāṃ yad yavā yad yavānāṃ tokma saṃbharanti sainānyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti | [AB, 8, 16 4]
{AB, 8, 17}
athāsmā audumbarīm āsandīṃ saṃbharanti tasyā uktam brāhmaṇam audumbaraś camaso vā pātrī vodumbaraśākhā tān etān sambhārān saṃbhṛtyaudumbaryām pātryāṃ vā camase vā samāvapeyus teṣu samopteṣu dadhi madhu sarpir ātapavarṣyā āpo 'bhyānīya pratiṣṭhāpyaitām āsandīm abhimantrayeta | [AB, 8, 17 1]
bṛhac ca te rathaṃtaraṃ ca pūrvau pādau bhavatāṃ vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cāparau śākvararaivate śīrṣaṇye naudhasaṃ ca kāleyaṃ cānūcye ṛcaḥ prācīnātānāḥ sāmāni tiraścīnavāyā yajūṃṣy atīkāśā yaśa āstaraṇaṃ śrīr upabarhaṇaṃ savitā ca te bṛhaspatiś ca pūrvau pādau dhārayatāṃ vāyuś ca pūṣā cāparau mitrāvaruṇau śīrṣaṇye aśvināv anūcye iti | [AB, 8, 17 2]
athainaṃ etām āsandīm ārohayet | [AB, 8, 17 3]
vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā trivṛtā stomena rathaṃtareṇa sāmnārohantu tān anv āroha sāmrājyāya rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā pañcadaśena stomena bṛhatā sāmnārohantu tān anv āroha bhaujyāyādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā saptadaśena stomena vairūpeṇa sāmnārohantu tān anv āroha svārājyāya viśve tvā devā ānuṣṭubhena chandasaikaviṃśena stomena vairājena sāmnārohantu tān anv āroha vairājyāya marutaś ca tvāṅgirasaś ca devā atichandasā chandasā trayastriṃśena stomena raivatena sāmnārohantu tān anv āroha pārameṣṭhyāya sādhyāś ca tvāptyāś ca devāḥ pāṅktena chandasā triṇavena stomena śākvareṇa sāmnārohantu tān anv āroha rājyāya māhārājyāyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyātiṣṭhāyārohety etām āsandīm ārohayet | [AB, 8, 17 4]
tam etasyām āsandyām āsīnaṃ rājakartāro brūyur na vā anabhyutkruṣṭaḥ kṣatriyo vīryaṃ kartum arhaty abhy enam utkrośāmeti tatheti taṃ rājakartāro 'bhyutkrośantīmaṃ janā abhyutkrośata samrājaṃ sāmrājyam bhojam bhojapitaraṃ svarājaṃ svārājyaṃ virājaṃ vairājyam parameṣṭhinam pārameṣṭhyaṃ rājānāṃ rājapitaraṃ kṣatram ajani kṣatriyo 'jani viśvasya bhūtasyādhipatir ajani viśām attājany amitrāṇāṃ hantājani brāhmaṇānām goptājani dharmasya goptājanīti | [AB, 8, 17 5]
tam abhyutkruṣṭam evaṃvid abhiṣekṣyann etayarcābhimantrayeta | [AB, 8, 17 6]
{AB, 8, 18}
niṣasāda dhṛtavrato varuṇaḥ pastyāsv ā sāmrājyāya bhaujyāya svārājyāya vairājyāya pārameṣṭhyāya rājyāya māhārājyāyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyātiṣṭhāya sukratur iti tam etasyām āsandyām āsīnam evaṃvit purastāt tiṣṭhan pratyaṅmukha audumbaryārdrayā śākhayā sapalāśayā jātarūpamayena ca pavitreṇāntardhāyābhiṣiñcatīmā āpaḥ śivatamā ity etena tṛcena devasya tveti ca yajuṣā bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity etābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ | [AB, 8, 18 1]
{AB, 8, 19}
prācyāṃ tvā diśi vasavo devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhiṣiñcantv etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ sāmrājyāya dakṣiṇasyāṃ tvā diśi rudrā devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhiṣiñcantv etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhir bhaujyāya pratīcyāṃ tvā diśy ādityā devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhiṣiñcantv etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ svārājyāyodīcyāṃ tvā diśi viśve devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhiṣiñcantv etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhir vairājyāyordhvāyāṃ tvā diśi marutaś cāṅgirasaś ca devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caiva pañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhiṣiñcantv etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhiḥ pārameṣṭhyāyāsyāṃ tvā dhruvāyāṃ madhyamāyām pratiṣṭhāyāṃ diśi sādhyāś cāptyāś ca devāḥ ṣaḍbhiś caivapañcaviṃśair ahobhir abhiṣiñcantv etena ca tṛcenaitena ca yajuṣaitābhiś ca vyāhṛtibhī rājyāya māhārājyādhipatyāya svāvaśyāyādhiṣṭhāyeti sa parameṣṭhī prājāpatyo bhavati | [AB, 8, 19 1]
sa etenaindrena mahābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktaḥ kṣatriyaḥ sarvā jitīr jayati sarvāṃl lokān vindati sarveṣāṃ rājñāṃ śraiṣṭhyam atiṣṭhām paramatāṃ gacchati sāmrājyam bhaujyaṃ svārājyam pārameṣṭhyaṃ rājyam māhārājyam ādhipatyaṃ jitvāsmiṃlloke svayambhūḥ svarāﾱ amṛto 'muṣmin svarge loke sarvān kāmān āptvāmṛtaḥ sambhavati yam etenaindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa kṣatriyaṃ śāpayitvābhiṣiñcati | [AB, 8, 19 2]
{AB, 8, 20}
indriyaṃ vā etad asmiṃlloke yad dadhi yad dadhnābhiṣiñcatīndriyam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti raso vā eṣa oṣadhivanaspatiṣu yan madhu yan madhvābhiṣiñcati rasam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti tejo vā etat paśūnāṃ yad ghṛtaṃ yad ghṛtenābhiṣiñcati teja evāsmiṃs tad dadhāty amṛtaṃ vā etad asmiṃlloke yad āpo yad adbhir abhiṣiñcaty amṛtatvam evāsmiṃs tad dadhāti | [AB, 8, 20 1]
so 'bhiṣikto 'bhiṣektre brāhmaṇāya hiraṇyaṃ dadyāt sahasraṃ dadyāt kṣetraṃ catuṣpād dadyād athāpy āhur asaṃkhyātam evāparimitaṃ dadyād aparimito vai kṣatriyo 'parimitasyāvaruddhyā iti | [AB, 8, 20 2]
athāsmai surākaṃsaṃ hasta ādadhāti svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayā pavasva soma dhārayā indrāya pātave suta iti | [AB, 8, 20 3]
tām pibed yad atra śiṣṭaṃ rasinaḥ sutasya yad indro apibacchacībhiḥ idaṃ tad asya manasā śivena somaṃ rājānam iha bhakṣayāmi abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sute sutaṃ sṛjāmi pītaye tṛmpa vyaśnuhī madam iti | [AB, 8, 20 4]
yo ha vāva somapīthaḥ surāyām praviṣṭaḥ sa haiva tenaindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktasya kṣatriyasya bhakṣito bhavati na surā | [AB, 8, 20 5]
tām pītvābhimantrayetāpāma somaṃ śaṃ no bhaveti | [AB, 8, 20 6]
tad yathaivādaḥ priyaḥ putraḥ pitaram priyā vā jāyā patiṃ sukhaṃ śivam upaspṛśaty ā visrasa evaṃ haivaitenaindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇābhiṣiktasya kṣatriyasya surā vā somo vānyad vānnādyaṃ sukhaṃ śivam upaspṛśaty ā visrasaḥ | [AB, 8, 20 7]
{AB, 8, 21}
etena ha vā aindrena mahābhiṣekeṇa turaḥ kāvaṣeyo janamejayam pārikṣitam abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u janamejayaḥ pārikṣitaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 1]
tad eṣābhi yajñagāthā gīyate | [AB, 8, 21 2]
āsandīvati dhānyādaṃ rukmiṇaṃ haritasrajam aśvam babandha sāraṅgaṃ devebhyo janamejaya iti | [AB, 8, 21 3]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa cyavano bhārgavaḥ śāryātam mānavam abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u śāryāto mānavaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje devānāṃ hāpi satre gṛhapatir āsa | [AB, 8, 21 4]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa somaśuṣmā vājaratnāyanaḥ śatānīkaṃ sātrājitam abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u śatānīkaḥ sātrājitaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 5]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa parvatanāradāv āmbāṣṭhyam abhiṣiṣicatus tasmād v āmbāṣṭhyaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 6]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa parvatanāradau yudhāṃśrauṣṭim augrasainyam abhiṣiṣicatus tasmād u yudhāṃśrauṣṭir augrasainyaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 7]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa kaśyapo viśvakarmāṇam bhauvanam abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u viśvakarmā bhauvanaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 8]
bhūmir ha jagāv ity udāharanti | [AB, 8, 21 9]
na mā martyaḥ kaścana dātum arhati viśvakarman bhauvana māṃ didāsitha nimaṅkṣye 'haṃ salilasya madhye moghas ta eṣa kaśyapāyāsa saṃgara iti | [AB, 8, 21 10]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa vasiṣṭhaḥ sudāsam paijavanam abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u sudāḥ paijavanaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 11]
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa saṃvarta āṅgiraso maruttam avikṣitam abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u marutta āvikṣitaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 21 12]
tad apy eṣa śloko 'bhigītaḥ | [AB, 8, 21 13]
marutaḥ pariveṣṭāro maruttasyāvasan gṛhe āvikṣitasya kāmaprer viśve devāḥ sabhāsada iti | [AB, 8, 21 14]
{AB, 8, 22}
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇodamaya ātreyo 'ṅgam abhiṣiṣeca tasmādvaṅgaḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvena ca medhyeneje | [AB, 8, 22 1]
sa hovācālopāṅgo daśa nāgasahasrāṇi daśa dāsīsahasrāṇi dadāmi te brāhmaṇopa māsmin yajñe hvayasveti | [AB, 8, 22 2]
tad apy ete ślokā abhigītāḥ | [AB, 8, 22 3]
yābhir gobhir udamayam praiyamedhā ayājayan dve dve sahasre badvānām ātreyo madhyato 'dadāt | [AB, 8, 22 4]
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi śvetān vairocano hayān praṣṭīn niścṛtya prāyacchad yajamāne purohite | [AB, 8, 22 5]
deśād deśāt samoﾱhānāṃ sarvāsām āḍhyaduhitṝṇām daśādadāt sahasrāṇy ātreyo niṣkakaṇṭhyaḥ | [AB, 8, 22 6]
daśa nāgasahasrāṇi dattvātreyo 'vacatnuke śrāntaḥ pārikuṭān praipsad dānenāṅgasya brāhmaṇaḥ | [AB, 8, 22 7]
śataṃ tubhyaṃ śataṃ tubhyam iti smaiva pratāmyati sahasraṃ tubhyam ity uktvā prāṇān sma pratipadyata iti | [AB, 8, 22 8]
{AB, 8, 23}
etena ha vā aindreṇa mahābhiṣekeṇa dīrghatamā māmateyo bharataṃ dauḥṣantim abhiṣiṣeca tasmād u bharato dauḥṣantiḥ samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāyāśvair u ca medhyair īje | [AB, 8, 23 1]
tad apy ete ślokā abhigītāḥ | [AB, 8, 23 2]
hiraṇyena parīvṛtān kṛṣṇāñchukladato mṛgān | [AB, 8, 23 3.1]
maṣṇāre bharato 'dadācchatam badvāni sapta ca | [AB, 8, 23 3.2]
bharatasyaiṣa dauḥṣanter agniḥ sācīguṇe citaḥ | [AB, 8, 23 4.1]
yasmin sahasram brāhmaṇā badvaśo gā vibhejire | [AB, 8, 23 4.2]
aṣṭāsaptatim bharato dauḥṣantir yamunām anu | [AB, 8, 23 5.1]
gaṅgāyāṃ vṛtraghne 'badhnāt pañcapañcāśataṃ hayān | [AB, 8, 23 5.2]
trayastriṃśacchataṃ rājāśvān baddhvāya medhyān | [AB, 8, 23 6.1]
dauḥṣantir atyagād rājño 'māyān māyavattaraḥ | [AB, 8, 23 6.2]
mahākarma bharatasya na pūrve nāpare janāḥ | [AB, 8, 23 7.1]
divam martya iva hastābhyāṃ nodāpuḥ pañca mānavā iti | [AB, 8, 23 7.2]
etaṃ ha vā aindram mahābhiṣekam bṛhaduktha ṛṣir durmukhāya pāñcālāya provāca tasmād u durmukhaḥ pāñcālo rājā san vidyayā samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāya | [AB, 8, 23 8]
etaṃ ha vā aindram mahābhiṣekaṃ vāsiṣṭhaḥ sātyahavyo 'tyarātaye jānaṃtapaye provāca tasmād v atyarātir jānaṃtapir arājā san vidyayā samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīṃ jayan parīyāya | [AB, 8, 23 9]
sa hovāca vāsiṣṭhaḥ sātyahavyo 'jaiṣīr vai samantaṃ sarvataḥ pṛthivīm mahan mā gamayeti sa hovācātyarātir jānaṃtapir yadā brāhmaṇottarakurūñ jayeyam atha tvam u haiva pṛthivyai rājā syāḥ senāpatir eva te 'haṃ syām iti sa hovāca vāsiṣṭhaḥ sātyahavyo devakṣetraṃ vai tan na vai tan martyo jetum arhaty adrukṣo vai ma āta idaṃ dada iti tato hātyarātiṃ jānaṃtapim āttavīryaṃ niḥśukram amitratapanaḥ śuṣmiṇaḥ śaibyo rājā jaghāna | [AB, 8, 23 10]
tasmād evaṃ viduṣe brāhmaṇāyaivaṃ cakruṣe na kṣatriyo druhyen ned rāṣṭrād avapadyeya ned vā mā prāṇo jahad iti jahad iti | [AB, 8, 23 11]
{AB, 8, 24}
athātaḥ purodhāyā eva | [AB, 8, 24 1]
na ha vai a purohitasya rājñaḥ devāḥ annam adanti | [AB, 8, 24 638604_1]
tasmāt rājā yakṣyamāṇaḥ brāhmaṇam purodadhīta devāḥ me annam adan iti | [AB, 8, 24 638604_2]
agnīn vā eṣa svargyān rājoddharate yat purohitam | [AB, 8, 24 3]
tasya purohita evāhavanīyo bhavati jāyā gārhapatyaḥ putro 'nvāhāryapacanaḥ sa yat purohitāya karoty āhavanīya eva taj juhoty atha yaj jāyāyai karoti gārhapatya eva taj juhoty atha yat putrāya karoty anvāhāryapacana eva taj juhoti ta enaṃ śāntatanavo 'bhihutā abhiprītāḥ svargaṃ lokam abhivahanti kṣatraṃ ca balaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca viśaṃ ca | [AB, 8, 24 4]
ta evainam aśāntatanavo 'nabhihutā anabhiprītāḥ svargāl lokān nudante kṣatrāc ca balāc ca rāṣṭrāc ca viśaś ca | [AB, 8, 24 5]
agnir vā eṣa vaiśvānaraḥ pañcamenir yat purohitas tasya vācy evaikā menir bhavati pādayor ekā tvacy ekā hṛdaya ekopastha ekā tābhir jvalantībhir dīpyamānābhir upodeti rājānaṃ sa yad āha kva bhagavo 'vātsīs tṛṇāny asmā āharateti tenāsya tāṃ śamayati yāsya vāci menir bhavaty atha yad asmā udakam ānayanti pādyaṃ tenāsya tāṃ śamayati yāsya pādayor menir bhavaty atha yad enam alaṃkurvanti tenāsya tāṃ śamayati yāsya tvaci menir bhavaty atha yad enaṃ tarpayanti tenāsya tāṃ śamayati yāsya hṛdaye menir bhavaty atha yad asyānāruddho veśmasu vasati tenāsya tāṃ śamayati yāsyopasthe menir bhavati | [AB, 8, 24 6]
sa enaṃ śāntatanur abhihuto 'bhiprītaḥ svargaṃ lokam abhivahati kṣatraṃ ca balaṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca viśaṃ ca sa evainam aśāntatanur anabhihuto 'nabhiprītaḥ svargāllokān nudate kṣatrāc ca balāc ca rāṣṭrāc ca viśaś ca | [AB, 8, 24 7]
{AB, 8, 25}
agnir vā eṣa vaiśvānaraḥ pañcamenir yat purohitas tābhī rājānam parigṛhya tiṣṭhati samudra iva bhūmim | [AB, 8, 25 1]
ayuvamāry asya rāṣṭram bhavati nainam purāyuṣaḥ prāṇo jahāty ā jarasaṃ jīvati sarvam āyur eti na punar mriyate yasyaivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇo rāṣṭragopaḥ purohitaḥ | [AB, 8, 25 2]
kṣatreṇa kṣatraṃ jayati balena balam aśnute yasyaivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇo rāṣṭragopaḥ purohitaḥ | [AB, 8, 25 3]
tasmai viśaḥ saṃjānate sammukhā ekamanaso yasyaivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇo rāṣṭragopaḥ purohitaḥ | [AB, 8, 25 4]
{AB, 8, 26}
tad apy etad ṛṣiṇoktam | [AB, 8, 26 1]
sa id rājā pratijanyāni viśvā śuṣmeṇa tasthāv abhi vīryeṇeti | [AB, 8, 26 2]
sapatnā vai dviṣanto bhrātṛvyā janyāni tān eva tac chuṣmeṇa vīryeṇādhitiṣṭhati | [AB, 8, 26 3]
bṛhaspatiṃ yaḥ subhṛtam bibhartīti bṛhaspatir ha vai devānām purohitas tam anv anye manuṣyarājñām purohitā bṛhaspatiṃ yaḥ subhṛtam bibhartīti yad āha purohitaṃ yaḥ subhṛtaṃ bibhartīty eva tad āha | [AB, 8, 26 4]
valgūyati vandate pūrvabhājam ity apacitim evāsmā etad āha | [AB, 8, 26 5]
sa it kṣeti sudhita okasi sva iti gṛhā vā okaḥ sveṣv eva tad gṛheṣu suhito vasati | [AB, 8, 26 6]
tasmā iﾱā pinvate viśvadānīm ity annaṃ vā iﾱānnam evāsmā etad ūrjasvac chaśvad bhavati | [AB, 8, 26 7]
tasmai viśaḥ svayam evā namanta iti rāṣṭrāṇi vai viśo rāṣṭrāṇy evainaṃ tat svayam upanamanti | [AB, 8, 26 8]
yasmin brahmā rājani pūrva etīti purohitam evaitad āha | [AB, 8, 26 9]
apratīto jayati saṃ dhanānīti rāṣṭrāṇi vai dhanāni tāny apratīto jayati | [AB, 8, 26 10]
pratijanyāny uta yā sajanyeti sapatnā vai dviṣanto bhrātṛvyā janyāni tān apratīto jayati | [AB, 8, 26 11]
avasyave yo varivaḥ kṛṇotīti yad āhāvasīyase yo vasīyaḥ karotīty eva tad āha | [AB, 8, 26 12]
brahmaṇe rājā tam avanti devā iti purohitam evaitad abhivadati | [AB, 8, 26 13]
{AB, 8, 27}
yo ha vai trīn purohitāṃs trīn purodhātṝn veda sa brāhmaṇaḥ purohitaḥ sa vadeta purodhāyā agnir vāva purohitaḥ pṛthivī purodhātā vāyur vāva purohito 'ntarikṣam purodhātādityo vāva purohito dyauḥ purodhātaiṣa ha vai purohito ya evaṃ vedātha sa tirohito ya evaṃ na veda | [AB, 8, 27 1]
tasya rājā mitram bhavati dviṣantam apabādhate yasyaivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇo rāṣṭragopaḥ purohitaḥ | [AB, 8, 27 2]
kṣatreṇa kṣatraṃ jayati balena balam aśnute yasyaivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇo rāṣṭragopaḥ purohitas tasmai viśaḥ saṃjānate sammukhā ekamanaso yasyaivaṃ vidvān brāhmaṇo rāṣṭragopaḥ purohitaḥ | [AB, 8, 27 3]
bhūr bhuvaḥ svar om amo 'ham asmi sa tvaṃ sa tvaṃ asy amo 'haṃ dyaur aham pṛthivī tvaṃ sāmāham ṛk tvaṃ tāv eha saṃvahāvahai purāṇyasmāt mahābhayāt tanūr asi tanvam me pāhi | [AB, 8, 27 4]
yā oṣadhīḥ somarājñīr bahvīḥ śatavicakṣaṇāḥ | [AB, 8, 27 5.1]
tā mahyam asminn āsane 'chidraṃ śarma yacchata | [AB, 8, 27 5.2]
yā oṣadhīḥ somarājñīr viṣṭhitāḥ pṛthivīm anu | [AB, 8, 27 6.1]
tā mahyam asminn āsane 'chidraṃ śarma yacchata | [AB, 8, 27 6.2]
asmin rāṣṭre śriyam āveśayāmy ato devīḥ pratipaśyāmy āpaḥ | [AB, 8, 27 7]
dakṣiṇam pādam avanenije 'smin rāṣṭra indriyaṃ dadhāmi | [AB, 8, 27 8.1]
savyam pādam avanenije 'smin rāṣṭra indriyaṃ vardhayāmi | [AB, 8, 27 8.2]
pūrvam anyam aparam anyam pādāv avanenije | [AB, 8, 27 8.3]
devā rāṣṭrasya guptyā abhayasyāvaruddhyai | [AB, 8, 27 8.4]
āpaḥ pādāvanejanīr dviṣantaṃ nirdahantu me | [AB, 8, 27 9]
{AB, 8, 28}
athāto brahmanaḥ parimaro yo ha vai brahmaṇaḥ parimaraṃ veda pary enaṃ dviṣanto bhrātṛvyāḥ pari sapatnā mriyante | [AB, 8, 28 1]
ayaṃ vai brahma yo 'yam pavate tam etāḥ pañca devatāḥ parimriyante vidyud vṛṣṭiś candramā ādityo 'gniḥ | [AB, 8, 28 2]
vidyud vai vidyutya vṛṣṭim anupraviśati sāntardhīyate tāṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 3]
yadā vai mriyate 'thāntardhīyate 'thaināṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 4]
sa brūyād vidyuto maraṇe dviṣan me mriyatāṃ so 'ntardhīyatāṃ tam mā nirjñāsiṣur iti | [AB, 8, 28 5]
kṣipraṃ haivainaṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 6]
vṛṣṭir vai vṛṣṭvā candramasam anupraviśati sāntardhīyate tāṃ na nirjānanti yadā vai mriyate 'thāntardhīyate 'thainaṃ na nirjānanti sa brūyād vṛṣṭer maraṇe dviṣan me mriyatāṃ so 'ntardhīyatāṃ tam mā nirjñāsiṣur iti kṣipraṃ haivainaṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 7]
candramā vā amāvāsyāyām ādityam anupraviśati so'ntardhīyatāṃ taṃ na nirjānanti yadā vai mriyate 'thāntardhīyate 'thainaṃ na nirjānanti sa brūyāc candramaso maraṇe dviṣan me mriyatāṃ so 'ntardhīyatāṃ tam mā nirjñāsiṣur iti kṣipraṃ haivainaṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 8]
ādityo vā astaṃ yann agnim anupraviśati so 'ntardhīyate taṃ na nirjānanti yadā vai mriyate 'thāntardhīyate 'thainam na nirjānanti sa brūyād ādityasya maraṇe dviṣan me mriyatāṃ so 'ntardhīyatāṃ tam mā nirjñāsiṣur iti kṣipraṃ haivainaṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 9]
agnir vā udvān vāyum anupraviśati so 'ntardhīyate taṃ na nirjānanti yadā vai mriyate 'thāntardhīyate 'thainaṃ na nirjānanti sa brūyād agner maraṇe dviṣan me mriyatāṃ so 'ntardhīyatāṃ tam mā nirjñāsiṣur iti kṣipraṃ haivainaṃ na nirjānanti | [AB, 8, 28 10]
tā vā etā devatā ata eva punar jāyante | [AB, 8, 28 11]
vāyor agnir jāyate prāṇāddhi balān mathyamāno 'dhijāyate taṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyād agnir jāyatām mā me dviṣañ jany ata eva parāṅ prajighyatv iti ato haiva parāṅ prajighyati | [AB, 8, 28 12]
agner vā ādityo jāyate taṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyād ādityo jāyatām mā me dviṣañ jany ata eva parāṅ prajighyatv ity ato haiva parāṅ prajighyati | [AB, 8, 28 13]
ādityād vai candramā jāyate taṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyāc candramā jāyatām mā me dviṣañ jany ata eva parāṅ prajighyatv iti ato haiva parāṅ prajighyati | [AB, 8, 28 14]
candramaso vai vṛṣṭir jāyate tāṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyād vṛṣṭir jāyatām mā me dviṣañ jany ata eva parāṅ prajighyatv ity ato haiva parāṅ prajighyati | [AB, 8, 28 15]
vṛṣṭer vai vidyuj jāyate tāṃ dṛṣṭvā brūyād vidyuj jāyatām mā me dviṣañ jany ata eva parāṅ prajighyatv ity ato haiva parāṅ prajighyati | [AB, 8, 28 16]
sa eṣa brahmaṇaḥ parimaraḥ | [AB, 8, 28 17]
tam etam brahmaṇaḥ parimaram maitreyaḥ kauṣāravaḥ sutvane kairiśaye bhārgāyaṇāya rājñe provāca taṃ ha pañca rājānaḥ parimamrus tataḥ sutvā mahajjagāma | [AB, 8, 28 18]
tasya vrataṃ na dviṣataḥ pūrva upaviśed yadi tiṣṭhantam manyeta tiṣṭhetaiva na dviṣataḥ pūrvaḥ saṃviśed yady āsīnam manyetāsītaiva na dviṣataḥ pūrvaḥ prasvapyād yadi jāgratam manyeta jāgṛyād eva | [AB, 8, 28 19]
api ha yady asyāśmamūrdhā dviṣan bhavati kṣipraṃ haivainaṃ stṛṇute stṛṇute | [AB, 8, 28 20]
